# Government Solutions | Verkada Help

**Overview** Verkada Government Solutions is a cloud-managed security platform designed to meet the needs of federal, state, and local agencies. It provides centralized management of cameras, access control, alarms, sensors, and intercoms while ensuring compliance with government security standards, including FIPS 140-2 and TAA. The platform supports secure cloud hosting, SSO, and third-party provisioning to help agencies manage users and maintain consistent access policies.

This collection provides detailed guidance on deploying devices, configuring settings, monitoring activity, and maintaining secure, compliant operations in government environments.

Check out these links to get started:

[Get Started with Government Solutions](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/get-started-with-government-solutions)

[Why Government Solutions/FIPS Devices?](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/why-government-solutionsfips-devices)

[Required Camera Network Settings - Government Solutions](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-camera-network-settings-government-solutions)

# Air Quality Sensors | Air Quality | Verkada Help

**Overview** Verkada Air Quality Sensors are cloud-managed devices that let you monitor air quality and environmental conditions across your facilities from a single interface. They measure CO₂, temperature, humidity, particulate matter (PM), VOCs, and other indicators, providing real-time insights to help maintain a healthy and safe environment.

This collection provides detailed guidance on installing and configuring sensors, monitoring readings, setting up alerts, and maintaining reliable operation. It helps you set up sensors efficiently and keep your environmental monitoring accurate and dependable.

Check out these links to get started:

[Get Started with Verkada Air Quality Sensors](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/get-started-with-verkada-air-quality-sensors)

[Quick Reference Guide for Verkada Air Quality Sensors](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/quick-reference-guide-for-verkada-air-quality-sensors)

[Air Quality Sensor Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/air-quality-sensor-network-settings)

# Security Trailer | Verkada Help

**Overview** The Verkada Security Trailer is a solar-powered, cloud-managed mobile security platform that brings enterprise-grade surveillance to sites without existing infrastructure. It can be deployed to parking lots, construction sites, events, remote areas, or any location where wired power or network connection is unavailable.

The trailer supports up to six cameras (or other Verkada devices), includes a built-in PoE switch, and provides power and network via solar panels and an Verkada gateway.

This collection provides guidance on selecting the right trailer configuration, installing and commissioning the trailer, adding devices, and managing the setup through Verkada Command.

Last updated 1 day ago

Was this helpful?

# Connectivity | Verkada Help

**Overview** Verkada Connectivity uses gateways to provide network and power to Verkada devices in locations where traditional wiring is difficult. Gateways support cellular or WiFi connections and can deliver PoE to connected devices, which makes it possible to place cameras and other Verkada hardware in remote or outdoor areas.

This collection provides guidance on choosing a gateway, installing it, configuring connectivity, and maintaining reliable operation. It helps you extend your Verkada deployment to sites that need flexible power and network options.

Check out these links to get started:

[Get Started with the Cellular Gateway](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/get-started-with-the-cellular-gateway)

[Roles and Permissions for Gateway](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/roles-and-permissions-for-gateway)

[Gateways Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/gateways-network-settings)

# Viewing Station | Verkada Help

The Verkada Viewing Station is a plug-and-play device that streams live video feeds from your Verkada cameras to a display. It lets you monitor multiple camera feeds at once with low latency and smooth playback.

This collection walks you through how to set up, claim, and configure a Viewing Station in your organization. You can use your Viewing Station to bring real-time visibility across sites. This is ideal for control rooms, security desks, or anywhere you need a stable, always-on video wall. It supports multiple camera streams, flexible layout configuration, and integrates with other Verkada systems for unified monitoring.

# Command Connector | Verkada Help

**Overview** Command Connector lets you integrate non-Verkada cameras into the cloud-based Verkada Command platform, giving you a unified management interface. It provides a cost-effective way to migrate to cloud-based video security while preserving current investments in hardware.

This collection guides you through how to add a Command Connector, connect compatible non-Verkada cameras (ONVIF-Profile S), and bring them under Command for centralized viewing and management. Command Connector supports core platform features such as live video monitoring, video retention, and basic analytics such as people and vehicle search.

Check out these links to get started:

[Get started with Command Connector](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/get-started-with-command-connector)

[Command Connector Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/command-connector-network-settings)

[Prepare for a Command Connector Deployment](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/hardware-installation/prepare-for-a-command-connector-deployment)

# Mailroom | Verkada Help

**Overview** Verkada Mailroom is a cloud-managed mail and package management solution that helps organizations track deliveries, notify recipients, and manage inventory from a single interface. The mobile app scans shipping labels and automatically captures recipient names, carriers, tracking numbers, and other key details.

After a package is scanned, Mailroom sends notifications by email, SMS, Slack, or Microsoft Teams. When paired with security cameras, Mailroom links scans and pickups to video so you can see when items arrive and when they are collected. This adds clear context and helps prevent lost or misplaced packages.

This collection explains how to configure Mailroom sites in Command, add employees, set up pickup locations, enable notifications, and use context cameras.

Check out these links to get started:

[Roles and Permissions for Mailroom](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/roles-and-permissions-for-mailroom)

[Mailroom Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/mailroom-network-settings)

[Customize Your Mailroom Dashboard](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/configuration-and-setup/customize-your-mailroom-dashboard)

Last updated 1 day ago

Was this helpful?

# Incident Response | Verkada Help

**Overview** Verkada Incident Response helps organizations track the well-being and location of people during an emergency or incident. It allows you to account for employees, visitors, or students quickly and can be used to reunify students with their guardians in school settings.

This collection explains how to set up Incident Response in Verkada Command, including importing sites, managing personnel lists, and building Response Templates that define who must be accounted for, which statuses can be used, and how locations are tracked.

[Incident Response Portal](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/incident-response-portal)

[Create Response Templates](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-response-templates)

# Access Control | Verkada Help

**Overview** Verkada Access Control is a cloud-managed door security system that gives you centralized control over who can enter your buildings. The platform combines door controllers, readers, and credential management with a single interface in Command. You can manage users, monitor door activity, and review access events from any location without relying on local servers or fragmented hardware systems.

This collection covers how to install and wire door controllers and readers, configure access permissions, manage credentials, review activity logs, and respond to access-related events. It also explains how Access Control works alongside other Verkada products so you can create a unified approach to building security.

# Intercom | Verkada Help

**Overview** Verkada Intercom is a cloud-managed video and audio entry system that lets you manage building access from a single interface. It combines live video, two-way audio, and door control so you can see visitors, communicate with them, and grant access securely. The platform integrates with cameras, access control, and other Verkada products, providing a unified approach to building security.

# Command | Verkada Help

**Overview** Verkada Command is a cloud-based platform that lets you manage all Verkada products from a single, secure interface. You can monitor devices and system health, adjust settings, review events, and manage users across all sites in your organization. Command supports SSO and third-party provisioning to centralize authentication and automate user management through your identity provider. The platform unifies cameras, access control, alarms, sensors, intercom, and other products in one place to keep your security operations efficient and organized.

This collection guides you through using Command to manage your organization and sites, configure user roles and permissions, monitor device health, track activity across all products, and leverage tools that simplify day-to-day security operations.

Check out these links to get started:

[Get Started with Verkada Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)

[Quick Reference Guide for Verkada Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/quick-reference-guide-for-verkada-command)

[Required Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings)

# Video Security | Verkada Cameras | Verkada Help

**Overview** Verkada Video Security is a cloud-managed camera platform that brings together reliable onboard storage, secure remote access, and centralized administration in Command. The system records and stores video on each device, uploads metadata to the cloud for quick search, and gives you a single interface to view footage, manage settings, and monitor health across all sites.

With Verkada, you can deploy cameras on standard PoE networks, manage them without local servers or NVRs, and apply consistent configurations at scale. The platform includes tools for live monitoring, historical video review, people and vehicle analytics, alerts, sharing, and retention management. It also provides built-in security features like automatic firmware updates, encrypted data handling, and role-based user management.

This collection helps you understand how the system works, how to install and configure devices, and how to maintain a reliable video security environment across your organization.

Check out these links to get started:

[Get Started with Verkada Security Cameras](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/get-started-with-verkada-security-cameras)

[Quick Reference Guide for Verkada Cameras](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/quick-reference-guide-for-verkada-cameras)

[Camera Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/camera-specifications/camera-network-settings)

* * *

You can also check out this video and others on our [video training center.](https://www.youtube.com/@Verkada)

# Contact Verkada Support - Government Solutions | Government Solutions | Verkada Help

Verkada offers dedicated assistance to government customers who need support from representatives in the United States to ensure fast and secure service. Our US-based team is equipped to handle inquiries related to deployment, troubleshooting, or general product guidance. To get in touch, log in to your [Government Solutions Command Account](https://command.verkadagov.com/admin/support)
 to open a case.

See [Contact Verkada Support](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support)
 for the support contact information of non-Government Solutions organizations.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/contact-verkada-support-government-solutions#contact-verkada-support)

Contact Verkada Support


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before you contact Verkada Support, it is best to have a support token ready. See [Enable Support Access](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/enable-support-access)
 for more information on creating a support token.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/contact-verkada-support-government-solutions#command-navigation)

Command navigation

1

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/contact-verkada-support-government-solutions#log-in-to-verkada-command)

Log in to Verkada [Command](https://command.verkadagov.com/)
.

2

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/contact-verkada-support-government-solutions#at-the-bottom-left-click-greater-than-contact-us)

At the bottom left, click **\>** **Contact Us**.

3

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/contact-verkada-support-government-solutions#connect-with-verkada-support-via-live-chat-email-or-phone)

# Get Started with Government Solutions | Government Solutions | Verkada Help

1

**Send an email to** [**\[email protected\]**](https://help.verkada.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#74131b0211061a19111a00340211061f1510155a171b19)
 **with the following information:**

*   Reason for GovCloud organization (e.g., FedRAMP, CJIS, CMMC, NCIC)\*
    
*   Name of the organization
    
*   Name of the first user to be invited
    
*   Email of the first user to be invited
    

2

**Verkada reviews the request according to our policy and responds within 48 hours. You will receive an email invitation to join the provisioned organization if approved.**

3

**From the invitation email, click Accept Invite.**

4

**On the invite page:**

a. Enter your name. b. Set a password. c. Click **Submit.**

5

**A warning notice will appear. After reading, if you wish to proceed, click Acknowledge.**

6

**(Optional) Select one of the options to enable 2FA.**

7

**You can now access your Government Solutions Command organization.**

\*Contact your Sales Representative for more information about Verkada’s compliance offerings.

# Why Government Solutions/FIPS Devices? | Government Solutions | Verkada Help

U.S. government customers can have their [Verkada Command](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/get-started-with-government-solutions)
 organization hosted in an isolated AWS region designed to host sensitive data and regulated workloads for those organizations that must adhere to strict government security and compliance requirements.

For added compliance and data protection, government customers can choose to host their Verkada Command organization in an isolated AWS region built to support sensitive data and regulated workloads. These solutions are ideal for a wide range of government entities to enable them to meet strict security requirements while leveraging modern, cloud-based physical security tools.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/why-government-solutionsfips-devices#fips)

FIPS

Verkada FIPS-validated devices meet the U.S. Federal Information Processing Standard [(FIPS) 140-2 encryption standard](https://csrc.nist.gov/pubs/fips/140-2/upd2/final)
, as validated by the National Institute of Standards and Technology (NIST). The FIPS 140 government standard specifies the minimum security requirements for cryptographic modules in information technology products.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/why-government-solutionsfips-devices#supported-organizations)

Supported organizations

*   Any combination of federal, state, or local government entities
    
*   Tribal government organizations
    
*   Research institutions
    
*   Federal contractors
    
*   Government contractors
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/why-government-solutionsfips-devices#supported-product-lines)

Supported product lines


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada is actively working to bring all product lines into the Government Solutions platform to support organizations with stringent compliance and security requirements. The goal is to provide a unified, secure experience across Verkada’s ecosystem while ensuring compatibility with the standards of AWS GovCloud and FIPS 140 encryption.

Below are the product lines that are currently supported on the Government Solutions platform:

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/why-government-solutionsfips-devices#verkada-command)

Verkada Command

Government customers in the United States can choose to use Verkada Command hosted in an isolated AWS region, which gives them the flexibility to use our secure cloud solutions on top of the additional stringent security controls provided by AWS GovCloud. Government Solutions Command organizations support our FIPS-validated camera models, FIPS-validated SV25 Air Quality Sensor, and Verkada Guest.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/why-government-solutionsfips-devices#video-security)

Video Security

Verkada’s FIPS-validated cameras incorporate encryption that meets the FIPS 140 and FedRAMP Moderate standards. They have durable, vandal-resistant designs, advanced computer vision features, and are TAA and FY 2019 NDAA compliant.

**Product**

**Models**

Domes

CD43-F / CD43-E-F / CD53-F / CD53-E-F / CD63-F / CD63-E-F / CD42-F / CD42-E-F / CD52-F / CD52-E-F

Bullets

CB52-E-F / CB52-TE-F / CB62-E-F / CB62-TE-F

Multisensors

CH52-E-F

PTZ

CP52-E-F / CP63-E-F

Fisheye

CF83-F

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/why-government-solutionsfips-devices#air-quality-sensors)

Air Quality Sensors

Verkada Air Quality Sensors help organizations monitor indoor environments for pollutants, unwanted behaviors, and optimal conditions at scale. Sensors integrate with Verkada cameras to provide visual context, including synced footage and People Analytics. Ideal for sensitive areas like bathrooms and locker rooms, they enable privacy-conscious detection of behaviors such as vaping or bullying. U.S. government customers can use Verkada Sensors to meet strict data and compliance requirements.

**Product**

**Models**

Air Quality Sensors

SV25-HW-F

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/why-government-solutionsfips-devices#command-connector)

Command Connector

Verkada’s Command Connector is a FIPS 140 validated solution designed to bridge third-party ONVIF cameras to Verkada Command. It supports encryption standards required for FedRAMP Moderate deployments and enables organizations to view non-Verkada cameras through a single, secure platform.

**Product**

**Models**

Command Connector

CC700-16TB-HW-F

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/why-government-solutionsfips-devices#connectivity)

Connectivity

Verkada Cellular Gateways make it easy to deploy video security in remote or hard-to-wire locations. By connecting to cellular networks and providing Power-over-Ethernet (PoE) to Verkada cameras and other devices, they enable plug-and-play installation without the need for traditional infrastructure.

Ideal for sites like construction zones, parking lots, and temporary facilities, Cellular Gateways help ensure reliable connectivity wherever it’s needed. U.S. government customers can rely on this solution to support Verkada’s FIPS-validated cameras in compliance-driven environments.

**Product**

**Models**

Indoor Cellular Gateway

GC31-HW

Outdoor Cellular Gateway

GC31-E-HW

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/why-government-solutionsfips-devices#access)

**Access**

Verkada Access Control offers a secure, scalable solution for managing physical access to government facilities. Integrated with Verkada Command, it provides unified visibility and management of doors and cameras through a single cloud-based platform. Administrators can configure permissions, monitor door activity in real time, and respond to security events remotely.

The system supports role-based access control, automated door schedules, and video-based event verification. U.S. government customers can deploy Verkada’s FIPS-validated hardware within the government hosting environment.

Verkada is actively pursuing an APL listing for FICAM compliance, but does not yet meet the full scope of FIPS 201.3.

**Product**

**Models**

Single Door PoE Controller

AC12-G-HW

16 Door Access Controller

AC62-G-HW

Contactless Badge Reader

AD34-G-HW

Pinpad Contactless Badge Reader

AD64-G-HW

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/why-government-solutionsfips-devices#guest)

Guest

Verkada Guest is a visitor management system that enhances building security while offering a seamless check-in experience with features like touchless entry, document signing, and host notifications. Built on the Verkada Command platform, it integrates with FIPS-validated cameras to monitor visitor activity. U.S. government customers can use Verkada Guest to add compliance and data security.

**Product**

**Models**

Apple 10.2 inch iPad

ACCX-TBL-1

Apple 10.9 inch iPad

ACCX-TBL-2

Guest in Government Solutions does not support:

*   [Security Screens](https://help.verkada.com/guest/configuration-and-setup/security-screening-settings)
    
*   Access control door integration
    
*   The ability to send visitor invitations through a calendar integration
    

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/why-government-solutionsfips-devices#viewing-station)

Viewing station

The Viewing Station is identical to our commercial offering. As an Apple device, it uses Apple-managed FIPS certificates. While Verkada does not manage these certificates, we ensure the device runs the latest iOS. Apple [states](https://support.apple.com/en-au/guide/certifications/apc3fa917cb49/web)
 the device uses FIPS-compliant encryption.

**Product**

**Models**

Viewing Station

VX52-HW

# Air Quality Sensor Network Settings | Air Quality | Verkada Help

This article outlines the required network settings that your Verkada [Air Quality Sensors](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
 ("sensors") need to communicate with [Verkada Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
. For more information on the required network settings for other Verkada product lines see [Required Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings)
.

Verkada devices are incompatible with LANs that require proxy servers or Secure Socket Layer (SSL)/Transport Layer Security (TLS) inspection. If either is in use, a bypass for all Verkada devices must be implemented for Verkada devices to communicate with Verkada Command.

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/air-quality-sensor-network-settings#status-led)

Status LED


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A flashing white or flashing blue [status LED](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-status-led)
 on the front of the sensor indicates the sensor is not communicating with Verkada Command. If you see this behavior, check that the network is set up correctly with the sensor’s requirements. If the problem persists, contact [Verkada Support](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support)
.

When sensors are offline, alerts/events do not trigger. They continue to record measurements and sync with Command once they reconnect.

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/air-quality-sensor-network-settings#ip-address)

IP address


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada Air Quality Sensors must be assigned an IPv4 address to communicate on the LAN and to Verkada Command. Verkada sensors use Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP) and User Datagram Protocol (UDP) to obtain their IP addresses and network configurations.

If you want to have a specific IP address on your sensor device, you can:

*   Set up a [static IP address through Command](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/configure-static-ip-addresses-for-air-quality-sensors-sv20-series-only)
     for SV20 series sensors (SV21, SV23, SV25)
    
*   Set a DHCP reservation using the device’s Media Access Control (MAC) address (found on the device’s label or in Command).
    

To configure a static IP address on a sensor device, the device must initially connect to Command and update to the latest firmware using DHCP. Once the update process is complete, it will have the ability to receive the new static IP configuration.

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/air-quality-sensor-network-settings#domain-name-system)

Domain Name System


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sensors use the DNS server to resolve Verkada’s fully qualified domain names (FQDN) to IP addresses to communicate with them. Your DHCP server tells the sensor where the DNS server is on the network and the sensor communicates using UDP port 53.

DNS over HTTPS (DoH) is currently not supported.

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/air-quality-sensor-network-settings#power)

Power


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sensors are powered through Power over Ethernet (PoE). This means the network switch needs to provide power to the sensor, or a PoE injector needs to be utilized. For specifics on power requirements, see the [1st generation](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/sensors-overview.pdf)
 and [2nd generation](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
 sensor datasheets.

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/air-quality-sensor-network-settings#network-time-security-nts)

Network Time Security (NTS)


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

SV20 series sensors can use Network Time Security (NTS) which uses a Secure Socket Layer (SSL) for secure time synchronization, unlike NTP. We recommend you exempt these connections from SSL decryption policies.

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/air-quality-sensor-network-settings#firewall-settings)

Firewall settings


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sensors require access to many endpoints to ensure they can communicate with Command and all features will be accessible. Many customers may want to allow the sensors to communicate with the general required endpoints.

These are the general domains to allow, **applicable for all organization-regions**:

Copy

    *.verkada.com - UDP/123 + TCP+UDP/443
    time.cloudflare.com - TCP/4460 + UDP/123

If you prefer a more granular allowlist, you can add both IP addresses and full FQDNs to your firewall rules based on the region where your devices are located.

Your region is selected when you [create an organization](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
 in Command.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/air-quality-sensor-network-settings#region-united-states)

Region: United States

Copy

    api.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443 
    api.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    firmware.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    index.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    time.control.verkada.com - UDP/123
    update.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.global-prod.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vsensor.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    time.cloudflare.com - TCP/4460 + UDP/123

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/air-quality-sensor-network-settings#region-europe)

Region: Europe

Copy

    api.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.prod2.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    index.prod2.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.prod2.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    time.control.verkada.com - UDP/123
    update.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.global-prod.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.prod2.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vsensor.prod2.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/air-quality-sensor-network-settings#region-australia)

Region: Australia

Copy

    api.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.prod-ap-syd.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    index.prod-ap-syd.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.prod-ap-syd.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    time.control.verkada.com - UDP/123
    update.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.global-prod.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.prod-ap-syd.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vsensor.prod-ap-syd.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443

Use the [Verkada Network Tester](https://network-tester.support.verkada.com/)
 to verify your devices can connect to Verkada Command. Select your region and the **Air Quality** product type to run the check.

The following endpoints must be allowed on your network for the test to work:

*   speed.cloudflare.com
    
*   network-tester.support.verkada.com

# Get Started with Verkada Air Quality Sensors | Air Quality | Verkada Help

Verkada Air Quality Sensors offer a variety of different readings to ensure safe air quality and elevate building performance.

⚠️ **Warning**. The Verkada sensors are not life safety devices and do not satisfy the requirements to be used as emergency smoke or carbon monoxide detectors.

You need Org Admin and/or Site Admin [permissions](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
 for your Verkada Command organization to complete these actions.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/get-started-with-verkada-air-quality-sensors#what-you-need)

What you need

*   PoE-enabled switch or PoE injector
    
*   DHCP-enabled network
    
*   Cat5 or Cat6 cabling
    

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/get-started-with-verkada-air-quality-sensors#create-a-site)

Create a site


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sites are the logical way of grouping and managing devices within your Command organization. Site-level permissions make managing and viewing your devices easier. See [Manage Your Sites and Subsites](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/manage-sites-and-subsites)
 for more information on site creation and management.

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/get-started-with-verkada-air-quality-sensors#add-a-sensor)

Add a sensor


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sensors can be added from the **Devices** page or directly from a site. At least one sensor needs to be added to Command before you can see the **Air Quality** tab in the **All Products** menu. See [Add a Device to Your Command Account](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/add-a-device-to-your-command-organization)
 for more information.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/get-started-with-verkada-air-quality-sensors#sensor-readings)

Sensor readings

Verkada sensors detect a wide variety of readings that are used to track information about your environment. See [Air Quality Sensor Readings](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
 for an in-depth explanation of the sensor readings.

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/get-started-with-verkada-air-quality-sensors#licensing)

Licensing


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Every sensor you manage in Command needs a license. Verkada licensing is applied for each Command organization, and the licenses co-term to a single expiration date. Your licenses may have been automatically added if you claimed your devices via order number. Otherwise, manually add the licenses from the Admin page. See [Manage Your Licenses](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses)
 for more information on adding and managing licenses.

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/get-started-with-verkada-air-quality-sensors#connect-your-sensor)

Connect your sensor


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

While Verkada sensors are considered low-voltage devices that do not require a certified electrician to install, we strongly recommend you work with a system integrator or other professional for installation.

Refer to the sensor’s [setup guide](https://www.verkada.com/docs/?product=sensors&contentType=setupGuide)
 for mounting instructions.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/get-started-with-verkada-air-quality-sensors#power-and-network)

Power and network

Verkada sensors use Power over Ethernet (PoE) for power and communication over the LAN. In most cases, sensors will need to connect directly to a standard switch. PoE injectors can be used when a PoE switch is not available. See the sensor’s [datasheet](https://www.verkada.com/docs/?product=sensors&contentType=datasheet)
 for the power requirements of your specific sensor model.

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/get-started-with-verkada-air-quality-sensors#check-network-settings)

Check network settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada sensors are designed to be plug-and-play. However, if your environment includes a firewall with custom rules and policies, you may need to make some configuration changes to get your sensors connected to the cloud. See [Air Quality Sensor Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/air-quality-sensor-network-settings)
 for more information.

If you require your device to have a specific IP address, create a DHCP reservation using the device’s Media Access Control (MAC) address (found on the device’s label). You can also set up [static IP addresses](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/configure-static-ip-addresses-for-air-quality-sensors-sv20-series-only)
 in Command for SV20 Series Air Quality Sensor Devices.

To configure a static IP address on a sensor device, the device must initially connect to Command and update to the latest firmware using DHCP. Once the update process is complete, it will have the ability to receive the new static IP configuration.

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/get-started-with-verkada-air-quality-sensors#configure-alerts)

Configure alerts


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada Command allows you to receive push, email, and SMS alerts for events generated in your organization. The ![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-91bd70c6d63692bdc09cfe2b790499421775da49%252F05283db7c21547b9b9a924fe0723bd14f6720315.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=461661e3&sv=2) in the bottom left of Command takes you to the **Alerts** page where you can set up and manage alerts. Sensor events include vape detection, tamper detection, air quality index, and more. See [Configure Air Quality Event Alerts](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/events-and-alerts/configure-air-quality-event-alerts)
 for more information on sensor events and creating alerts.

Last updated 1 day ago

Was this helpful?

# Sensor Data | Air Quality | Verkada Help

[Air Quality Sensor Status LED](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-status-led)
[Audio Recording with the SV25](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/audio-recording-with-the-sv25)

# MT81 Cloud-Managed Security Trailer FAQ | Security Trailer | Verkada Help

Review these FAQs to optimize your MT81 Cloud-Managed Security Trailer experience.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#trials-purchasing-and-returns)

Trials, purchasing, & returns


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When should I buy a Verkada trailer vs. a third-party trailer with Verkada cameras and gateways?[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#when-should-i-buy-a-verkada-trailer-vs.-a-third-party-trailer-with-verkada-cameras-and-gateways)

The MT81 is a cloud-managed, streamlined solution with a standard configuration that works across the United States. We strongly recommend reviewing our two [Verkada-Validated Configurations](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/mt81-security-trailer-datasheet.pdf#page=8)
 and selecting whichever one better meets your needs for your trailer solution. A customer’s security requirements, budget, and weather forecast will all impact what the best solution is for them. We fully support our ecosystem of Verkada partners to offer tailored solutions for these needs.

Is the MT81 available for trial?[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#is-the-mt81-available-for-trial)

MT81 trials are not available at this time. However, you can request a demo through your Verkada Account Executive or by contacting [\[email protected\]](https://help.verkada.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
.

Purchased MT81s can be returned under our 30-day return policy. Customers are responsible for arranging and paying for return shipping. Returns over $250,000 USD are subject to Verkada approval.

How can I purchase the MT81?[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#how-can-i-purchase-the-mt81)

The MT81 is available to purchase through the Verkada partner network.

What’s the difference between the two sizes - MT81-6KWH and MT81-13KWH[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#whats-the-difference-between-the-two-sizes-mt81-6kwh-and-mt81-13kwh)

The only difference is battery capacity. The MT81-6KWH features a single 6.6KWH lithium ion battery pack. The MT81-13KWH features two 6.6KWH lithium ion battery packs for 13.2KWH total capacity.

Can I return my trailer?[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#can-i-return-my-trailer)

Yes, trailers are covered by our 30-day return policy. Customers are responsible for arranging and paying for return shipping. Reach out to [\[email protected\]](https://help.verkada.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
 to initiate a return.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#warranty-and-repairs)

Warranty & repairs


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Is the MT81 covered under warranty?[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#is-the-mt81-covered-under-warranty)

The MT81 includes a parts-only 5-year warranty. The warranty does not cover servicing or field installation. Claims are managed by Verkada Support and fulfilled by Wanco, subject to their lead times.

A part on my trailer is broken. What should I do?[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#a-part-on-my-trailer-is-broken.-what-should-i-do)

Contact Verkada Support and provide your MT81 serial number with photos of the damaged component. Either Verkada Support will troubleshoot and diagnose the issue, or involve Wanco if it is a trailer specific component needing to be investigated.

Will Verkada service my trailer?[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#will-verkada-service-my-trailer)

Trailer servicing and warranty field installation is handled through the Verkada partner network.

Who is Wanco?[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#who-is-wanco)

Wanco is the manufacturer Verkada partners with to build the MT81 trailer.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#third-party-modifications)

Third-party modifications


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Can I mount third-party devices on my Verkada trailer?[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#can-i-mount-third-party-devices-on-my-verkada-trailer)

_Customers may use third-party cameras, gateways, and devices, but mounting_ compatibility isn’t guaranteed. Third-party devices can’t be monitored in Command, have limited data on the Verkada data plan, and may reduce trailer battery life and uptime.

The MT81 trailer is not compatible with [Verkada Command Connectors](https://www.verkada.com/security-cameras/command-connector/)
. Command Connectors are typically used to monitor 3rd party cameras in Verkada Command but are only recommended for indoor environments.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#command-management)

Command management


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

How do I add the MT81 or the attached Verkada devices to Command?[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#how-do-i-add-the-mt81-or-the-attached-verkada-devices-to-command)

MT81s are commissioned into command similar to any other Verkada device.

Do all of the Verkada devices mounted on the MT81 need to be in the same organization and site?[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#do-all-of-the-verkada-devices-mounted-on-the-mt81-need-to-be-in-the-same-organization-and-site)

Not all devices mounted on the MT81 are required to be in the same org, however we strongly recommend all devices are in the same org to ensure a seamless user experience.

Can I add third-party trailers to Verkada Command?[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#can-i-add-third-party-trailers-to-verkada-command)

Trailer management in Verkada Command is exclusively available to the MT series.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#power-and-battery)

Power and battery


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

What do I do when my battery runs out and I can’t charge via solar?[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#what-do-i-do-when-my-battery-runs-out-and-i-cant-charge-via-solar)

You can plug your trailer into an outlet using the male AC port.

Can I monitor battery usage in Command?[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#can-i-monitor-battery-usage-in-command)

Yes, current and historical battery charge percentage is available on the stats page in Command.

Can I provide supplemental power to the MT81?[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#can-i-provide-supplemental-power-to-the-mt81)

Yes you can connect shore power or a generator to the trailer to add supplementary power. This is most helpful in times of low sunlight where you may not get a full battery charge during the day. Set up power alerts to be notified if your trailer is running low on battery power, so you can connect supplementary power to ensure consistent device uptime.

How long will the charge on my battery last on a single charge?[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#how-long-will-the-charge-on-my-battery-last-on-a-single-charge)

*   Battery lifespan depends on the number of devices on your trailer and the weather.
    
*   For most configurations - [including VVC1 and VVC2](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/mt81-security-trailer-datasheet.pdf#page=8)
    
    1.  MT81-6KWH will last >2 days without additional charging
        
    2.  MT81-13KWH will last > 4 days without additional charging
        
    

What is the MT81 battery lifespan?[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#what-is-the-mt81-battery-lifespan)

These lithium ion batteries have a warranty period of 5 years.

If a customer buys the 6KWH version and needs a higher capacity, are they able to buy more batteries?[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#if-a-customer-buys-the-6kwh-version-and-needs-a-higher-capacity-are-they-able-to-buy-more-batteries)

We have a path to upgrade batteries. Contact your account rep or [\[email protected\]](https://help.verkada.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#shipping-and-installation)

Shipping & installation


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

How is the MT81 delivered?[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#how-is-the-mt81-delivered)

MT81 trailers are delivered by flatbed truck. Customers or partners need a forklift for unloading and equipment to tow them to the final location.

Are cameras installed on the trailer before shipping?[](https://help.verkada.com/security-trailer/mt81-cloud-managed-security-trailer-faq#are-cameras-installed-on-the-trailer-before-shipping)

Trailers do not ship with Verkada devices installed. Installation of the devices is completed by the partner.

Last updated 20 hours ago

# Roles and Permissions for Gateway | Connectivity | Verkada Help

This article describes the set of roles and associated permissions for Verkada [Gateways](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/gc31-cellular-gateway-datasheet.pdf)
. For more information on roles and permissions for other Verkada product lines, see [Roles and Permissions for Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
.

*   **Site-level roles** determine the access a user or group has to devices in the site.
    
*   **Org-level roles** allow users or groups to manage permissions and devices at a global level.
    
*   **Permissions** are set using roles, which define the level of access users and groups have to devices and settings within an organization and its sites.
    

* * *

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/roles-and-permissions-for-gateway#permissions-considerations)

Permissions considerations

*   Subsites inherit permissions from all parent sites, including the ultimate parent.
    
*   Users can belong to multiple groups. When roles conflict, the user receives the **highest role** granted directly or through any group.
    
*   Group-assigned roles can be manually upgraded but not downgraded. Remove the user from the group with the higher role to downgrade their access.
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/roles-and-permissions-for-gateway#site-level-roles)

Site-level roles


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

No Access[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/roles-and-permissions-for-gateway#no-access)

A No Access user cannot view gateways within a site.

Live-Only Viewer[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/roles-and-permissions-for-gateway#live-only-viewer)

A Live-Only Viewer user cannot view gateways within a site.

Site Viewer[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/roles-and-permissions-for-gateway#site-viewer)

Site Viewers can:

*   Access Gateway Home page
    
*   Access Gateway Details Page
    
*   Run Speed test
    
*   View connected devices
    
*   View historical power usage
    
*   View Activity logs
    
*   View data graphs
    
*   Set up alerts
    

Site Admin[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/roles-and-permissions-for-gateway#site-admin)

Site Admins can do everything Site Viewers can as well as:

*   Claim Device
    
*   Setup Device
    
*   Manage Device
    
*   Delete Device
    
*   Manage data License
    
*   Access Gateway Home page
    
*   Access Gateway Details Page
    
*   Run Speed test
    
*   Run Packet capture
    
*   View connected devices
    
*   Power cycle ports
    
*   View historical power usage
    
*   Switch to WAN mode
    
*   View Activity logs
    
*   Claim connected devices
    
*   Change network settings
    
*   Toggle smart data usage
    
*   View data graphs
    
*   Identify Device
    
*   Reboot Device
    
*   Set up alerts
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/roles-and-permissions-for-gateway#org-level-roles)

Org-level roles


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Org Admin[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/roles-and-permissions-for-gateway#org-admin)

Org Admins can:

*   Claim SW License
    
*   Claim data License
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/roles-and-permissions-for-gateway#set-permissions)

Set permissions


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can set site permissions for existing users and groups by managing user roles, groups, or sites.

You will have access to all cameras, viewing stations, air quality sensors, intercoms, gateways, New Alarms, and Command Connectors once you have been granted permissions for a site.

Users[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/roles-and-permissions-for-gateway#users)

1.  In Verkada Command, go to **All Products > Admin**.
    
2.  Under **Org Settings > Users & Permissions**, select **Users**.
    
3.  Select a user.
    
4.  At the top right, click **Manage Roles**.
    
    1.  Set the needed permissions.
        
    2.  Click **Save**.
        
    

Groups[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/roles-and-permissions-for-gateway#groups)

1.  In Verkada Command, go to **All Products > Admin**.
    
2.  Under **Org Settings > Users & Permissions**, select **Groups**.
    
3.  Select a group.
    
4.  At the top, select **Site Roles > Manage Roles**.
    
    1.  Set the needed permissions.
        
    2.  Click **Save**.
        
    

Sites[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/roles-and-permissions-for-gateway#sites)

1.  In Verkada Command, go to **All Products > Admin**.
    
2.  In the left navigation, select **Sites**.
    
3.  At the top left, click **Manage Sites**.
    
4.  Select a site to manage and in the right pane, click **Manage**.
    
    1.  In the top right, click **Add** to add a new user or group.
        
    2.  Select an existing user or group to edit their permissions.
        
    

Last updated 22 hours ago

Was this helpful?

# Classic Alarms Network Settings | Classic Alarms | Verkada Help

This article is a guide for classic Alarms. Refer to this [article](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/alarms-specifications/alarms-network-settings)
 if you have new Alarms. See [New Alarms vs Classic Alarms](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/new-alarms-vs-classic-alarms)
 if you are unsure which version of Alarms you have.

* * *

This article outlines the required network settings that your Verkada Classic Alarms devices need to communicate with [Verkada Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
. For more information on the required network settings for other Verkada product lines see [Required Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings)
.

Verkada devices are incompatible with LANs that require proxy servers or Secure Socket Layer (SSL)/Transport Layer Security (TLS) inspection. If either is in use, a bypass for all Verkada devices must be implemented for Verkada devices to communicate with Verkada Command.

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/classic-alarms-network-settings#ip-address)

IP address


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Alarms devices must be assigned an IPv4 address to communicate on the LAN and to Verkada Command. Alarms devices use Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP) and User Datagram Protocol (UDP) to obtain their IP addresses and network configurations.

If you require your Alarms device to have a specific IP address, create a DHCP reservation using the device’s Media Access Control (MAC) address (found on the device’s label).

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/classic-alarms-network-settings#domain-name-system)

Domain Name System


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Alarms devices use the DNS server to resolve Verkada’s fully qualified domain names (FQDN) to IP addresses to communicate with them. Your DHCP server tells the Alarms device where the DNS server is on the network and the Alarms device communicates using UDP port 53.

DNS over HTTPS (DoH) is currently not supported.

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/classic-alarms-network-settings#power)

Power


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Some Alarms devices are powered through Power over Ethernet (PoE). This means the network switch needs to provide power to them, or a PoE injector needs to be utilized. For specifics on power requirements, see the [Alarms device’s datasheet](https://www.verkada.com/docs/?product=alarms&contentType=datasheet)
.

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/classic-alarms-network-settings#firewall-settings)

Firewall settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Alarms devices require access to many endpoints to ensure they can communicate with Command and all features will be accessible. Many customers may want to allow the devices to communicate with the general required endpoints.

These are the general domains to allow, **applicable for all organization-regions**:

Copy

    34.216.15.26 - UDP/123
    *.verkada.com - UDP/123 + TCP+UDP/443
    *.appcenter.ms - TCP/443
    global.turn.twilio.com - TCP/443

If you prefer a more granular allowlist, you can add IP addresses, full FQDNs, and wildcard domains to your firewall rules based on the region where your devices are located.

Your region is selected when you [create an organization](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
 in Command.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/classic-alarms-network-settings#region-united-states)

Region: United States

Copy

    34.216.15.26 - UDP/123
    alarms.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    alarms.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    firmware.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    index.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    time.control.verkada.com - UDP/123
    update.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    valarm.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    valarm.global-prod.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.global-prod.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    *.appcenter.ms - TCP/443
    global.turn.twilio.com - TCP/443

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/classic-alarms-network-settings#region-europe)

Region: Europe

Copy

    alarms.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    alarms.prod2.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.prod2.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    index.prod2.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.prod2.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    time.control.verkada.com - UDP/123
    update.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    valarm.global-prod.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    valarm.prod2.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vbroadcast.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vbroadcast.prod2.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.global-prod.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.prod2.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/classic-alarms-network-settings#all-regions)

All regions

BC51s **in all regions** require these endpoints:

Copy

    *.apple.com - TCP/80
    *.apple.com - TCP/443
    *.apple.com - TCP/2197
    *.apple.com - TCP/5223
    *.apple.com - UDP/123
    crl.entrust.net - TCP/80
    crl3.digicert.com - TCP/80
    crl4.digicert.com - TCP/80
    global.stun.twilio.com - UDP/3478
    global.turn.twilio.com - UDP/3478
    *.mzstatic.com - TCP/80
    *.mzstatic.com - TCP/443
    ocsp.digicert.com - TCP/80
    ocsp.entrust.net - TCP/80
    vmdm.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vmdm.global-prod.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443

BK21s in **all regions** require these endpoints:

Copy

    time.cloudflare.com - TCP/4460
    time.cloudflare.com - UDP/123

BZ11s in **all regions** require these endpoints:

Copy

    global.stun.twilio.com - UDP/3478
    global.turn.twilio.com - UDP/3478

Use the [Verkada Network Tester](https://network-tester.support.verkada.com/)
 to verify your devices can connect to Verkada Command. Select your region and the **Classic Alarms** product type to run the check.

The following endpoints must be allowed on your network for the test to work:

*   speed.cloudflare.com
    
*   network-tester.support.verkada.com

# Get Started with the Cellular Gateway | Connectivity | Verkada Help

Verkada’s [GC31 Cellular Gateway](https://www.verkada.com/cellular-gateway)
 helps you connect Verkada products in remote locations, such as parks, parking lots, construction sites, oil and gas drilling sites, school buses, and even police cars. Anyone can easily set up the GC31 with its Power over Ethernet (PoE) input and PoE output. You can also easily manage and troubleshoot the router remotely via [Verkada Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
.

The GC31 natively integrates with Verkada products to enable faster setup, remote troubleshooting, and more efficient data usage. The GC31 instantly recognizes any Verkada device you connect to it, eliminating the need to input serial numbers or scan QR codes during device setup. You can track data usage for each connected device and receive alerts if a device is offline.

More key features include:

*   View the status and GPS location of your gateways
    
*   See which cell tower each gateway is using
    
*   Remotely run packet capture and speed tests
    
*   Remotely power cycle devices
    
*   Recognize connected Verkada devices and streamline setup.
    

[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/get-started-with-the-cellular-gateway#step-1-set-up-verkada-command)

Step 1: Set up Verkada Command


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Required**. You must create a [Verkada Command account](https://command.verkada.com/register)
 to activate and configure a GC31. You must be an Org Admin to configure a GC31. Learn more about [Roles and Permissions for Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
.

[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/get-started-with-the-cellular-gateway#step-2-set-up-the-hardware)

Step 2: Set up the hardware


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Follow the steps to set up, install (wire and mount) the GC31 ([indoor](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/gc31-indoor-cellular-gateway-install-guide.pdf)
) | GC31-E ([outdoor](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/gc31e-outdoor-cellular-gateway-install-guide.pdf)
).

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/get-started-with-the-cellular-gateway#troubleshoot-the-gc31)

Troubleshoot the GC31


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you experience any issues with your GC31, we recommend following these steps:

1

**Power cycle the GC31.**

2

**If the device connected to the GC31 is not getting power, check for the following:**

*   Is the GC31 powered on?
    
    *   If not, check the power input to the GC31.
        
    
*   Is the GC31 powered by a PoE injector?
    
    *   Check if the injector is rated to provide enough power (must be 90W) to the GC31 and devices connected to it.
        
    *   Check if the ethernet cable is connected properly and is verified.
        
    
*   Is the gateway powered through the terminal block?
    
    *   Check if the power input line is rated 12–36V and is providing enough wattage to power the GC31 and devices connected to it.
        
    
*   Is the GC31 powered through an AC/DC power adapter?
    
    *   Check if the power input line is rated 12–36V and is providing enough wattage to power the GC31 and devices connected to it.
        
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/get-started-with-the-cellular-gateway#faq)

FAQ


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

How should I manage the cellular connectivity?[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/get-started-with-the-cellular-gateway#how-should-i-manage-the-cellular-connectivity)

A common issue with the GC31 is that the cellular connectivity might not be powerful enough. If this is the case, consider external/directional antennas to increase the signal strength and connectivity.

What if I have a weak connection?[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/get-started-with-the-cellular-gateway#what-if-i-have-a-weak-connection)

If cameras don’t have a good connection, when making changes, such as enabling analytics, the CV image might not get downloaded properly. A weak connection might lead to issues with uploading and downloading data, resulting in degraded device performance. The only way to resolve this issue is to reboot the camera so that it attempts again.

Last updated 22 hours ago

Was this helpful?

# Roles and Permissions for Classic Alarms | Classic Alarms | Verkada Help

This article is a guide for classic Alarms. Refer to this [article](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-new-alarms)
 if you have new Alarms. See [New Alarms vs Classic Alarms](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/new-alarms-vs-classic-alarms)
 if you are unsure which version of Alarms you have.

* * *

This article describes the set of roles and associated permissions for [Verkada Classic Alarms](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/alarms-professional-monitoring-overview.pdf)
. For more information on roles and permissions for other Verkada product lines, see [Roles and Permissions for Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
.

*   **Site-level roles** determine the access a user or group has to devices in the site.
    
*   **Org-level roles** allow users or groups to manage permissions and devices at a global level.
    
*   **Permissions** are set using roles, which define the level of access users and groups have to devices and settings within an organization and its sites.
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-classic-alarms#site-level-roles)

Site-level roles


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

No Access[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-classic-alarms#no-access)

*   By default, cannot arm/disarm Alarm sites.
    
*   Unable to view any details about Alarm sites in Command.
    
*   When explicitly granted alarm user permissions, can arm/disarm an Alarm site in Command and from the Alarms mobile app.
    

Live-Only Viewer[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-classic-alarms#live-only-viewer)

*   By default, cannot arm/disarm Alarm sites.
    
*   When explicitly granted alarm user permissions, can arm/disarm an Alarm site in Command and from the Alarms mobile app.
    
*   If Arm/Disarm Geofencing is enabled, the user will only be able to arm/disarm sites from the Verkada Alarms Mobile App.
    
*   See live video and new events on the Alarm site page.
    

Site Viewer[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-classic-alarms#site-viewer)

*   By default, cannot arm/disarm Alarm sites.
    
*   When explicitly granted alarm user permissions, can arm/disarm an Alarm site in Command and from the Alarms mobile app.
    
*   If Arm/Disarm Geofencing is enabled, the user will only be able to arm/disarm sites from the Verkada Alarms Mobile App.
    
*   View all alarm activity and event history with historical footage.
    
*   Listen in and initiate talk-downs to the alarm console.
    

Site Admin[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-classic-alarms#site-admin)

*   By default, can arm/disarm sites via Command and the Alarms mobile app. You can find the arm/disarm capability in the user settings profile (**Site Access** > **Alarm User** checkbox).
    
*   Update all site settings, including trigger events and alarm response notifications/actions, via the Command and Alarms mobile apps.
    
*   Add or remove Verkada devices and wired inputs/outputs on the site.
    
*   View all alarm activity and event history with historical video.
    
*   Listen in and initiate talk-downs to the alarm console.
    

You also need Org Admin permissions to generate key codes.

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-classic-alarms#org-level-roles)

Org-level roles


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Org Admin[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-classic-alarms#org-admin)

*   Can generate user key codes.
    
*   By default, can arm/disarm sites via Command and the Alarms mobile app. You can find the arm/disarm capability in the user settings profile (**Site Access** > **Alarm User** checkbox).
    
*   Set up new alarm sites and change all site settings, including trigger events and alarm response notifications/actions via Command and the Alarms mobile app.
    
*   Add or remove Verkada devices and wired inputs/outputs on the site.
    
*   View all alarm activity and event history with historical video.
    
*   Listen in and initiate talk-downs to the alarm console.
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-classic-alarms#set-permissions)

Set permissions


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Users[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-classic-alarms#users)

In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .UnderOrg Settings, select Users.Select a user.At the top right, click Manage Roles.a. Check the Alarm User box. b. Click Save.

Groups[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-classic-alarms#groups)

In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .UnderOrg Settings, select Groups.Select a group.At the top, select Site Roles > Manage Roles.a. Check the Alarm User box. b. Click Save.

Sites[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-classic-alarms#sites)

In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .In the left navigation, select Sites.Select a site to manage and in the right pane, click Manage .a. In the top right, click Add to add a new user or group. b. Select an existing user or group to edit their permissions.

Last updated 23 hours ago

Was this helpful?

# Gateways Network Settings | Connectivity | Verkada Help

This article outlines the required network settings that your Verkada [Gateways](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/gc31-cellular-gateway-datasheet.pdf)
 need to communicate with [Verkada Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
. The gateways can connect to your network by utilizing the [WAN Failover](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/configuration-and-setup/use-cellular-gateways-for-wan-failover)
 mode. For more information on the required network settings for other Verkada product lines, see [Required Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings)
.

Verkada devices are incompatible with LANs that require proxy servers or Secure Socket Layer (SSL)/Transport Layer Security (TLS) inspection. If either is in use, a bypass for all Verkada devices must be implemented for Verkada devices to communicate with Verkada Command.

[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/gateways-network-settings#status-led)

**Status LED**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A flashing blue status LED on the gateway indicates the device is not communicating with Command. Check the [status LED](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/configuration-and-setup/cellular-gateway-status-leds)
 doc for explanations of each LED pattern. If you see this behavior, check that the network is set up with the gateway’s requirements. If the problem persists, contact [Verkada Support](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support)
.

When gateways are offline, alerts/events do not trigger. They continue to record data and sync with Command once they reconnect.

[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/gateways-network-settings#ip-address)

**IP address**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada gateways must be assigned an IPv4 address to communicate on the LAN and to Verkada Command. Gateways use Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP) and User Datagram Protocol (UDP) to obtain their IP addresses and network configurations.

[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/gateways-network-settings#domain-name-system)

**Domain Name System**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada gateways use the DNS server to resolve Verkada’s fully qualified domain names (FQDN) to IP addresses to communicate with them. Your DHCP server tells the gateway where the DNS server is on the network and the gateway communicates using UDP port 53.

DNS over HTTPS (DoH) is currently not supported.

[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/gateways-network-settings#power)

**Power**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada GC31-Es are powered through Power over Ethernet (PoE). This means the network switch needs to provide power to the GC31-E, or a PoE injector needs to be utilized. A GC31 is powered through a barrel-jack adapter. For specifics on power requirements, see the [gateway’s datasheet](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/gc31-cellular-gateway-datasheet.pdf)
.

[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/gateways-network-settings#firewall-settings)

**Firewall settings**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Gateways require access to many endpoints to ensure they can communicate with Command and all features will be accessible. Many customers may want to allow the gateways to communicate with the general required endpoints.

These are the general domains to allow, **applicable for all organization-regions:**

Copy

    34.216.15.26 - UDP/123
    *.verkada.com - UDP/123 + TCP+UDP/443

If you prefer a more granular allowlist, you can add both IP addresses and full FQDNs to your firewall rules based on the region where your devices are located.

Your region is selected when you [create an organization](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
 in Command.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/gateways-network-settings#region-united-states)

**Region: United States**

Copy

    34.216.15.26 - UDP/123
    api.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    firmware.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    index.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    time.control.verkada.com - UDP/123
    update.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.global-prod.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vnet.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/gateways-network-settings#region-europe)

**Region: Europe**

Copy

    api.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.prod2.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    index.prod2.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.prod2.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    time.control.verkada.com - UDP/123
    update.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.global-prod.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.prod2.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vnet.prod2.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/gateways-network-settings#region-australia)

**Region: Australia**

Copy

    api.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.prod-ap-syd.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    index.prod-ap-syd.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.prod-ap-syd.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    time.control.verkada.com - UDP/123
    update.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.global-prod.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.prod-ap-syd.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vnet.prod-ap-syd.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443

Use the [Verkada Network Tester](https://network-tester.support.verkada.com/)
 to verify your devices can connect to Verkada Command. Select your region and the **Gateways** product type to run the check.

The following endpoints must be allowed on your network for the test to work:

*   speed.cloudflare.com
    
*   network-tester.support.verkada.com
