# Required Camera Network Settings - Government Solutions | Government Solutions | Verkada Help

Verkada devices need to communicate with a [Government Solution Command organization](https://www.verkada.com/solutions/government-grade)
 via their local network. In most cases, minimal updates to your network settings are needed. Additional configuration may be required for complex or highly secure networks.

See [Required Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings)
 for more information on the required network settings for other Verkada product lines.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-camera-network-settings-government-solutions#compatibility)

Compatibility


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada devices are incompatible with local area networks (LANs) that require proxy servers or Secure Socket Layer (SSL)/Transport Layer Security (TLS) inspection. If either is in use, a bypass for all Verkada devices must be implemented for your Verkada devices to communicate with Verkada Command.

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-camera-network-settings-government-solutions#ip-address)

IP address


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada devices must be assigned an IPv4 address to communicate on the LAN and to Verkada Command through the internet. By default, all Verkada devices use Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP) and User Datagram Protocol (UDP) to obtain their IP addresses and network configurations.

If you require your device to have a specific IP address, create a DHCP reservation using the device’s Media Access Control (MAC) address (found on the device’s label). You can also set up [static IP addresses](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/hardware-installation/advanced-installation/configure-static-ip-addresses-for-cameras)
 in Command for cameras.

Verkada devices may utilize path MTU discovery to determine the maximum transmission unit of the network path. Therefore, it is necessary to permit ICMP Fragmentation Needed (Type 3, Code 4) and ICMPv6 Packet Too Big (Type 2) packets. Ensure your firewall(s) are configured to permit this in the return path to your Verkada devices.

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-camera-network-settings-government-solutions#domain-name-system)

Domain Name System


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada devices use the Domain Name System (DNS) server to resolve Verkada’s fully qualified domain names (FQDN) to IP addresses to communicate with them. Your DHCP server tells the Verkada device where the DNS server is on the network, and the device communicates using UDP port 53.

DNS over HTTPS (DoH) is not currently supported.

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-camera-network-settings-government-solutions#power)

Power


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Most Verkada devices are powered through Power over Ethernet (PoE). You can use the product [datasheets](https://www.verkada.com/docs/?contentType=datasheet)
 to figure out the power requirements for your Verkada devices.

These are the most common power requirements:

*   IEE 802.3af, Type 1 PoE
    
*   IEEE 802.3at, Type 2 PoE+
    
*   IEEE 802.3bt, Type 3 PoE++
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-camera-network-settings-government-solutions#camera-firewall-settings)

Camera firewall settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada cameras require access to many endpoints to ensure they can communicate with Command and that all features are accessible.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-camera-network-settings-government-solutions#region-united-states-gov)

Region: United States Gov

*   api.global-prod.control.verkada.com (HTTPS/443)
    
*   update.control.verkada.com (HTTPS/443)
    
*   NTP: returned by DHCP client option 42, if not provided, falls back to time.nist.gov (UDP/123)
    
*   Local streaming: \*:4100 on LAN (HTTPS/443)
    
*   RTSP: \*:8554 on LAN
    
*   \*.kinesisvideo.us-gov-west-1.amazonaws.com (HTTPS/443)
    
*   s3.us-gov-west-1.amazonaws.com (HTTPS/443)
    
*   verkada-firmware.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com (HTTPS/443)
    
*   \*.prod-govus-pine.control.verkadagov.com (HTTPS/443)
    
*   api.control.verkada.com (HTTPS/443)
    

* * *

**Prefer to see it in action?** Check out the [video tutorial](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=5pRUeH_bhw0)
.

# Mailroom Network Settings | Mailroom | Verkada Help

This article outlines the required network settings that your [Verkada Mailroom](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/mailroom-overview.pdf)
 tablets and phones need to be able to communicate with [Verkada Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
. For more information on the required network settings for other Verkada product lines see [Required Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings)
.

Verkada devices are incompatible with LANs that require proxy servers or Secure Socket Layer (SSL)/Transport Layer Security (TLS) inspection. If either is in use, a bypass for all Verkada devices must be implemented for Verkada devices to communicate with Verkada Command.

[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/mailroom-network-settings#ip-address)

IP address


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mailroom tablets and phones must be assigned an IPv4 address to communicate on the LAN and to Verkada Command. Mailroom devices use Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP) and User Datagram Protocol (UDP) to obtain their IP addresses and network configurations.

If you require your Mailroom device to have a specific IP address, create a DHCP reservation using the device’s Media Access Control (MAC) address (found on the device’s label).

[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/mailroom-network-settings#domain-name-system)

Domain Name System


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mailroom tablets and phones use the DNS server to resolve Verkada’s fully qualified domain names (FQDN) to IP addresses to communicate with them. Your DHCP server tells the Mailroom device where the DNS server is on the network and the Mailroom device communicates using UDP port 53.

DNS over HTTPS (DoH) is currently not supported.

[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/mailroom-network-settings#firewall-settings)

Firewall settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mailroom tablets and phones require access to many endpoints to ensure they can communicate with Command and all features will be accessible. Many customers may want to allow the Mailroom devices to communicate with the general required endpoints.

These are the general domains to allow, **applicable for all organization-regions**:

Copy

    3.1.77.0/24 - UDP/10000-20000
    3.104.90.0/24 - UDP/10000-20000
    3.112.80.0/24 - UDP/10000-20000
    3.122.181.0/24 - UDP/10000-20000
    18.228.249.0/24 - UDP/10000-20000
    34.203.250.0/23 - UDP/10000-20000
    34.216.15.26 - UDP/123
    35.156.191.128/25 - UDP/10000-20000
    52.215.127.0/24 - UDP/10000-20000
    54.65.63.192/26 - UDP/10000-20000
    54.169.127.128/26 - UDP/10000-20000
    54.171.127.192/26 - UDP/10000-20000
    54.172.60.0/23 - UDP/10000-20000
    54.244.51.0/24 - UDP/1024-65535
    54.252.254.64/26 - UDP/10000-20000
    177.71.206.192/26 - UDP/10000-20000
    *.verkada.com - UDP/123 + TCP+UDP/443

If you prefer a more granular allowlist, you can add both IP addresses and full FQDNs to your firewall rules based on the region where your devices are located.

Your region is selected when you [create an organization](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
 in Command.

# Smart Tiles | Viewing Station | Verkada Help

Smart Tiles allows you to display key information from access events, sensor data, and notable camera activity.

You must be an **Org Admin** to claim and manage a Viewing Station.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/smart-tiles#configuration)

Configuration


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Devices.**

2

**Select your viewing station, then click the arrow on the right to open its page.**

3

**At the top right, click Manage Tiles > Smart Tiles.**

4

**Choose the type of Smart Tile to add.**

*   [Active Area](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/smart-tiles#h_269a6209f8)
    
*   [Access Control](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/smart-tiles#h_1e8080a3ec)
    
*   [Sensor Readings](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/smart-tiles#h_df6f11f1ca)
    
*   [Live Face Blur](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/smart-tiles#h_c692516d8c)
    

* * *

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/smart-tiles#active-area)

Active Area

Displays the camera with the most motion. To change which camera(s) display on the active area tile, select the tile to see the information panel where you can select from the following options:

*   **Current Page -** Includes all cameras on the current page.
    
*   **All Pages -** Includes all cameras on all pages.
    
*   **Select Cameras -** Choose which cameras you want to display.
    
    ![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1530499399-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FfFkKNdIGPl0XHde4cZf7%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-6bf65156c31b8abb454223478b8592910b088c34%252F97542e96f9ed47be968c501f4f2afd861575de00.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1cf00117&sv=2)
    

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/smart-tiles#access-control)

Access Control

Displays the most recent door events, including all events visible in **Door History**, such as:

*   Access granted
    
*   Access denied
    
*   Door opened
    
*   Door held open (DHO)
    
*   Door forced open (DFO)
    

When you select this tile, you can choose which door is displayed.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/smart-tiles#sensor-readings)

Sensor Readings

Displays air quality readings from a selected sensor. From the **Customize Data** tab, choose which sensor reading to display in the tile.

See [Air Quality Sensor Readings](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
 for more information.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/smart-tiles#live-face-blur)

Live Face Blur

Displays a live camera feed with faces automatically blurred in real time to protect individual privacy. When you select this tile, choose which camera feed to display with Live Face Blur enabled.

*   The selected camera must support Live Face Blur. See [Enable Face Blur on Verkada Cameras](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/enable-face-blur-on-verkada-cameras)
     for a list of supported cameras.
    
*   The Viewing Station must be running the latest software version and tvOS. You can find the software version and serial number under **Settings > Device**.
    

Last updated 1 day ago

Was this helpful?

# Create Guardian Forms for Reunification | Incident Response | Verkada Help

Verkada Incident Response helps schools manage every step of a Reunification event. Guardian forms allow schools to collect required information from guardians before releasing students.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-guardian-forms-for-reunification#create-guardian-forms)

Create guardian forms


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Admins can create site-specific guardian forms or global forms that can be used across multiple sites.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-guardian-forms-for-reunification#global)

Global

You need at least **Org Admin** permissions to create global guardian forms.

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Workplace Incident Response.**

2

**On the left navigation, click Incident Response Settings.**

3

**Under Guardian Sign-In, select Manage Guardian Forms.**

a. In the top right, select **Add Guardian Form**. b. Enter a unique name. c. Click **Save.**

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-guardian-forms-for-reunification#site-specific)

Site-specific

You need at least **Workplace Site Admin** permissions to create site-specific guardian forms.

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Workplace Incident Response.**

2

**On the left navigation, click Incident Response Settings > your site.**

3

**Under Guardian Sign-In, select Manage Guardian Forms.**

a. In the top right, select **Add Guardian Form**. b. Enter a unique name. c. Click **Save.**

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-guardian-forms-for-reunification#configuration)

Configuration


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All guardian forms must collect the guardian’s name and the names of the students they are requesting. Organizations can also include the following optional steps:

*   Contact Info (email and/or phone number)
    
*   [Security Screening](https://help.verkada.com/guest/configuration-and-setup/guest-security-screening)
    
*   Guardian Photo
    
*   Open Response Questions
    
*   Multiple Choice Questions
    
*   Questionnaires
    
*   Videos
    
*   PDFs
    
*   Documents
    

The security screening step requires capturing an image of the guardian’s ID at check-in. The feature extracts the legal name and date of birth from the ID for verification.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-guardian-forms-for-reunification#add-a-guardian-form-to-a-response-template)

Add a guardian form to a Response template


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A guardian form must be assigned for Response templates enabled for Reunification. You can select the desired form when configuring the Response template. See [Create a Response Template](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-response-templates)
 for more information.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3922624211-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fn49pz7ZddUdVxNdz2EFE%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-2e0f410520a8d71df6264f938ec39670fb823fec%252F5fb614c160fe81792a9622d16160c9152a68a982.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c2ef6906&sv=2)

Last updated 18 hours ago

Was this helpful?

# Viewing Station Network Settings | Viewing Station | Verkada Help

This article outlines the required network settings that your Verkada [viewing stations](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/viewing-station-overview.pdf)
 need to communicate with [Verkada Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
. For more information on the required network settings for other Verkada product lines see [Required Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings)
.

Verkada devices are incompatible with LANs that require proxy servers or Secure Socket Layer (SSL)/Transport Layer Security (TLS) inspection. If either is in use, a bypass for all Verkada devices must be implemented for Verkada devices to communicate with Verkada Command.

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/viewing-station-network-settings#ip-address)

IP address


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Viewing stations must be assigned an IPv4 address to communicate on the LAN and to Verkada Command. Viewing stations support both wired and wireless internet connections. They use Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP) and User Datagram Protocol (UDP) to obtain their IP addresses and network configurations.

If you require your viewing station to have a specific IP address, create a DHCP reservation using the device’s Media Access Control (MAC) address (found on the device’s label).

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/viewing-station-network-settings#domain-name-system)

Domain Name System


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Viewing stations use the DNS server to resolve Verkada’s fully qualified domain names (FQDN) to IP addresses to communicate with them. Your DHCP server tells the intercom where the DNS server is on the network and the intercom communicates using UDP port 53.

DNS over HTTPS (DoH) is currently not supported.

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/viewing-station-network-settings#firewall-settings)

Firewall settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Viewing stations require access to many endpoints to ensure they can communicate with Command and all features will be accessible. Many customers may want to allow the viewing stations to communicate with the general required endpoints.

These are the general domains to allow, **applicable for all organization-regions**:

Copy

    34.216.15.26 - UDP/123
    *:4100 - TCP/UDP on local network
    *.verkada.com - UDP/123 + TCP+UDP/443
    *.vcamera.net - TCP+UDP/443
    apple.com - TCP/80
    apple.com - TCP/443
    *.apple.com - TCP/80
    *.apple.com - TCP/443
    *.apple.com - TCP/2197
    *.apple.com - TCP/5223
    *.apple.com - UDP/123
    *.cdn-apple.com 443
    *.aaplimg.com - TCP/80/443+UDP/123
    app-measurement.com - TCP+UDP/443
    browser-intake-datadoghq.com - TCP+UDP/443
    firebaselogging-pa.googleapis.com - TCP+UDP/443
    crl.entrust.net - TCP/80
    crl3.digicert.com - TCP/80
    crl4.digicert.com - TCP/80
    *.mzstatic.com - TCP/443
    ocsp.digicert.com - TCP/80
    ocsp.entrust.net - TCP/80

If you prefer a more granular allowlist, you can add IP addresses, full FQDNs, and wildcard domains to your firewall rules based on the region where your devices are located.

Your region is selected when you [create an organization](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
 in Command.

# Incident Response Portal | Incident Response | Verkada Help

The Incident Response portal is a web page where employees can account for evacuees during an active Response. Any Workplace employee can access the Incident Response portal to interact with active responses at their site.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/incident-response-portal#incident-response-portal)

Incident Response portal


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When a Response is launched in **Incident** or **Drill mode** with employee notifications enabled, all Workplace employees at the site receive a magic link via email and/or SMS to access the Incident Response portal. Employees can also log in at any time at [unite.my.verkada.com](https://unite.my.verkada.com/)
.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/incident-response-portal#people-status-page)

People Status page


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can search evacuees by name and view or update their status and location. To update an evacuee’s status or location:

1

**Log in to** [**unite.my.verkada.com**](https://unite.my.verkada.com/)
**.**

2

**(Optional) Apply** [**filters**](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/incident-response-portal#h_457b70e469)
**.**

3

**Select an evacuee.**

a. Select a **Status**. b. Select a **Location**. c. Click **Save**.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3922624211-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fn49pz7ZddUdVxNdz2EFE%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-8efa1e1c34ef32faedc58f921e0c38fabd392ad5%252Fe7ed808760100e642989622ddd0b011ee89b8c4c.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=75803cf3&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/incident-response-portal#filters)

Filters

Workplace Employees can use the search bar and filters on the People Status page to find specific evacuees. Filters include:

1

**Evacuee status**

2

**Evacuee location**

3

**Teacher & Section (for K12 customers with an SIS integration)**

4

**Edited by me**

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/incident-response-portal#sign-in-guardians-page)

Sign in Guardians page


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Employees will see the **Sign in Guardians** page for Response Templates with [Reunification enabled](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-response-templates)
. From here, employees can sign in and review guardians:

1

**Log in to** [**unite.my.verkada.com**](https://unite.my.verkada.com/)
**.**

2

**Select the Sign in Guardians page.**

3

**Select your location.**

4

**At the bottom, select Sign in a guardian.**

5

**Fill out the** [**form**](https://app.intercom.com/a/apps/q5re5q6g/knowledge-hub/all-content?activeContentId=13666171&activeContentType=article&editorMode=view&search=guardian%20form)
 **on behalf of the guardian.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3922624211-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fn49pz7ZddUdVxNdz2EFE%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-23eef526c5eceba76c17719709dd72c22943aaf5%252F87cf0fc6596ffd6affb0ebe0c910b2c0eecd386f.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2a62ee05&sv=2)

By default, the **Sign in Guardians** page shows all waiting guardians. Employees can filter to view:

*   All guardians checked in during the Response
    
*   Denied guardians
    
*   Reunified guardians
    

By selecting a guardian, employees can view the student(s) they requested to release and the employee who checked them in.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/incident-response-portal#reunify-students-and-guardians)

Reunify Students and Guardians


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Employees will see the **Reunify Students + Guardians** page for Response Templates with [Reunification enabled](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-response-templates)
. By default, this page displays all student/guardian pairings where:

1

**The student’s status is not unknown and not reunified.**

2

**The guardian is signed in and fully approved (e.g., passed security screening or temporary guardian exception)**

Employees can use location and status filters to refine which pairings appear. Filters only affect the individual’s view and do not impact what other employees see. The location filter applies to both guardians and students.

Last updated 18 hours ago

# Get started with Command Connector | Command Connector | Verkada Help

The Command Connector enables organizations to integrate non-Verkada video feeds into Verkada’s Command platform for centralized video security management. It offers a cost-effective migration for non-Verkada cameras.

You need Organization Admin and/or Site Admin [permissions](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
 for your Verkada Command organization to complete these actions.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/get-started-with-command-connector#what-you-need)

What you need

*   A standard AC electrical outlet
    
*   DHCP-enabled network
    
*   Cat5 or Cat6 cabling
    

[](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/get-started-with-command-connector#create-a-site)

Create a site


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sites are the logical way of grouping and managing devices within your Command organization. Site-level permissions make managing and viewing your devices easier. See [Manage Your Sites and Subsites](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/manage-sites-and-subsites)
 for more information on site creation and management.

[](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/get-started-with-command-connector#add-a-command-connector)

Add a Command Connector


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Command Connectors can be added from the **Devices** page or directly from a site. See [Add a Device to Your Command Account](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/add-a-device-to-your-command-organization)
 for more information.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/get-started-with-command-connector#connect-a-non-verkada-camera)

Connect a non-Verkada camera

You can connect multiple non-Verkada cameras to Command using a Command Connector. All non-Verkada cameras must be on the same LAN and support ONVIF (Profile S). See [Add a Non-Verkada Camera to a Command Connector](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/configuration-and-setup/add-a-non-verkada-camera-to-a-command-connector)
 for more information.

[](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/get-started-with-command-connector#licensing)

Licensing


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Every non-Verkada camera that is connected to the Command Connector will require a valid camera license. The Command Connector itself does not require a license.

Verkada licensing is applied for each Command organization, and the licenses co-term to a single expiration date. Your licenses may have been automatically added if you claimed your devices via order number. Otherwise, manually add the license key from the Admin page. See [Manage Your Licenses](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses)
 for more information on adding and managing licenses.

[](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/get-started-with-command-connector#connect-your-command-connector)

Connect your Command Connector


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

While Command Connectors are considered low-voltage devices that do not require a certified electrician to install, we strongly recommend you work with a system integrator or other professional for installation.

Please refer to the Command Connector [setup guide](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/Verkada-CC300-500-700-Command-Connector-Install-Guide.pdf)
 for instructions on mounting the device. The device can be mounted on a standard 19-inch server rack and takes up 1 rack unit or 1U.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/get-started-with-command-connector#power-and-network)

Power and network

Command Connectors are powered via AC power and connect to your network via Ethernet.

The Command Connector has 2 RJ-45 Ethernet interfaces. Only **connect one** of the interfaces to your network for initial configuration. To configure both ports, see [Configure Two Ethernet Ports for Command Connector](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/configuration-and-setup/configure-two-ethernet-ports-for-command-connector)
.

[](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/get-started-with-command-connector#check-network-settings)

Check Network Settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Command Connector is designed to be plug-and-play. However, if your environment includes a firewall with custom rules and policies, you may need to make some configuration changes to get your connected cameras to stream on Command. See [Command Connector Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/command-connector-network-settings)
 for more information.

Last updated 1 day ago

Was this helpful?

# Create Response Templates | Incident Response | Verkada Help

Workplace Site Admins can create Response Templates for different types of incidents. A Response Template defines:

*   Who needs to be accounted for as evacuees
    
*   What statuses can be assigned to evacuees
    
*   Where evacuees can be marked as present
    

For schools, configure the Response Template for [Reunification](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-response-templates#h_4e94526bd9)
 and set up a Guardian Form.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-response-templates#create-a-response-template)

Create a Response Template


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Workplace Incident Response.**

2

**On the left navigation, click Response Templates.**

3

**At the top, select your site.**

4

**Select Add Template and configure the template settings:**

a. [General](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-response-templates#h_6b3cdc0e04)
 b. [People](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-response-templates#h_f2978457f3)
 c. [Reunification](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-response-templates#h_4e94526bd9)
 d. [People Statuses](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-response-templates#h_57bacd963e)
 e. [Location Names](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-response-templates#h_86abe03c6c)

Response Templates are site-specific and apply to a single site.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-response-templates#general)

General

1

**Enter a unique Template Name.**

2

**Choose Template Color.**

3

**Choose Template Icon.**

4

**Enter a Template Description.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3922624211-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fn49pz7ZddUdVxNdz2EFE%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-bee8dab09c23c3dadb35624470783d209e8a29cb%252F57bec27fc52fb1e2c06b5c79c0756a66e2c2de38.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=41b167a0&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-response-templates#people)

People

This setting defines who will be tracked as evacuees when a Response Template is launched. You can choose from three groups:

*   **Students** – All students in the school linked to the Workplace site.
    
*   [**Staff**](https://help.verkada.com/guest/configuration-and-setup/manage-host-lists-in-guest)
     – All Workplace employees assigned to the site.
    
*   **Visitors (from Guest)** – All visitors signed in on the day the Response is launched.
    

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-response-templates#reunification)

Reunification

For K12 customers, enabling Reunification lets employees check in guardians and mark students as reunified. This adds a Reunified status for evacuees. Admins can also customize a Guardian Form to collect guardian information at check-in.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3922624211-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fn49pz7ZddUdVxNdz2EFE%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-2f69fcb500692de5c49da48c72258c5f6dcbd32d%252Fba6bbf045344b9a7311db27d223cf3d8da758064.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=38f11fcf&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-response-templates#person-statuses)

Person Statuses

Admins can define which statuses can be assigned to evacuees. If Reunification is enabled, a Reunified status will always be available.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3922624211-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fn49pz7ZddUdVxNdz2EFE%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-4e42d24522bc654ebea118704c0a66fbc2b2e235%252F2a990dd19725b6b5f0462426509dffcaa1581d8a.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bfe5b360&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-response-templates#location-names)

Location Names

Admins can define where evacuees and guardians (if Reunification is enabled) are expected to assemble.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3922624211-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fn49pz7ZddUdVxNdz2EFE%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-0cf1da1a1554d8772de2a01930aee8ec8786688c%252F7a65b5d40bb7b7db4a0c748e03ace7004c58dd73.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ec8eea84&sv=2)

Last updated 18 hours ago

# Prepare for a Command Connector Deployment | Command Connector | Verkada Help

[](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/hardware-installation/prepare-for-a-command-connector-deployment#prerequisites-and-planning)

Prerequisites and planning


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Are the cameras IP-based?**
    
    *   Analog cameras require an encoder to function (not recommended).
        
    
*   **Are cameras on the** [Hardware Compatibility List](https://www.verkada.com/security-cameras/command-connector/hcl)
    ?
    
    *   If not, verify they support ONVIF Profile S or RTSP.
        
    *   Use the [ONVIF Conformant Products](https://www.onvif.org/conformant-products/)
         tool to verify compatibility.
        
    
*   **Do you have complete camera specifications?**
    
    *   Camera type and model
        
    *   Megapixel resolution
        
    *   Encoding format
        
    *   Number of video feeds
        
    *   IP address and login credentials
        
    
*   **Where are the cameras connected?**
    
    *   Ideally, they should connect to the same network switch as the Command Connector.
        
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/hardware-installation/prepare-for-a-command-connector-deployment#device-requirements)

Device requirements


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/hardware-installation/prepare-for-a-command-connector-deployment#camera-capabilities)

Camera capabilities

*   **Encoding format**: Only H.264 streams are supported.
    
*   **Resolution**:
    
    *   **≤ 5MP**: Recommended for optimal performance.
        
    *   **8MP** = Supported, but reduces the number of cameras that can be connected per Command Connector.
        
    *   **\> 8MP** = May not be supported. Contact your Verkada Solutions Engineer for more information.
        
    
*   **Multisensor cameras**: Require one license per video stream.
    
*   **Login access**: Each camera must have a known IP address and admin credentials.
    

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/hardware-installation/prepare-for-a-command-connector-deployment#network-setup)

Network setup

*   Cameras must be on the same LAN as the Command Connector.
    
*   Avoid configurations where cameras are only accessible through an NVR’s internal switch.
    
*   IT resources:
    
    *   [Network Requirements](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/command-connector-network-settings)
        
    *   [Local Streaming](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/live-streaming/local-streaming-on-verkada-cameras)
        
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/hardware-installation/prepare-for-a-command-connector-deployment#sizing-and-licensing)

Sizing and licensing


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Collaborate with your Verkada Partner or Sales Rep to determine:

*   The number of Command Connectors required.
    
*   Whether camera retention settings align with expected video usage and storage needs.
    

One **LIC-CAM** license is required per video stream.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/hardware-installation/prepare-for-a-command-connector-deployment#physical-installation)

Physical installation


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each Command Connector is a 1RU rack-mount server and requires:

*   AC power
    
*   One network connection to the site switch
    
*   (Optional) Alternative mounting solutions are available from third-party suppliers.
    

Reference: [Command Connector Install Guide (PDF)](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/Verkada-CC300-500-700-Command-Connector-Install-Guide.pdf)
.

Last updated 1 day ago

Was this helpful?

# Get Started with Verkada Mailroom | Mailroom | Verkada Help

[Verkada Mailroom](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/mailroom-overview.pdf)
 enables your organization to quickly and securely manage packages that are delivered. Mailroom can also leverage camera feeds to allow you to see when a package was delivered, scanned, or picked up.

[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/get-started-with-verkada-mailroom#create-a-site)

Create a site


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sites are the logical way of grouping and managing devices within your Command organization. Site-level permissions make managing and viewing your devices easier. See [Mailroom Sites](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/configuration-and-setup/mailroom-sites)
 for more information on site creation and management.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/get-started-with-verkada-mailroom#configure-settings)

Configure settings

You can edit Mailroom settings at the organization level or site level. You can add pickup locations, add context cameras, manage multiple languages, etc, to make your Mailroom pickup experience easier. See [Mailroom Settings](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/configuration-and-setup/view-and-edit-mailroom-settings)
 for more information.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/get-started-with-verkada-mailroom#download-the-mailroom-app)

Download the Mailroom app

Verkada Mailroom allows you to use your existing phone or tablet without the need to purchase any additional devices. Download the Mailroom app from the [App Store](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/verkada-mailroom/id1631622141)
 or the [Google Play](https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.verkada.mailroom&hl=en&gl=US&pli=1)
 store.

[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/get-started-with-verkada-mailroom#supported-mailroom-carriers)

Supported Mailroom carriers


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada Mailroom supports a variety of mail carriers to streamline your experience. See [Supported Mailroom Carriers](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/configuration-and-setup/supported-mailroom-carriers)
 for more information.

[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/get-started-with-verkada-mailroom#licensing)

Licensing


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Every Mailroom site you manage in Command will need a license. Verkada licensing is applied for each Command organization, and the licenses co-term to a single expiration date. For more information on adding and managing licenses, see [Manage Your Licenses](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses)
.

[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/get-started-with-verkada-mailroom#check-network-settings)

Check network settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada Mailroom is designed to be plug-and-play. However, if your environment includes a firewall, you may need to make some configuration changes to get your Mailroom devices online. For more information on Mailroom network settings, see [Mailroom Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/mailroom-network-settings)
.

# Roles and Permissions for Mailroom | Mailroom | Verkada Help

This article describes the set of roles and associated permissions for Verkada Mailroom. For more information on roles and permissions for other Verkada product lines, see [Roles and Permissions for Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
.

*   **Site-level roles** determine the access a user or group has to devices in the site.
    
*   **Org-level roles** allow users or groups to manage permissions and devices at a global level.
    
*   **Permissions** are set using roles, which define the level of access users and groups have to devices and settings within an organization and its sites.
    

* * *

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/roles-and-permissions-for-mailroom#permissions-considerations)

Permissions considerations

*   Subsites inherit permissions from all parent sites, including the ultimate parent.
    
*   Users can belong to multiple groups. When roles conflict, the user receives the **highest role** granted directly or through any group.
    
*   Group-assigned roles can be manually upgraded but not downgraded. Remove the user from the group with the higher role to downgrade their access.
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/roles-and-permissions-for-mailroom#site-level-roles)

Site-level roles


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Site-level roles can be assigned to individual users or groups and are specific to a particular site. Subsites inherit the permissions from the parent sites above them.

Site Viewer[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/roles-and-permissions-for-mailroom#site-viewer)

*   View Mailroom logs and analytics.
    
*   Scan in delivered packages.
    
*   Search for packages delivered.
    
*   View context camera footage (if the user has the appropriate [camera permissions](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/roles-and-permissions-for-cameras)
    ).
    

Site Admin[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/roles-and-permissions-for-mailroom#site-admin)

*   Manage employees from site-specific employee lists.
    
*   Edit site-specific Mailroom Settings.
    
*   Add/edit cameras (only if the user has at least a Live-Only Viewer role for Cameras).
    
*   Add/edit doors (only if the user is an [Access Site Admin](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control)
    ).
    
*   View Mailroom logs and analytics.
    
*   Scan in delivered packages.
    
*   Search for packages delivered.
    
*   View context camera footage (if the user has the appropriate [camera permissions](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/roles-and-permissions-for-cameras)
    ).
    

[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/roles-and-permissions-for-mailroom#org-level-roles)

Org-level roles


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Org Admin[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/roles-and-permissions-for-mailroom#org-admin)

*   Assign/remove Workplace Site Admin role.
    
*   Assign/remove Workplace Site Viewer role.
    
*   Import and modify sites.
    
*   Manage employees from site-specific and organization-level employee lists.
    
*   Edit site-specific and organization-level Mailroom settings.
    
*   Add/edit cameras (if the user is at least a Live-Only Viewer for the cameras in the site).
    
*   View Mailroom logs and analytics.
    
*   Scan in delivered packages.
    
*   Search for packages delivered.
    
*   View context camera footage (if the user has the appropriate [camera permissions](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/roles-and-permissions-for-cameras)
    ).
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/roles-and-permissions-for-mailroom#set-permissions)

Set permissions


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can set site permissions for existing users and groups by managing user roles, groups, or sites.

Users[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/roles-and-permissions-for-mailroom#users)

In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .Under Org Settings, select Users.Select a user.At the top right, click Manage Roles.a. Set the needed permissions. b. Click Save.

Groups[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/roles-and-permissions-for-mailroom#groups)

In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .Under Org Settings, select Groups.Select a group.At the top, select Site Roles > Manage Roles.a. Set the needed permissions. b. Click Save.

Sites[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/roles-and-permissions-for-mailroom#sites)

In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .In the left navigation, select Sites.Select a site to manage and in the right pane, click Manage .a. In the top right, click Add to add a new user or group. b. Select an existing user or group to edit their permissions.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/roles-and-permissions-for-mailroom#faq)

FAQ


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

How do I grant Mailroom permissions but not Guest permissions, or vice versa?[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/roles-and-permissions-for-mailroom#how-do-i-grant-mailroom-permissions-but-not-guest-permissions-or-vice-versa)

To separate these permissions, make your Mailroom site and Guest site separate sites entirely. Guest and Mailroom sites imported from the same site will share the roles given to users. Learn more about [Roles and Permissions for Mailroom](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/roles-and-permissions-for-mailroom)
.

Can a Mailroom user get access to my cameras if they have "No Access" to the site in Command?[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/roles-and-permissions-for-mailroom#can-a-mailroom-user-get-access-to-my-cameras-if-they-have-no-access-to-the-site-in-command)

Mailroom users must have at least the Live-Only Viewer role for the cameras in the site to view the camera feeds in Mailroom.

What are the minimum permissions needed to see the Mailroom tab under All Products in Command?[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/roles-and-permissions-for-mailroom#what-are-the-minimum-permissions-needed-to-see-the-mailroom-tab-under-all-products-in-command)

Users must be at least a Site Viewer for 1 site to see the **Mailroom** tab under **All Products**.

What is the best role I should grant to my front desk receptionist?[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/roles-and-permissions-for-mailroom#what-is-the-best-role-i-should-grant-to-my-front-desk-receptionist)

It depends on the specific permissions you want to grant. In most scenarios, receptionists only need to be Site Viewers.

What access is needed to use the Mailroom app?[](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/roles-and-permissions-for-mailroom#what-access-is-needed-to-use-the-mailroom-app)

To use the Mailroom app to scan in packages, ensure that a user is at least a Site Viewer for the site(s) they need access to.

Last updated 1 day ago

Was this helpful?

# Set Up Your Viewing Station | Viewing Station | Verkada Help

The Verkada [Viewing Station](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/viewing-station-overview.pdf)
 is a plug-and-play device that streams multiple camera feeds simultaneously on a display with no local configuration required. It serves as a dedicated, admin-managed device with customizable layouts.

*   Supports up to 30 camera feeds per page
    
*   Supports up to 10 pages
    

You must be an **Org Admin** to claim and manage a Viewing Station.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/set-up-your-viewing-station#connect-your-viewing-station)

Connect your viewing station


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the box, you’ll find:

*   HDMI cable
    
*   Power cord
    
*   Viewing Station remote
    

You’ll need to provide an Ethernet cable. For network configuration details, see [Viewing Station Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/set-up-your-viewing-station)
.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/set-up-your-viewing-station#installation)

Installation

1

**Connect the power cord to the Viewing Station and plug it into a power source.**

2

**Connect one end of the HDMI cable to the Viewing Station and the other end to your display.**

3

**Connect an Ethernet cable from the Viewing Station to your network.**

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/set-up-your-viewing-station#claim-your-viewing-station)

Claim your viewing station


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/set-up-your-viewing-station#find-the-serial-number)

Find the serial number

There are two ways to find your Viewing Station’s serial number:

1

**On the device: When powered on, the serial number and a QR code appear on the display.**

2

**In Verkada Command:**

*   Go to **All Products > Devices** and select the Viewing Station.
    
*   The right panel displays details such as **Site**, **Location**, **Date Added**, **Serial Number**, **Model**, **Timezone**, and **Local IP**.
    

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/set-up-your-viewing-station#claim-the-device)

Claim the device

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Devices > Add Devices.**

2

**Enter or scan the Viewing Station’s serial number.**

3

**When prompted, claim and configure the device as needed.**

Once the VX52 is claimed, it’s ready to be configured and added to your organization’s layout.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/set-up-your-viewing-station#configure-your-viewing-station)

Configure your viewing station


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/set-up-your-viewing-station#find-your-viewing-station)

Find your viewing station

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Devices.**

2

**Filter the list to show Viewing Stations.**

3

**At the top right, select the arrow icon to begin configuration.**

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/set-up-your-viewing-station#edit-the-viewing-station-name)

Edit the viewing station name

1

**At the top left of the page, select the current name.**

2

**Enter a new, unique name.**

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/set-up-your-viewing-station#add-camera-tiles-and-smart-tiles)

Add camera tiles and Smart Tiles

You can add up to 10 pages and up to 30 live feeds per page.

1

**On the Viewing Station page, select Add Camera Tiles.**

2

**To display additional data, select Add Smart Tiles. Smart Tiles can show:**

*   The most active camera
    
*   The most recent access control event
    
*   Air quality or environmental sensor information
    

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/set-up-your-viewing-station#customize-the-layout)

Customize the layout

1

**Select Settings (gear icon) > Layout.**

2

**Choose your preferred display layout.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1530499399-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FfFkKNdIGPl0XHde4cZf7%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-74ce41d466d1203cc83effd9133c98a73828c18e%252F697768105502ec0b69d723597293bb8821984e8f.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=28866f2e&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/set-up-your-viewing-station#add-additional-pages)

Add additional pages

1

**Select the plus (+) icon.**

2

**You can create up to 10 pages, each supporting 30 live feeds.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1530499399-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FfFkKNdIGPl0XHde4cZf7%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-baf9e1eeb4f952768ec6abac63f9ca8e7a0d55d5%252F037f5febaca9c158848814a406fa358a31f1c807.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1f2b617b&sv=2)

Each page includes a **timer** that automatically cycles through different sets of cameras on your Viewing Station.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/set-up-your-viewing-station#configure-viewing-station-settings)

Configure viewing station settings


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Category**

**Settings**

**Description**

**Notifications**

Offline Notifications

Select which users should receive alerts when the viewing station goes offline.

**General**

Name

Edit your viewing station name.

Show Labels

If enabled, Viewing Station will show camera names.

Enable Cloud Streaming

Stream video through the cloud (only when video is unavailable on the local network). This option must be enabled to stream remote cameras.

Enable History Playback

Allows viewers to scrub through past footage with their Apple TV remote. Due to privacy concerns, some organizations choose to disable this feature, restricting their VX to display only live footage.

Test Offline Mode

Simulate a WAN outage on the viewing station to test offline connectivity.

Mute Audio

Mute the audio in camera video playback.

Global Banner

Create a text banner on every page on this Viewing Station.

Locale

Set the language on your Viewing Station.

Delete

Device will be removed from this organization.

**Intercoms**

Intercom Integrations

Select intercoms that will display video during an in-progress call.

[**Wi-Fi**](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/set-up-your-viewing-station#h_f283fae089)

Wi-Fi

Configure your viewing station to use Wi-Fi.

**Device**

General settings

View general device settings.

Copy Existing Viewing Station

Copy live feed configurations and Viewing Station settings from another Viewing Station in your organization.

Restart Viewing Station

The viewing station becomes unavailable for a few minutes while it restarts.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/set-up-your-viewing-station#configure-wi-fi)

Configure Wi-Fi

Wi-Fi support on the Viewing Station requires Verkada software version 2.2.0 (137) or higher. You can find the software version and serial number under **Settings > Device**.

1

**Connect the Viewing Station to a wired network and complete the setup process.**

2

**Once it is online via a wired network, enter the Wi-Fi Network Name (SSID).**

3

**Select the Security Type (WPA3, WPA2, WPA, WEP, or None).**

4

**Enter the Wi-Fi network Password, then click Save.**

**Note:** Hidden SSIDs are not supported.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1530499399-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FfFkKNdIGPl0XHde4cZf7%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-eade08960dae5235133c37c6ebc3ad02f5e306b7%252F9894a169ef95c64b46bbecff3d0c965ad16169be.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=22710d4d&sv=2)

5

**Wait 1–2 minutes and then power down the viewing station, disconnect the network cable, and power it back on. The viewing station should then connect to Wi-Fi and continue operating as usual.**

# Review Responses from Command | Incident Response | Verkada Help

In Command, you can manage active and historic Responses, review key metrics, track evacuees and guardians, and access a complete log of actions taken. These tools give Workplace Site Admins a central view to monitor and manage every stage of the Incident Response process.

You need at least Workplace Site Admin permissions to view the Analytics page.

* * *

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/review-responses-from-command#analytics)

Analytics

The **Analytics** page displays key metrics for each Response, including:

*   Evacuees updated by person type (Student, Staff, or Visitor)
    
*   Total number of evacuees by status
    
*   Total unique evacuees updated by each staff member
    

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3922624211-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fn49pz7ZddUdVxNdz2EFE%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-c089fa43d1900485235a6616bb90526b3ebedd0e%252F84e91c9f156ee4266f57674da82dfb1858721dea.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d4bc3683&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/review-responses-from-command#evacuees)

Evacuees

Workplace Site Admins can review the status and updates for all evacuees on the **Evacuees** page. Admins can filter the list of evacuees by status, location, as well as class section.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3922624211-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fn49pz7ZddUdVxNdz2EFE%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-632b3e064f8d1c3566bedabe747fdde349536348%252F9a4a196f24ee73de9abc931c750d246c2edcfc44.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=67af96d0&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/review-responses-from-command#guardians)

Guardians

Employees will see the **Guardians** page for Response Templates with Reunification enabled. This allows Workplace Site Admins to view all signed-in guardians and their details.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/review-responses-from-command#history)

History

The **History** page shows all actions taken in the Incident Response Portal for a single Response. Logs can be exported as a .json file from this page.

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Workplace Incident Response.**

2

**Select a Response.**

3

**At the top, select History.**

4

**In the top right, select Export logs.**

# Roles and Permissions for Air Quality Sensors | Air Quality | Verkada Help

This article describes the set of roles and associated permissions for Verkada [Air Quality Sensors](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
. For more information on roles and permissions for other Verkada product lines, see [Roles and Permissions for Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
.

*   **Site-level roles** determine the access a user or group has to devices in the site.
    
*   **Org-level roles** allow users or groups to manage permissions and devices at a global level.
    
*   **Permissions** are set using roles, which define the level of access users and groups have to devices and settings within an organization and its sites.
    

* * *

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/roles-and-permissions-for-air-quality-sensors#permissions-considerations)

Permissions considerations

*   Subsites inherit permissions from all parent sites, including the ultimate parent.
    
*   Users can belong to multiple groups. When roles conflict, the user receives the **highest role** granted directly or through any group.
    
*   Group-assigned roles can be manually upgraded but not downgraded. Remove the user from the group with the higher role to downgrade their access.
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/roles-and-permissions-for-air-quality-sensors#site-level-roles)

Site-level roles


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

No Access[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/roles-and-permissions-for-air-quality-sensors#no-access)

A No Access user **cannot** view air quality devices within a site.

Live-Only Viewer[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/roles-and-permissions-for-air-quality-sensors#live-only-viewer)

A Live-Only Viewer user **cannot** view air quality devices within a site.

Site Viewer[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/roles-and-permissions-for-air-quality-sensors#site-viewer)

*   View the sensors in the site
    
*   View analytics values for the sensors in the site
    
*   Toggle between different durations (live, today, this week, etc.)
    
*   View dashboards
    

Site Admin[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/roles-and-permissions-for-air-quality-sensors#site-admin)

For each category below, Site Admins can perform specific actions.

**Air Quality Sensors Home**

*   Add/remove devices.
    
*   Move devices between sites.
    
*   Set up (enable/disable) and edit triggers and their sensitivity values.
    
*   Reboot a device.
    
*   Set up offline notifications for the sensors in the sites they have access to.
    
*   Link a camera as a context camera to monitor events.
    
    **Note:** You must be a Site Admin for the site the camera is in.
    
*   Download a (comma-separated value) CSV file of the sensor data for any of the readings.
    
*   Enable live audio and recorded audio (for [SV25](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
    s that support audio recording and have this feature enabled).
    

**Dashboards**

*   Pair dashboards with a display.
    
*   Share the dashboard with other users.
    
*   Delete dashboards.
    
*   Edit tiles to view a time-series line graph.
    
*   Display sensor readings only.
    
*   View a single aggregated metric, a gauge, or a list of the readings’ values.
    
*   Delete tiles on the dashboard.
    
*   Choose the sensor to view on the dashboard.
    
*   Choose which sensor readings to display on each tile (for example, Temp/Vape Index/Humidity, and so on).
    
*   Choose the timescale (3 hrs or 24 hrs \[only two options available\]).
    
*   Adjust the thresholds for each of the selected values to set their own ranges for good, fair, and bad values.
    

**Analytics**

*   View the values and the sites where the Site Admin has access.
    
*   Sort filters to view specific readings, such as Temp/Vape Index/Humidity, and duration (weekly, daily, monthly).
    
*   Toggle between sites where the Site Admin has access.
    

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/roles-and-permissions-for-air-quality-sensors#org-level-roles)

Org-level roles


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Org Admin[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/roles-and-permissions-for-air-quality-sensors#org-admin)

The Org Admin must also be a Site Admin for the sites where the sensors are located.

*   Create and edit dashboards.
    
*   Enable/disable features for sensors (sensor audio, BACnet, calibration).
    
*   **Only role** that can calibrate sensors.
    
*   **Only role** that can create, edit, and remove dashboards.
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/roles-and-permissions-for-air-quality-sensors#set-permissions)

Set permissions


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can set site permissions for existing users and groups by managing user roles, groups, or sites.

You will have access to all cameras, viewing stations, air quality sensors, intercoms, gateways, New Alarms, and Command Connectors once you have been granted permissions for a site.

Users[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/roles-and-permissions-for-air-quality-sensors#users)

In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .UnderOrg Settings, select Users.Select a user.At the top right, click Manage Roles.a. Set the needed permissions. b. Click Save.

Groups[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/roles-and-permissions-for-air-quality-sensors#groups)

In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .UnderOrg Settings, select Groups.Select a group.At the top, select Site Roles > Manage Roles.a. Set the needed permissions. b. Click Save.

Sites[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/roles-and-permissions-for-air-quality-sensors#sites)

In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .In the left navigation, select Sites.Select a site to manage and in the right pane, click Manage .a. In the top right, click Add to add a new user or group. b. Select an existing user or group to edit their permissions.

Last updated 22 hours ago

Was this helpful?

5

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F287279980-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FNVCL5fLNdL5l9LkT0AR5%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-ff46f5d9339d58796923de030ff33e041218d56b%252Fb0eebacbd0485a0111cb9669d91ae0ecd65b24b2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9ef5124&sv=2)

# Command Connector Network Settings | Command Connector | Verkada Help

This article outlines the required network settings for your Command Connector to communicate with non-Verkada cameras and [Verkada Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
. For more information on the required network settings for other Verkada product lines, see [Required Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings)
.

The Command Connector has 2 RJ-45 Ethernet interfaces. Only **connect one** of the interfaces to your network for initial configuration. To configure both ports, see [Configure Two Ethernet Ports for Command Connector](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/configuration-and-setup/configure-two-ethernet-ports-for-command-connector)
.

[](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/command-connector-network-settings#ip-address)

IP address


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Command Connector must be assigned an IPv4 address to communicate on the LAN and with Verkada Command. The Command Connector obtains its IP address and network configurations using Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP).

The Command Connector has two ethernet interfaces. If you are using IP address reservations, it is recommended to configure two reservations—one for each Ethernet port.

[](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/command-connector-network-settings#domain-name-system)

Domain Name System


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Command Connectors use a DNS server to resolve Verkada’s fully qualified domain names (FQDN) to IP addresses to communicate with them. Your DHCP server tells the Command Connector where the DNS server is on the network, and it communicates using UDP port 53.

DNS over HTTPS (DoH) is currently not supported.

[](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/command-connector-network-settings#non-verkada-cameras)

Non-Verkada cameras


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Ensure that the Command Connector and non-Verkada cameras can communicate bi-directionally. If they are on separate or remote subnets, verify that routing works correctly in both directions. Note that dynamic NAT or Layer 3 (L3) translation is not supported between these devices.

Command Connector connects to non-Verkada cameras over the LAN using port 554 to pull RTSP streams, and port 80 or 8080 for ONVIF HTTP requests.

Verify these ports are allowed on the network:

*   **TCP+UDP ports 80, 8080, 443**: Enables the Command Connector to read and set camera parameters.
    
*   **TCP+UDP port 554**: Enables the Command Connector to ingest RTSP video streams from non-Verkada cameras.
    
*   **TCP+UDP Port 3702**: Enables WS-Discovery so the Command Connector can discover and connect to non-Verkada cameras over the LAN.
    

[](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/command-connector-network-settings#firewall-settings)

Firewall settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Command Connectors require access to many endpoints to ensure they can communicate with Command and all features will be accessible. Many customers may want to allow the Command Connector to communicate with the general required endpoints.

These are the general domains to allow, **applicable for all organizations**:

Copy

    34.216.15.26 - UDP/123 (Fallback NTP)
    *:4100 - TCP/UDP on LAN
    *.verkada.com - UDP/123 + TCP+UDP/443
    time.cloudflare.com - TCP/4460 + UDP/123
    *.amazonaws.com - TCP+UDP/443

If you prefer a more granular allowlist, you can add IP addresses, full FQDNs, and wildcard domains to your firewall rules based on the region where your devices are located.

Your region is selected when you [create an organization](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
 in Command.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/command-connector-network-settings#region-united-states)

Region: United States

Copy

    34.216.15.26 - UDP/123 (Fallback NTP)
    *:4100 - TCP/UDP on LAN (for local streaming)
    api.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api-ga.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    device.pyramid.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    firmware.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    index.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    time.control.verkada.com - UDP/123
    update.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vlogging.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443

# Get Started with Incident Response | Incident Response | Verkada Help

Incident Response helps organizations track the well-being and location of people during an incident. It enables organizations to account for employees and visitors, and allows schools to reunite students with their guardians.

Incident Response is only available in sites with Verkada Guest.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/get-started-with-incident-response#set-up-incident-response)

Set up Incident Response


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You need **Org Admin** permissions to configure Incident Response.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/get-started-with-incident-response#initial-site)

Initial site

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Workplace Incident Response.**

2

**Click Import Existing Guest Sites.**

3

**Select your site > Import Site.**

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/get-started-with-incident-response#additional-sites)

Additional sites

After setting up the first Workplace site for Incident Response, you can configure additional sites.

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Workplace Incident Response.**

2

**On the left navigation, click Incident Response Settings.**

3

**At the top, select Organization > Sites.**

4

**Click Import Site.**

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/get-started-with-incident-response#response-templates)

Response templates


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Workplace Site Admins can create Response Templates for different types of incidents. A Response Template defines:

*   Who needs to be accounted for as evacuees
    
*   What statuses can be assigned to evacuees
    
*   Where evacuees can be marked as present
    

For schools, configure the Response Template for Reunification and set up a Guardian Form.

See [Create Response Templates](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/create-response-templates)
 for more information.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/get-started-with-incident-response#workplace-employees)

Workplace Employees


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Employees assigned to an Incident Response site can take part in any active Response at that site. Employees are shared across all Workplace products (Guest, Mailroom, and Incident Response) for that site.

*   You need **Workplace Site Admins** to manage site-level employee lists.
    
*   You need **Org Admins** permissions to manage the organization-level employee list.
    

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Workplace Incident Response.**

2

**On the left navigation, click Incident Response Settings.**

3

**At the top, select Site > Employees.**

4

**Select Manage Employee List.**

See [Manage Host Lists in Guest](https://help.verkada.com/guest/configuration-and-setup/manage-host-lists-in-guest)
 for more information.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/get-started-with-incident-response#launch-a-response)

Launch a Response


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Only **Workplace Site Admins** can launch a Response.

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Workplace Incident Response.**

2

**On the Incident Response Home, click Launch Response.**

3

**Select a Response Template.**

4

**(Optional) Toggle on Drill mode to treat the Response as a drill.**

**Note:** If Drill mode is enabled, toggle on **Notify Staff** to send notifications with magic links to employees.

5

**Click Launch.**

When a Response is launched (Drill mode disabled), all employees will be sent notifications that include magic links to the [Incident Response portal](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/incident-response-portal)
.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3922624211-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fn49pz7ZddUdVxNdz2EFE%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-80eb931955c613ccbd9286b6a1cc67c55f4d3a9d%252F7a71e02311aa5330d387458c32ea839bfb9f90f4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6b59e4e7&sv=2)

At the beginning of a Response, all evacuees have a status and location of **Unknown**.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/incident-response/get-started-with-incident-response#end-a-response)

End a Response


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You need permissions **Workplace Site Admins** to end a Response.

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Workplace Incident Response.**

2

**On the Incident Response Home, click Active Response.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3922624211-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fn49pz7ZddUdVxNdz2EFE%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-08d26370f24e2030d89ddf46cecca217fe977375%252F71fbc94f4fb1839db5b4d5618af5f6c415d8d453.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=26f179a1&sv=2)

3

**In the top right, click End.**

4

**In the confirmation menu, select End Incident.**

Ending a Response locks further changes on the Incident Response portal. For non-Drill Responses, all employees are notified that the Response has ended.

Last updated 18 hours ago

Was this helpful?
