# Get Started with Verkada Classic Alarms | Classic Alarms | Verkada Help

This article is a guide for classic Alarms. Refer to this [article](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/getting-started-with-verkada-alarms)
 if you have new Alarms. See [New Alarms vs Classic Alarms](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/new-alarms-vs-classic-alarms)
 if you are unsure which version of Alarms you have.

* * *

Verkada [Alarms](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/alarms-professional-monitoring-overview.pdf)
, also known in the industry as _intrusion detection_ or simply _intrusion_, provide fully integrated, 24/7 professional monitoring with emergency dispatch services. You can use your existing Verkada devices without purchasing any additional hardware.

You need Org Admin and/or Site Admin [permissions](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
 for your Verkada Command organization to complete these actions.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/get-started-with-verkada-classic-alarms#what-you-need)

What you need

*   PoE-enabled switch or PoE injector
    
*   DHCP-enabled network
    
*   Cat5 or Cat6 cabling
    

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/get-started-with-verkada-classic-alarms#create-a-site)

Create a site


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sites are the logical way of grouping and managing devices within your Command organization. Site-level permissions make managing and viewing your devices easier. See [Alarms Sites](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/configuration-and-setup/classic-alarms-sites)
 for more information on site creation and management.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/get-started-with-verkada-classic-alarms#configure-settings)

Configure settings

The Alarms site settings page allows you to configure various settings, such as alarm triggers, arm/disarm schedules, alarm responses, and more. Each site’s settings can be uniquely configured to suit your security needs. See [Configure Alarms Site Settings](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/configuration-and-setup/configure-classic-alarms-site-settings)
 for more information.

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/get-started-with-verkada-classic-alarms#add-alarms-devices)

Add Alarms devices


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can add an Alarms device from the **Devices** page. See [Add a Device to Your Command Account](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/add-a-device-to-your-command-organization)
 for more information.

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/get-started-with-verkada-classic-alarms#licensing)

Licensing


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Most Alarms devices you manage in Command will need a license. Verkada licensing is applied for each Command organization, and the licenses co-term to a single expiration date. Your licenses may have been automatically added if you claimed your devices via order number. Otherwise, manually add the licenses from the Admin page. See [Manage Your Licenses](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses)
 for more information on adding and managing licenses.

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/get-started-with-verkada-classic-alarms#connect-your-alarms-devices)

Connect your Alarms devices


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

While Verkada Alarms devices are considered low-voltage devices that do not require a certified electrician to install, we strongly recommend you work with a system integrator or other professional for installation.

Please refer to the device [setup guide](https://www.verkada.com/docs/?product=alarms&contentType=setupGuide)
 for installation instructions.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/get-started-with-verkada-classic-alarms#powered-and-network)

Powered and network

The Alarms devices are powered in various ways.

*   The Alarms consoles, hub, and horn speaker use Power over Ethernet (PoE) for power and communication over the LAN. In most cases, these devices need to connect directly to a standard switch. PoE injectors can be used when a PoE switch is not available.
    
*   The Alarm panel is powered via AC power and connects to your network via Ethernet.
    
*   The wireless relay is powered via DC power.
    
*   The wireless Alarms devices are powered by CR123A lithium batteries.
    

For more information on power and network requirements, see the product [datasheet](https://www.verkada.com/docs/?product=alarms&contentType=datasheet)
.

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/get-started-with-verkada-classic-alarms#check-network-settings)

Check network settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada Alarms devices are designed to be plug-and-play. However, if your environment includes a firewall with custom rules and policies, you may need to make some configuration changes to get your devices connected to the cloud. See [Alarms Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/classic-alarms-network-settings)
 for more information.

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/get-started-with-verkada-classic-alarms#alarms-reports)

Alarms reports


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Reports allow you to easily gather information about your Alarms site. You can create reports for a variety of events, including device actions and video verifications. For more information on creating reports, see [Alarms Reports](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/networking-and-reports/alarms-reports)
.

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/get-started-with-verkada-classic-alarms#alarms-monitoring-certificate)

Alarms Monitoring Certificate


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

An Alarm Monitoring Certificate confirms that Verkada professionally monitors your alarm system and serves as proof for your insurance provider. See [Verkada Alarms Monitoring Certificate](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/alarms-specifications/verkada-alarms-monitoring-certificate)
 for more information. ​

Last updated 1 day ago

Was this helpful?

# Roles and Permissions for Intercom | Intercom | Verkada Help

This article describes the set of roles and associated permissions for [Verkada Intercom](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/get-started-with-verkada-intercom)
. For more information on roles and permissions for other Verkada product lines, see [Roles and Permissions for Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
.

*   **Site-level roles** determine the access a user or group has to devices in the site.
    
*   **Permissions** are set using roles, which define the level of access users and groups have to devices and settings within an organization and its sites.
    

* * *

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/roles-and-permissions-for-intercom#permissions-considerations)

Permissions considerations

*   Subsites inherit permissions from all parent sites, including the ultimate parent.
    
*   Users can belong to multiple groups. When roles conflict, the user receives the **highest role** granted directly or through any group.
    
*   Group-assigned roles can be manually upgraded but not downgraded. Remove the user from the group with the higher role to downgrade their access.
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/roles-and-permissions-for-intercom#site-level-roles)

Site-level roles


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada Intercom permissions determine who can receive calls, view intercom video, and unlock intercom doors. Intercom permissions depend on your site-level permissions and whether you’re configured as a Receiver.

You must be configured as a receiver to receive calls.

At a high level, these are the permissions granted to each level of Intercom devices:

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3022285914-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTH6kITd3Fb5UOnnsfQ9r%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-3c0d4d35489d7c354c25e790a8403f314714b5f4%252F6dd199e34e75c9300457af4e6fe86e544ec5e6d2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=72f3ae9e&sv=2)

Receiver[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/roles-and-permissions-for-intercom#receiver)

Verkada Intercom Receivers have the baseline receiver permissions. A user’s intercom permissions for a site are based on their baseline and site-level roles.

Receivers, such as Desk Stations and Session Initiation Protocol (SIP) phones\*\*,\*\* are not tied to a Verkada Command user. This means these receivers cannot be granted site-level permissions.

Regardless of their site-level permissions, a Receiver can:

*   Receive calls with video.
    
*   See 24/7 live intercom video, even if not on an active call.
    
*   Unlock the door both during and outside of a call.
    
*   Talk down to the intercom.
    

Live-View Only[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/roles-and-permissions-for-intercom#live-view-only)

*   Receive calls with video.
    
*   See 24/7 live intercom video, even if not on an active call.
    

Site Viewer[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/roles-and-permissions-for-intercom#site-viewer)

*   Receive calls with video.
    
*   See 24/7 live intercom video, even if not on an active call.
    
*   View historical video and events.
    

Site Admin[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/roles-and-permissions-for-intercom#site-admin)

*   Receive calls with video.
    
*   See 24/7 live intercom video, even if not on an active call.
    
*   View historical video and events.
    
*   Unlock the door both during and outside of a call.
    
*   Unlock the door 24/7.
    
*   Talk down to the intercom.
    
*   Change Receivers and device settings.
    

* * *

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/roles-and-permissions-for-intercom#verify-a-users-eligibility-to-receive-verkada-pass-calls)

Verify a user’s eligibility to receive Verkada Pass calls

Users configured as receivers can answer calls from the Pass app. To check their eligibility, hover over![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3022285914-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTH6kITd3Fb5UOnnsfQ9r%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-1025db08c5e6037ca1add97d01d61e290737f5f5%252F49ef4eb350f3daea087651a2bb2502c8dc5bd92e.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fb71d87c&sv=2) next to the user’s name in the receiver list.

*   A user who has **previously logged in** to Verkada Pass will see **Pass App**.
    
    ![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3022285914-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTH6kITd3Fb5UOnnsfQ9r%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-d4fbf243067696300febaaa88e549c1a9ae54270%252Fee0f927746019a9d211a636944976a26046fdc27.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=20715ca1&sv=2)
    
*   A user who has **never logged in** to the Verkada Pass will see **Send Pass App Invite**
    
    ![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3022285914-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTH6kITd3Fb5UOnnsfQ9r%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-3837a7e6d709232a65455d0640b85df88ac5691a%252F2496e67c27edda822836d16c93bbf9bb4e8c7a34.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f143d425&sv=2)
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/roles-and-permissions-for-intercom#set-permissions)

Set permissions


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can set site permissions for existing users and groups by managing user roles, groups, or sites.

You will have access to all cameras, viewing stations, air quality sensors, intercoms, gateways, New Alarms, and Command Connectors once you have been granted permissions for a site.

Users[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/roles-and-permissions-for-intercom#users)

In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .UnderOrg Settings, select Users.Select a user.At the top right, click Manage Roles.a. Set the needed permissions. b. Click Save.

Groups[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/roles-and-permissions-for-intercom#groups)

In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .UnderOrg Settings, select Groups.Select a group.At the top, select Site Roles > Manage Roles.a. Set the needed permissions. b. Click Save.

* * *

**Prefer to see it in action?** Check out the [video tutorial](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=SeBWHZAwCBg)
.

# Getting Started with Verkada Alarms | New Alarms | Verkada Help

This article is a guide for new Alarms. Refer to this [article](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/get-started-with-verkada-classic-alarms)
 if you have classic Alarms. See [New Alarms vs Classic Alarms](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/new-alarms-vs-classic-alarms)
 if you are unsure which version of Alarms you have.

* * *

Verkada Alarms, also known in the industry as _intrusion detection_ or simply _intrusion_, provides fully integrated, 24/7 professional monitoring with emergency dispatch services. You can use your existing Verkada devices without purchasing any additional hardware.

You need Org Admin and/or Site Admin [permissions](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
 for your Verkada Command organization to complete these actions.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/getting-started-with-verkada-alarms#what-you-need)

What you need

*   PoE-enabled switch or PoE injector (Cameras)
    
*   DHCP-enabled network
    
*   Cat5 or Cat6 cabling
    

[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/getting-started-with-verkada-alarms#create-a-site)

Create a site


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sites are the logical way of grouping and managing devices within your Command organization. Site-level permissions make managing and viewing your devices easier. See Alarms Sites for more information on site creation and management.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/getting-started-with-verkada-alarms#configure-settings)

Configure settings

The Alarms site settings page allows you to configure various settings, such as alarm triggers, arm/disarm schedules, alarm responses, and more. Each site’s settings can be uniquely configured to suit your security needs. See Configure Alarms Site Settings for more information.

[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/getting-started-with-verkada-alarms#add-alarms-devices)

Add Alarms devices


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can add serialized alarm devices (keypad, expander, etc.) from the alarm devices page you will need to change the view. Click the three horizontal lines located in the top right

[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/getting-started-with-verkada-alarms#licensing)

Licensing


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The cellular backup module is the only hardware device that requires a license. An Alarms license is required for each location that is monitored. Verkada licensing is applied for each Command organization, and the licenses co-term to a single expiration date. Your licenses may have been automatically added if you claimed your devices via order number. Otherwise, manually add the licenses from the Admin page. See [Manage Your Licenses](https://app.intercom.com/a/apps/q5re5q6g/articles/articles/6326326/show)
 for more information on adding and managing licenses.

[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/getting-started-with-verkada-alarms#connect-your-alarms-devices)

Connect your Alarms devices


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

While Verkada Alarms devices are considered low-voltage devices that do not require a certified electrician to install, we strongly recommend you work with a system integrator or other professional for installation.

Please refer to the device [setup guide](https://www.verkada.com/docs/?product=alarms&contentType=setupGuide)
 for installation instructions.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/getting-started-with-verkada-alarms#powered-and-network)

Powered and network

The alarm devices are powered in various ways.

*   The Alarms console requires DC power via the alarm panel and connects to your network via Ethernet.
    
*   The Alarm panel is powered via AC power and connects to your network via Ethernet.
    
*   The horn speaker uses Power over Ethernet (PoE) for power and communication over the LAN. In most cases, it needs to connect directly to a standard switch. PoE injectors can be used when a PoE switch is not available.
    
*   The wireless Alarms devices are powered by CR123A lithium batteries.
    

For more information on power and network requirements, see the product datasheet.

[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/getting-started-with-verkada-alarms#check-network-settings)

Check network settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada Alarms devices are designed to be plug-and-play. However, if your environment includes a firewall with custom rules and policies, you may need to make some configuration changes to get your devices connected to the cloud. See [Alarms Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/alarms-specifications/alarms-network-settings)
 for more information.

[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/getting-started-with-verkada-alarms#alarms-monitoring-certificate)

Alarms Monitoring Certificate


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

An Alarm Monitoring Certificate confirms that Verkada professionally monitors your alarm system and serves as proof for your insurance provider. See [Verkada Alarms Monitoring Certificate](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/alarms-specifications/verkada-alarms-monitoring-certificate)
 for more information. ​

Last updated 23 hours ago

Was this helpful?

# Access Control Network Settings | Access Control | Verkada Help

This article outlines the required network settings that your Verkada [access controllers](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/access-controllers-series-overview.pdf)
 need to communicate with [Verkada Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
. For more information on the required network settings for other Verkada product lines see [Required Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings)
.

Verkada devices are incompatible with LANs that require proxy servers or Secure Socket Layer (SSL)/Transport Layer Security (TLS) inspection. If either is in use, a bypass for all Verkada devices must be implemented for Verkada devices to communicate with Verkada Command.

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/access-control-network-settings#status-led)

Status LED


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

At the top left of the physical access controller, if you see a flashing blue [status LED](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/troubleshooting/verkada-ac41-status-led)
 this indicates that the access controller is not communicating with Command.

If you see this behavior:

*   Check that the network is set up correctly for the access controller.
    
*   See [Verkada Access Offline Operation](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/troubleshooting/verkada-access-offline-operation)
     to understand what the access system does when it cannot communicate with Command.
    

If the problem persists, contact [Verkada Support](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support)
.

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/access-control-network-settings#ip-address)

IP address


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Access controllers need an IPv4 address to communicate on the local area network (LAN) and to Command through the internet. Access controllers use Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP), UDP ports 67 and 68, to obtain their IP addresses and network configurations.

If you want to have a specific IP address on your access controller, set a DHCP reservation using the access controller’s [Media Access Control (MAC) address](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/hardware-installation/find-a-serial-number-and-mac-address)
 (found on the device’s label).

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/access-control-network-settings#domain-name-system)

Domain Name System


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Access Controllers use the DNS server to resolve Verkada’s fully qualified domain names (FQDN) to IP addresses to communicate with them. Your DHCP server tells the access controller where the DNS server is on the network and the access controller communicates using UDP port 53.

DNS over HTTPS (DoH) is currently not supported.

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/access-control-network-settings#power)

Power


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For specifics on power requirements, see the [access controller’s datasheet](https://www.verkada.com/docs/?product=accessControl&contentType=datasheet)
.

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/access-control-network-settings#firewall-settings)

Firewall settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada access controllers require access to many endpoints to ensure they can communicate with Command and all features will be accessible. Many customers may want to allow the access controllers to communicate with the general required endpoints.

These are the general domains to allow, **applicable for all organization-regions**:

Copy

    34.216.15.26 - UDP/123
    35.166.49.153 - UDP/123 + TCP+UDP/443
    *.verkada.com - UDP/123 + TCP+UDP/443

If you prefer a more granular allowlist, you can add both IP addresses and full FQDNs to your firewall rules based on the region where your devices are located.

Your region is selected when you [create an organization](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
 in Command.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/access-control-network-settings#region-united-states)

Region: United States

**Standard Verkada Endpoints**

Copy

    api.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api-ga.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP 443
    firmware.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    update.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.global-prod.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443

**NTP Endpoints**

Copy

    34.216.15.26 - UDP/123
    35.166.49.153 - UDP/123 + TCP+UDP/443
    time.control.verkada.com - UDP/123
    time.cloudflare.com - TCP/4460
    time.cloudflare.com - UDP/123

**Access Control Endpoints**

Copy

    access.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vcerberus.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/access-control-network-settings#region-europe)

Region: Europe

**Standard Verkada Endpoints**

Copy

    access.prod2.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.prod2.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api-ga.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP 443
    relay.prod2.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    update.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.global-prod.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.prod2.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vpeer-to-peer.prod2.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vinnout.prod2.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443

**NTP Endpoints**

Copy

    35.166.49.153 - UDP/123 + TCP+UDP/443
    time.control.verkada.com - UDP/123
    time.cloudflare.com - TCP/4460
    time.cloudflare.com - UDP/123

**Access Control Endpoints**

Copy

    access.prod2.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vcerberus.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/access-control-network-settings#region-australia)

Region: Australia

**Standard Verkada Endpoints**

Copy

    access.prod-ap-syd.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.prod-ap-syd.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api-ga.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP 443
    relay.prod-ap-syd.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    update.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.global-prod.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.prod-ap-syd.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vpeer-to-peer.prod-ap-syd.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vinnout.prod-ap-syd.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443

**NTP Endpoints**

Copy

    35.166.49.153 - UDP/123 + TCP+UDP/443
    time.control.verkada.com - UDP/123
    time.cloudflare.com - TCP/4460
    time.cloudflare.com - UDP/123

**Access Control Endpoints**

Copy

    access.prod-ap-syd.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vcerberus.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443

Use the [Verkada Network Tester](https://network-tester.support.verkada.com/)
 to verify your devices can connect to Verkada Command. Select your region and the **Access** product type to run the check.

The following endpoints must be allowed on your network for the test to work:

*   speed.cloudflare.com
    
*   network-tester.support.verkada.com

# Get Started with Verkada Intercom | Intercom | Verkada Help

Verkada’s intercom solution enables you to answer calls, grant entry, and secure entrances from anywhere.

**Required.** You need Org Admin and/or Site Admin [permissions](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
 for your Verkada Command organization to complete these actions.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/get-started-with-verkada-intercom#what-you-need)

What you need

*   PoE-enabled switch or PoE injector
    
*   DHCP-enabled network
    
*   Cat5 or Cat6 cabling
    

[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/get-started-with-verkada-intercom#create-a-site)

Create a site


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sites are the logical way of grouping and managing devices within your Command organization. Site-level permissions make managing and viewing your devices easier. See [Manage Your Sites and Subsites](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/manage-sites-and-subsites)
 for more information on site creation and management.

[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/get-started-with-verkada-intercom#add-an-intercom)

Add an intercom


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

At least one intercom needs to be added to Command before you can see the **Intercom** tab in the **All Products** menu. Intercoms can be added to Command from the **Devices** page. See [Add an Intercom to Your Site](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/configuration-and-setup/add-an-intercom-to-your-site)
 for more information.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/get-started-with-verkada-intercom#connect-a-door)

Connect a door

You can pair an existing access-controlled door or wire a door to the intercom that can be unlocked by an [intercom receiver](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/get-started-with-verkada-intercom#h_c6863790e9)
. See [Configure a TD52](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/configuration-and-setup/configure-a-td52)
 and [Wire a TD52 Video Intercom](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/configuration-and-setup/wire-a-video-intercom)
 for more information.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/get-started-with-verkada-intercom#configure-receivers)

Configure receivers

Receivers allow you to answer calls from an intercom and unlock any associated doors. See [Add and Configure Receivers in Intercom](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/configuration-and-setup/add-and-configure-receivers-in-intercom)
 for more information.

[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/get-started-with-verkada-intercom#licensing)

Licensing


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Every intercom you manage in Command will need a license. Verkada licensing is applied for each Command organization, and the licenses co-term to a single expiration date. Your licenses may have been automatically added if you claimed your devices via order number. Otherwise, manually add the licenses from the Admin page. See [Manage Your Licenses](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses)
 for more information on adding and managing licenses.

[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/get-started-with-verkada-intercom#connect-your-intercom)

Connect your intercom


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Recommendation**. While Verkada intercoms are considered low-voltage devices that do not require a certified electrician to install, we strongly recommend you work with a system integrator or other professional for installation.

Please refer to the intercom [setup guide](https://www.verkada.com/docs/?product=intercom&contentType=setupGuide)
 for instructions on mounting and wiring the door port.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/get-started-with-verkada-intercom#power-and-network)

Power and network

Verkada intercoms use Power over Ethernet (PoE) for power and communication over the LAN. In most cases, intercoms will connect directly to an 802.3af PoE standard switch. PoE injectors can be used when a PoE switch is not available. See the intercom’s [datasheet](https://www.verkada.com/docs/?product=intercom&contentType=datasheet)
 for more information.

[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/get-started-with-verkada-intercom#check-network-settings)

Check network settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada intercoms are designed to be plug-and-play. However, if your environment includes a firewall with custom rules and policies, you may need to make some configuration changes to get your access controllers connected to the cloud. See [Intercom Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/intercom-network-settings)
 for more information.

* * *

**Prefer to see it in action?** Check out the [video tutorial](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=O26przAa220)
.

# Get Started with Verkada Guest | Guest | Verkada Help

Verkada Guest enables your organization to quickly and securely manage guest access to your building and key areas. Guest leverages camera feeds and door events to track guests and hosts across your organization.

You need Org Admin and/or Site Admin [permissions](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
 for your Verkada Command organization to complete these actions.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/get-started-with-verkada-guest#what-you-need)

What you need

*   iPad on iOS 14 or higher
    
*   Badge printer
    
*   iPad stand (optional, but recommended for best Guest experience)
    

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/get-started-with-verkada-guest#create-a-site)

Create a site


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sites are the logical way of grouping and managing devices within your Command organization. Site-level permissions make managing and viewing your devices easier. See [Guest Sites](https://help.verkada.com/guest/configuration-and-setup/guest-sites)
 for more information on site creation and management.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/get-started-with-verkada-guest#configure-settings)

Configure settings

You can edit Guest settings at the organization level or site level. You can create Guest types, add cameras and doors to your sites, manage multiple languages, etc, to make your guest check-in experience easier. See [Guest Settings](https://help.verkada.com/guest/configuration-and-setup/view-and-edit-guest-settings)
 for more information.

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/get-started-with-verkada-guest#add-and-connect-guest-devices)

Add and connect Guest devices


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/get-started-with-verkada-guest#guest-tablet)

Guest tablet

Guest tablets are used to check in guests to your organization. You can add a tablet from the Guest site settings page. See [Set up a Guest Tablet](https://help.verkada.com/guest/configuration-and-setup/set-up-a-guest-tablet)
 for more information.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/get-started-with-verkada-guest#badge-printer)

Badge printer

Badge printers are used to print badges for your guests to wear while they are on your premises. You can add a badge printer from the Guest site settings page. See [Add a Printer to Verkada Guest](https://help.verkada.com/guest/configuration-and-setup/printers/brother-printer-setup-guide)
 for more information.

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/get-started-with-verkada-guest#licensing)

Licensing


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Every Guest tablet you manage in Command will need a license. Verkada licensing is applied for each Command organization, and the licenses co-term to a single expiration date. For more information on adding and managing licenses, see [Manage Your Licenses](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses)
.

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/get-started-with-verkada-guest#check-network-settings)

Check network settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada Guest is designed to be plug-and-play. However, if your environment includes a firewall, you may need to make some configuration changes to get your Guest devices online. See [Guest Network Setting](https://help.verkada.com/guest/guest-network-settings)
[**s**](https://help.verkada.com/guest/guest-network-settings)
 for more information.

For security screens to load properly in Guest from a computer, you should allowlist crimimages.com for TCP port 443 in any filtering device between the computer and your Internet Service Provider (ISP).

# Healthcare | Guest | Verkada Help

[Configure the Patient Visit Guest Type](https://help.verkada.com/guest/healthcare/configure-the-patient-visit-guest-type)
[Set up a Guest Tablet for Healthcare](https://help.verkada.com/guest/healthcare/set-up-a-guest-tablet-for-healthcare)

[Inpatient Visitor Sign-in](https://help.verkada.com/guest/healthcare/inpatient-visitor-sign-in)
[Manage Departments and Checkpoints](https://help.verkada.com/guest/healthcare/manage-departments-and-checkpoints)

# Roles and Permissions for New Alarms | New Alarms | Verkada Help

This article is a guide for New Alarms. Refer to this [article](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-classic-alarms)
 if you have classic Alarms. See [New Alarms vs Classic Alarms](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/new-alarms-vs-classic-alarms)
 if you are unsure which version of Alarms you have.

This article describes the set of roles and associated permissions for Verkada Alarms. For more information on roles and permissions for other Verkada product lines, see [Roles and Permissions for Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
.

*   **Site-level roles** determine the access a user or group has to devices in the site.
    
*   **Permissions** are set using roles, which define the level of access users and groups have to devices and settings within an organization and its sites.
    

* * *

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-new-alarms#permissions-considerations)

Permissions considerations

*   Subsites inherit permissions from all parent sites, including the ultimate parent.
    
*   Users can belong to multiple groups. When roles conflict, the user receives the **highest role** granted directly or through any group.
    
*   Group-assigned roles can be manually upgraded but not downgraded. Remove the user from the group with the higher role to downgrade their access.
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-new-alarms#new-alarms-roles)

New Alarms roles


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-new-alarms#arm-disarm)

Arm / Disarm

Users with this role can arm and disarm the site and resolve alarms through Command (web or mobile). They cannot access the alarm site configuration or other products unless explicitly granted permission.

This role is suited for users such as guards, cleaning staff, or contractors who need basic permissions to arm or disarm the alarm system without broader site or product access.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-new-alarms#unassigned)

Unassigned

This is the default role for users without an assigned New Alarms role. Users with this role cannot arm and disarm, access the alarm site configuration, or access other products.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-new-alarms#site-level-roles)

Site-level roles


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

No Access[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-new-alarms#no-access)

*   Cannot view the alarm site.
    
*   If added as a **response contact** for the alarm site, they can resolve an alarm and disarm the site through the incident link and agent call.
    

Site Viewer[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-new-alarms#site-viewer)

*   Cannot create or edit an alarm site.
    
*   Cannot arm or disarm alarm sites or resolve an alarm via Command.
    
*   Can view all alarm activity and event history with historical footage and live streams.
    
*   If added as a **response contact** for the alarm site, they can resolve an alarm and disarm the site through the incident link and agent call.
    

Site Admin[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-new-alarms#site-admin)

*   Can create or edit an alarm site.
    
*   Can create and edit keycodes along with all other alarm configurations.
    
*   Can arm or disarm alarm sites or resolve an alarm via Command.
    
*   Can add or remove Verkada devices and wired inputs/outputs on the site.
    
*   Can view all alarm activity and event history with historical video.
    
*   If added as a **response contact** for the alarm site, they can resolve an alarm and disarm the site through the incident link and agent call.
    

If a user is granted a **keycode** to the alarm site, they can arm or disarm the site and resolve an alarm via the keypad.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-new-alarms#set-permissions)

Set permissions


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You will have access to all cameras, viewing stations, air quality sensors, intercoms, gateways, New Alarms, and Command Connectors once you have been granted permissions for a site.

User[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-new-alarms#user)

1.  In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin ![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2Fq5re5q6g%2F1486870999%2F45308fafc2d4613daa8b2e50f802%2FScreenshot%2B2024-04-11%2Bat%2B10_49_58%25E2%2580%25AFAM.png%3Fexpires%3D1745388000%26signature%3Dadc8ee4008a88dbed98588be5a71a05c30176d978fc19ff1720bfa8b1e7e126a%26req%3DdSQvEMF5nYhWUPMW3Hu4gRH6C4wj8sPMsy1omMhZz9LkqOm09%252BcWpkMJ0rXo%250AQw%253D%253D%250A&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=20d08960&sv=2).
    
2.  Under![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2Fq5re5q6g%2F1488258786%2Fbfea6facb65e1cbe7142300986ce%2FScreenshot%252B2024-04-11%252Bat%252B10_49_58-E2-80-AFAM.png%3Fexpires%3D1745336400%26signature%3D97b6c7014329f46a270b4108105e8b7f39c894f12860e81c2df1f348cbd17db5%26req%3DdSQvHst7lYZXX%252FMU3HP0gJiLx0FTeXLfgq5wX6mb892cKMRzWgc%253D%250A&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=69a560c0&sv=2)Org Settings, select Users.

* * *

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-new-alarms#common-alarm-permission-configurations)

Common Alarm permission configurations

**Scenario**

**Role Configuration**

User requires full administrative control of the alarm site.

​For example, a Security Director, Facilities Manager.

Site Admin

User can view alarm incidents for investigation and arm or disarm the system through Command (web or mobile), but cannot modify the site configuration. ​ ​For example, a SOC team member.

Site Viewer + Arm/Disarm

User can only arm and disarm the site through Command (web or mobile) and has no access to the alarm site or other products within it.

For example, a guard, janitor, or contractor.

No access + Arm/Disarm

# Create a Command Organization | Command | Verkada Help

Verkada’s web software is Command. You need Command to interact with and monitor all of your Verkada devices.

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/create-a-command-organization#create-a-command-account)

Create a Command Account


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

**Navigate to the** [**Command**](https://command.verkada.com/)
 **home page.**

2

**Click Create a New Organization.**

3

**Enter your email and click Continue.**

4

**Enter your organization name and select a region to create your organization in.**

5

**Click Next to continue.**

6

**An organization short name will be automatically generated.**

**Note:** You can edit the short name to anything not already used by another Command account.

7

**Click Next to continue.**

8

**Select a data residency region for your organization.**

9

**Click Next to continue.**

10

**Enter the following user information:**

a. First Name b. Last Name c. Phone (optional) d. Create Password e. Confirm Password

11

**Click Submit to create your organization.**

* * *

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/create-a-command-organization#verify-your-email-address)

Verify your email address

You will need to verify your email address before you can access your Command account

1

**You will be brought to an overview page after you create your organization.**

2

**Click Next, and you will be prompted to check your inbox for a verification email.**

3

**From the email, click Verify Email.**

4

**A new web page will open confirming the email verification.**

5

**Click Continue to log in to your Command account.**

* * *

**Prefer to see it in action?** Check out the [video tutorial](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vme3YdOdhsE)
.

Last updated 22 hours ago

# Verkada Command System Requirements | Command | Verkada Help

You can use [Verkada Command](https://www.verkada.com/command/#overview)
 to interact with and monitor all of your Verkada devices. Command allows the ability to review video from cameras, monitor alarms and device events, configure your devices, and administrate your organization.

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/verkada-command-system-requirements#guidelines-for-using-verkada-command)

Guidelines for using Verkada Command


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To make sure your use of Verkada Command is secure and efficient, there are certain minimum system requirements and recommendations to consider and to ensure an optimal experience with Verkada Command.

We recommend regularly checking to make sure your setup meets or exceeds all of these criteria.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/verkada-command-system-requirements#recommended-compatible-browsers)

Recommended compatible browsers

Command is compatible with the latest versions of these browsers:

*   Google Chrome
    
*   Safari
    
*   Microsoft Edge
    
*   Mozilla Firefox
    

Ensure hardware acceleration is enabled for chromium-based browsers for best performance.

Other browsers might be able to load Command fully or partially, but this is the list of recommended browsers for an optimal experience.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/verkada-command-system-requirements#recommended-compatible-operating-systems)

Recommended compatible operating systems

*   **Windows**: Windows 10 or later
    
*   **Mac**: MacOS 10.12 (Monterrey) or later
    

For newer Apple Mac models using the M series processors, all will be compatible with Command.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/verkada-command-system-requirements#required-endpoints-and-ports)

Required endpoints and ports

To allow Command to load from a computer, you should allowlist the parent domain `*.verkada.com` for TCP port 443 in any filtering device between the computer and your Internet Service Provider (ISP).

We recommend allowlisting these domains:

Copy

    verkada.com
    *.verkada.com
    *.*.verkada.com
    *.command.verkada.com

For logging purposes, which help us improve the Command experience, we recommend allowlisting these domains:

Copy

    *.datadoghq.com
    *.browser-intake-datadoghq.com

Verkada devices have their own set of [required network settings](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings)
, and certain functions in Command, such as [local streaming](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/live-streaming/local-streaming-on-verkada-cameras)
 require communication between the computer and the Verkada device.

Last updated 1 day ago

# Get Started with Verkada Access Control | Access Control | Verkada Help

Verkada’s access control solution enables you to manage access user permissions and monitor entry points with features such as remote unlock and real-time alerts.

You need Org Admin and/or Access Site Admin [permissions](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
 for your Verkada Command organization to complete these actions.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/get-started-with-verkada-access-control#what-you-need)

What you need

*   DHCP-enabled network
    
*   Cat5 or Cat6 cabling
    

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/get-started-with-verkada-access-control#create-a-site)

Create a site


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sites are the logical way of grouping and managing devices within your Command organization. Site-level permissions make managing and viewing your devices easier. See [Manage Your Sites and Subsites](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/manage-sites-and-subsites)
 for more information on site creation and management.

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/get-started-with-verkada-access-control#add-an-access-controller)

Add an access controller


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

At least one access controller needs to be added to Command before you can see the **Access** tab in the **All Products** menu. Access controllers can be added from the **Devices** page. See [Add an Access Controller to Command](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/configuration-and-setup/add-an-access-controller-to-command)
 for more information.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/get-started-with-verkada-access-control#configure-a-door)

Configure a door

Doors are the configuration and components connected to a Verkada access controller cassette, including a lock, reader, door position indicator (DPI), and request to exit (REX). See [Configure a Door in Command](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/configuration-and-setup/configure-a-door-in-command)
 for more information on configuring door ports.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/get-started-with-verkada-access-control#configure-an-aux-output)

Configure an AUX output

The AUX port on an access controller is used to connect external devices, such as exit buttons, to enhance the functionality of your access control system. See [Configure an AUX Output on an Access Controller](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/configuration-and-setup/configure-an-aux-output-on-an-access-controller)
 for more information on configuring an AUX port.

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/get-started-with-verkada-access-control#add-access-users)

Add access users


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You need to add access users and assign them access credentials before they can unlock a door in your organization. We currently support badge-in, remote unlock, Bluetooth unlock, and web unlock credentials. See [Add a User to the Verkada Access System](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/configuration-and-setup/add-a-user-to-the-verkada-access-system)
 for more information.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/get-started-with-verkada-access-control#access-groups)

Access groups

Access groups are used to group together users who need to have the same permissions to access a door. You cannot badge into a door unless you are in an access group with at least one [access level](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/get-started-with-verkada-access-control#h_b1fa994097)
 associated. See [Add and Modify Access Groups](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/configuration-and-setup/add-and-modify-access-groups)
 for more information.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/get-started-with-verkada-access-control#access-levels)

Access levels

Access levels are schedules that define when users in an access group can access a door. A door needs to be assigned to an access level, and the access level needs to be assigned to an [access group](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/get-started-with-verkada-access-control#h_b1fa994097)
. See [Add and Modify Access Levels](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/configuration-and-setup/add-and-modify-access-levels)
 for more information.

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/get-started-with-verkada-access-control#licensing)

Licensing


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Every access controlled door you manage in Command needs a license. Verkada licensing is applied for each Command organization, and the licenses co-term on a single expiration date. Your licenses may have been automatically added if you claimed your devices via order number. Otherwise, manually add the licenses from the Admin page. See [Manage Your Licenses](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses)
 for more information on adding and managing licenses.

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/get-started-with-verkada-access-control#connect-your-access-controller)

Connect your access controller


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

While Verkada access controllers are considered low-voltage devices that do not require a certified electrician to install, we strongly recommend you work with a system integrator or other professional for installation.

Refer to the door controller’s [setup guide](https://www.verkada.com/docs/?product=accessControl&contentType=setupGuide)
 for mounting and wiring instructions.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/get-started-with-verkada-access-control#power-and-network)

Power and network

Most Verkada access controllers are powered via AC power and connect to your network via Ethernet. The one-door controllers can be powered via PoE or DC power. See the controller’s [datasheet](https://www.verkada.com/docs/?product=accessControl&contentType=datasheet)
 for the power and network requirements of your specific access controller model.

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/get-started-with-verkada-access-control#check-network-settings)

Check network settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada access controllers are designed to be plug-and-play. However, if your environment includes a firewall with custom rules and policies, you may need to make some configuration changes to get your access controllers connected to the cloud. See [Access Control Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/access-control-network-settings)
 for more information.

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/get-started-with-verkada-access-control#configure-alerts)

Configure alerts


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada Command allows you to receive push, email, and SMS alerts for events generated in your organization. The ![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F134288481-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaaHs5RfKqv9Z49mi02cC%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-91bd70c6d63692bdc09cfe2b790499421775da49%252F05283db7c21547b9b9a924fe0723bd14f6720315.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b3179c5e&sv=2) in the bottom left of Command takes you to the **Alerts** page where you can set up and manage alerts. Access events include door events, controller events, lockdown triggered events, and more. See [Configure Access Control Event Alerts](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/alerts-and-events/configure-access-control-event-alerts)
 for more information about access events and creating alerts.

Last updated 1 day ago

Was this helpful?

# Get Started with Verkada Command | Command | Verkada Help

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command#create-a-command-account)

Create a Command account


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada’s web software is called Command. Command is the platform used to interact with and monitor all of your Verkada devices. See [Create a Command Account](https://help.verkada.com/command/create-a-command-organization)
 for more information.

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command#organization-settings)

Organization settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Org Admins will have access to the **Admin** page, where they can manage org-wide settings and configurations. These include managing users, accessing the audit log, licensing, and support access. See [Manage Your Admin Page Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command/organization-wide-settings/manage-your-admin-page-settings)
 for more information.

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command#add-devices)

Add devices


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Org Admins need to add devices to Command before you can access and manage them. Add devices from the **Devices** page or directly from the site for some product lines. See [Add a Device to Your Command Account](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/add-a-device-to-your-command-organization)
 for more information.

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command#licensing)

Licensing


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Most Verkada devices managed in Command will need a license. Licenses are managed from the [Manage Licenses](https://command.verkada.com/admin/org-settings/license-manager?tab=productLicenses)
 page. Verkada licensing is applied for each Command organization, and the licenses co-term to a single expiration date. Your licenses may have been automatically added if you claimed your devices via order number. Otherwise, manually add the licenses from the Admin page. See [Manage Your Licenses](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses)
 for more information on adding and managing licenses.

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command#add-users)

Add users


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Your Verkada Command software license includes unlimited users. See [Manage Users in Your Organization](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/manage-users-in-your-organization)
 for more information.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command#permissions)

Permissions

Assign different permission levels to users in your organization based on your organization’s security needs. Permissions can be assigned at the org level and the site level for each product line to give each user the exact amount of access they need. See [Roles and Permissions for Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
 for more information.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command#single-sign-on-sso)

Single Sign-On (SSO)

SSO allows you to log in using a third-party authentication service, such as Okta, Microsoft Entra ID, G Suite, etc. This method provides a single point of management for authentication across multiple applications, including Verkada Command. See [Single Sign-On (SSO)](https://help.verkada.com/command/single-sign-on-sso)
 for more information.

Verkada recommends enabling OIDC instead of SAML when available.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command#scim)

SCIM

SCIM allows you to sync users and groups from your IdP management software Verkada Command. This enables you to manage users and permission groups easily. See our [SCIM/SSO](https://help.verkada.com/command/third-party-user-provisioning)
 section of the knowledge base for more information.

* * *

**Prefer to see it in action?** Check out the [video tutorial](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QwSngXrWUoc)
.

# Roles and Permissions for Guest | Guest | Verkada Help

This article describes the set of roles and associated permissions for Verkada Guest. For more information on roles and permissions for other Verkada product lines, see [Roles and Permissions for Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
.

*   **Site-level roles** determine the access a user or group has to devices in the site.
    
*   **Org-level roles** allow users or groups to manage permissions and devices at a global level.
    
*   **Permissions** are set using roles, which define the level of access users and groups have to devices and settings within an organization and its sites.
    

* * *

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/roles-and-permissions-for-guest#permissions-considerations)

Permissions considerations

*   Subsites inherit permissions from all parent sites, including the ultimate parent.
    
*   Users can belong to multiple groups. When roles conflict, the user receives the **highest role** granted directly or through any group.
    
*   Group-assigned roles can be manually upgraded but not downgraded. Remove the user from the group with the higher role to downgrade their access.
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/roles-and-permissions-for-guest#site-level-roles)

Site-level roles


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Site-level roles can be assigned to individual users or groups and are specific to a particular site. Subsites inherit the permissions from the parent sites above them.

At a high level, these are the permissions granted to each Guest user:

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1436127735-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FZyuELZr7uIcXX3WnjX0N%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-1da0e5a6bae0e4466bcdc4703f3bc0230bdc52b9%252F6654bcf38f2ee2449738e300ec093aaca9dd4038.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d02603be&sv=2)

Site Viewer[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/roles-and-permissions-for-guest#site-viewer)

*   View guest logs and analytics.
    
*   Sign out users and print badges.
    
*   View and open doors (if the user has the appropriate [access control permissions](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/configuration-and-setup/assign-a-user-access-to-a-door)
    ).
    
*   View context camera footage (if the user has the appropriate [camera permissions](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/roles-and-permissions-for-cameras)
    ).
    

Site Admin[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/roles-and-permissions-for-guest#site-admin)

*   Manage employees from site-specific employee lists.
    
*   Edit site-specific Guest Settings.
    
*   Add/edit cameras (only if the user has at least a Live-Only Viewer role for Cameras).
    
*   Add/edit doors (only if the user is an [Access Site Admin](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control)
    ).
    
*   View guest logs and analytics.
    
*   Sign out users and print badges.
    
*   View and open doors (if the user has the appropriate [access control permissions](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/configuration-and-setup/assign-a-user-access-to-a-door)
    ).
    
*   View context camera footage (if the user has the appropriate [camera permissions](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/roles-and-permissions-for-cameras)
    ).
    

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/roles-and-permissions-for-guest#org-level-roles)

Org-level roles


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Org Admin[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/roles-and-permissions-for-guest#org-admin)

*   Assign/remove Workplace Site Admin role.
    
*   Assign/remove Workplace Site Viewer role.
    
*   Import and modify sites.
    
*   Manage employees from site-specific and organization-level employee lists.
    
*   Edit site-specific and organization-level Guest Settings.
    
*   Add/edit cameras (if the user is at least a Live-Only Viewer for the cameras in the site).
    
*   Add/edit doors (only if the user is an [Access Site Admin](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control)
    ).
    
*   View guest logs and analytics.
    
*   Sign out users and print badges.
    
*   View and open doors (if the user has the appropriate [access control permissions](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/configuration-and-setup/assign-a-user-access-to-a-door)
    ).
    
*   View context camera footage (if the user has the appropriate [camera permissions](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/roles-and-permissions-for-cameras)
    ).
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/roles-and-permissions-for-guest#set-permissions)

Set permissions


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can set site permissions for existing users and groups by managing user roles, groups, or sites.

Users[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/roles-and-permissions-for-guest#users)

In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .Under Org Settings, select Users.Select a user.At the top right, click Manage Roles.a. Set the needed permissions. b. Click Save.

Groups[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/roles-and-permissions-for-guest#groups)

In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .Under Org Settings, select Groups.Select a group.At the top, select Site Roles > Manage Roles.a. Set the needed permissions. b. Click Save.

Sites[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/roles-and-permissions-for-guest#sites)

In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .In the left navigation, select Sites.Select a site to manage and in the right pane, click Manage .a. In the top right, click Add to add a new user or group. b. Select an existing user or group to edit their permissions.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/roles-and-permissions-for-guest#faq)

FAQ


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

How do I grant Mailroom permissions but not Guest permissions, or vice versa?[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/roles-and-permissions-for-guest#how-do-i-grant-mailroom-permissions-but-not-guest-permissions-or-vice-versa)

To separate these permissions, make your Mailroom site and Guest site different sites entirely. Guest and Mailroom sites that are imported from the same site will share roles given to users. Learn more about [Roles and Permissions for Mailroom](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/roles-and-permissions-for-mailroom)
.

Can a Guest user get access to my cameras if they have "No Access" to the site in Command?[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/roles-and-permissions-for-guest#can-a-guest-user-get-access-to-my-cameras-if-they-have-no-access-to-the-site-in-command)

Guest users must at least have the Live-Only Viewer role for the cameras in the site to view the camera feeds in Guest.

What are the minimum permissions needed to see the Guest tab under All Products in Command?[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/roles-and-permissions-for-guest#what-are-the-minimum-permissions-needed-to-see-the-guest-tab-under-all-products-in-command)

Users must be at least a Site Viewer for 1 site to see the Guest tab under **All Products**.

What is the best role I should grant to my front desk receptionist?[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/roles-and-permissions-for-guest#what-is-the-best-role-i-should-grant-to-my-front-desk-receptionist)

It depends on the specific permissions you want to grant. In most scenarios, receptionists only need to be Site Viewers.

* * *

**Prefer to see it in action?** Check out the [video tutorial](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=byXR4aAmjfU)
.

Last updated 1 day ago

# Guest Network Settings | Guest | Verkada Help

This article outlines the required network settings that your [Verkada Guest](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/verkada-guest-quick-start-guide.pdf)
 tablets and phones need to be able to communicate with the printer through the LAN and speak with [Verkada Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
. For more information on the required network settings for other Verkada product lines see [Required Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings)
.

**Note**: Verkada devices are incompatible with LANs that require proxy servers or Secure Socket Layer (SSL)/Transport Layer Security (TLS) inspection. If either is in use, a bypass for all Verkada devices must be implemented for Verkada devices to communicate with Verkada Command.

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/guest-network-settings#ip-address)

IP address


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Guest tablets and phones must be assigned an IPv4 address to communicate on the LAN and to Verkada Command. Guest devices use Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP) and User Datagram Protocol (UDP) to obtain their IP addresses and network configurations.

If you require your Guest device to have a specific IP address, create a DHCP reservation using the device’s Media Access Control (MAC) address (found on the device’s label).

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/guest-network-settings#domain-name-system)

Domain Name System


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Guest tablets and phones use the DNS server to resolve Verkada’s fully qualified domain names (FQDN) to IP addresses to communicate with them. Your DHCP server tells the Guest device where the DNS server is on the network and the Guest device communicates using UDP port 53.

**Note**: DNS over HTTPS (DoH) is currently not supported.

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/guest-network-settings#firewall-settings)

Firewall settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Guest tablets and phones require access to many endpoints to ensure they can communicate with Command and all features will be accessible. Many customers may want to allow the Guest devices to communicate with the general required endpoints.

These are the general domains to allow, **applicable for all organization-regions**:

Copy

    34.216.15.26 - UDP/123
    34.203.250.0/23 - UDP/10000-20000
    35.156.191.128/25 - UDP/10000-20000
    52.215.127.0/24 - UDP/10000-20000
    54.65.63.192/26 - UDP/10000-20000
    54.169.127.128/26 - UDP/10000-20000
    54.171.127.192/26 - UDP/10000-20000
    54.172.60.0/23 - UDP/10000-20000
    54.244.51.0/24 - UDP/1024-65535
    168.86.128.0/18 - UDP/10000 - 60000
    54.252.254.64/26 - UDP/10000-20000
    177.71.206.192/26 - UDP/10000-20000
    *.verkada.com - UDP/123 + TCP+UDP/443

If you prefer a more granular allowlist, you can add IP addresses, full FQDNs, and wildcard domains to your firewall rules based on the region where your devices are located.

Your region is selected when you [create an organization](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
 in Command.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/guest-network-settings#region-united-states)

**Region: United States**

Copy

    34.216.15.26 - UDP/123
    3.235.111.128/25 - UDP/10000-60000 + TCP+UDP/443 + UDP/3478

# Intercom Network Settings | Intercom | Verkada Help

This article outlines the required network settings that your Verkada [Intercom](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/video-intercom-overview.pdf)
 needs to communicate with [Verkada Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
. For more information on the required network settings for other Verkada product lines see [Required Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings)
.

Verkada devices are incompatible with LANs that require proxy servers or Secure Socket Layer (SSL)/Transport Layer Security (TLS) inspection. If either is in use, a bypass for all Verkada devices must be implemented for Verkada devices to communicate with Verkada Command.

[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/intercom-network-settings#status-led)

Status LED


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A flashing blue [status LED](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/configuration-and-setup/td52-status-leds)
 on the top of the intercom indicates the intercom is not communicating with Command. If you see this behavior, check that the network is set up correctly with the intercom’s requirements. If the problem persists, contact [Verkada Support](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support)
.

[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/intercom-network-settings#ip-address)

IP address


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Intercoms must be assigned an IPv4 address to communicate on the LAN and to Verkada Command. Intercoms use Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP) and User Datagram Protocol (UDP) to obtain their IP addresses and network configurations.

If you require your intercom to have a specific IP address, create a DHCP reservation using the device’s Media Access Control (MAC) address (found on the device’s label).

Verkada intercoms respond to ICMP ping requests.

[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/intercom-network-settings#domain-name-system)

Domain Name System


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Intercoms use the DNS server to resolve Verkada’s fully qualified domain names (FQDN) to IP addresses to communicate with them. Your DHCP server tells the intercom where the DNS server is on the network and the intercom communicates using UDP port 53.

DNS over HTTPS (DoH) is currently not supported.

[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/intercom-network-settings#power)

Power


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Intercoms are powered through Power over Ethernet (PoE). This means the network switch needs to provide power to the intercom, or a PoE injector needs to be utilized. For specifics on power requirements, see the [Intercom datasheet](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/video-intercom-overview.pdf)
.

[](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/intercom-network-settings#firewall-settings)

Firewall settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Intercoms require access to many endpoints to ensure they can communicate with Command and all features will be accessible. Many customers may want to allow the intercoms to communicate with the general required endpoints.

These are the general domains to allow, **applicable for all organization-regions**:

**Mandatory:**

Copy

    *.amazonaws.com - TCP+UDP/443, UDP/1024 to 65535
    *.twilio.com - TCP+UDP/443, 5060, 5061
    *.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443, UDP/123
    *:4100 - TCP/UDP on LAN
    34.216.15.26 - UDP/123
    35.166.49.153 - TCP+UDP/443, UDP/123
    168.86.128.0/18 - UDP/1024 to 65535
    time.cloudflare.com - TCP/4460 + UDP/123
    *.livekit.cloud - TCP/443, UDP/50000 to 60000
    *.turn.livekit.cloud - TCP/443, UDP/50000 to 60000
    *.host.livekit.cloud - UDP/3478, UDP/50000 to 60000

LiveKit enables high quality, low latency video and audio streaming with Verkada intercoms.

If you prefer a more granular allowlist, you can add IP addresses, full FQDNs, and wildcard domains to your firewall rules based on the region where your devices are located.

Your region is selected when you [create an organization](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
 in Command.
