# Required Network Settings | Command | Verkada Help

Verkada devices need to communicate with [Verkada Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
, and they use the network they are connected to to do this. In most cases, minimal updates to your network settings are needed. Additional configuration may be required for complex or highly secure networks.

Use the [Verkada Network Tester](https://network-tester.support.verkada.com/)
 to verify your devices can connect to Verkada Command. Select your region and product type to run the check.

The following endpoints must be allowed on your network for the test to work:

*   speed.cloudflare.com
    
*   network-tester.support.verkada.com
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings#device-specific-network-settings)

Device-specific network settings


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each device type has required domains to allow them to properly operate on the network. Select a product from the list below for more information on its required network settings.

*   [Access Control Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/access-control-network-settings)
    
*   [Air Quality Sensor Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/air-quality-sensor-network-settings)
    
*   [Alarms Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/alarms-specifications/alarms-network-settings)
    
*   [Camera Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/camera-specifications/camera-network-settings)
    
*   [Classic Alarms Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/classic-alarms-network-settings)
    
*   [Command Connector Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/command-connector-network-settings)
    
*   [Gateway Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/gateways-network-settings)
    
*   [Guest Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/guest/guest-network-settings)
    
*   [Intercom Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/intercom/intercom-network-settings)
    
*   [Mailroom Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/mailroom/mailroom-network-settings)
    
*   [Viewing Station Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/viewing-station/viewing-station-network-settings)
    

Some firewalls do not allow wildcards (\*), so you may need to allow each endpoint individually.

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings#compatibility)

Compatibility


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada devices are incompatible with local area networks (LANs) that require proxy servers or Secure Socket Layer (SSL)/Transport Layer Security (TLS) inspection. If either is in use, a bypass for all Verkada devices must be implemented for your Verkada devices to communicate with Verkada Command.

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings#ip-address)

IP address


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada devices must be assigned an IPv4 address to communicate on the LAN and to Verkada Command through the internet. By default, all Verkada devices use Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP) and User Datagram Protocol (UDP) to obtain their IP addresses and network configurations.

If you require your device to have a specific IP address, create a DHCP reservation using the device’s Media Access Control (MAC) address (found on the device’s label). You can also set up [static IP addresses](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/hardware-installation/advanced-installation/configure-static-ip-addresses-for-cameras)
 in Command for cameras.

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings#domain-name-system)

Domain Name System


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada devices use the Domain Name System (DNS) server to resolve Verkada’s fully qualified domain names (FQDN) to IP addresses to communicate with them. Your DHCP server tells the Verkada device where the DNS server is on the network and the device communicates using UDP port 53.

**Note**: DNS over HTTPS (DoH) is currently not supported.

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings#power)

Power


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Most Verkada devices are powered through Power over Ethernet (PoE). You can use the product [datasheets](https://www.verkada.com/docs/?contentType=datasheet)
 to figure out the power requirements for your Verkada devices.

These are the most common power requirements:

*   IEE 802.3af, Type 1 PoE
    
*   IEEE 802.3at, Type 2 PoE+
    
*   IEEE 802.3bt, Type 3 PoE++
    
*   100–240 VAC, 50/60 Hz
    

Last updated 1 day ago

# Get Started with Verkada Security Cameras | Verkada Cameras | Verkada Help

Verkada security cameras offer comprehensive video surveillance solutions and deliver reliable monitoring capabilities for enhanced safety and security.

You need Org Admin and/or Site Admin [permissions](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
 for your Verkada Command organization to complete these actions.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/get-started-with-verkada-security-cameras#what-you-need)

What you need

*   PoE-enabled switch or PoE injector
    
*   DHCP-enabled network
    
*   Cat5 or Cat6 cabling
    

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/get-started-with-verkada-security-cameras#create-a-site)

Create a site


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sites are the logical way of grouping and managing devices within your Command organization. Site-level permissions make managing and viewing your devices easier. See [Manage Your Sites and Subsites](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/manage-sites-and-subsites)
 for more information on site creation and management.

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/get-started-with-verkada-security-cameras#add-a-camera)

Add a camera


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Cameras can be added from the **Devices** page or directly from a site. You can see a camera’s video stream once you’ve added it to Command and connected it to the internet. See [Add a Device to Your Command Account](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/add-a-device-to-your-command-organization)
 for more information.

Only footage recorded after a camera is added to Command will be accessible. Please ensure that the camera is successfully added to Command before you connect the camera. If you cannot add a camera, contact [Verkada Support](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support)
.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/get-started-with-verkada-security-cameras#configure-settings)

Configure settings

You can edit general settings from a camera’s settings page to make the camera more recognizable, such as changing the name and location. You can also enable more advanced settings, such as cloud backup, audio, etc., to better suit your security needs. See [View and Edit Camera Settings](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/view-and-edit-camera-settings)
 for more information on configuring camera settings.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/get-started-with-verkada-security-cameras#analytics)

Analytics

Most Verkada cameras support people, face, and vehicle analytics. Analytics need to be enabled in the camera’s settings before the results populate on the camera page and before you can set up most motion-based alerts. See [People Analytics](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/analytics-and-detection/people-analytics)
 and [Vehicle Analytics](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/analytics-and-detection/vehicle-analytics)
 for more information.

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/get-started-with-verkada-security-cameras#licensing)

Licensing


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Every camera you manage in Command needs a license. Verkada licensing is applied for each Command organization, and the licenses co-term to a single expiration date. Your licenses may have been automatically added if you claimed your devices via order number. Otherwise, manually add the licenses from the Admin page. See [Manage Your Licenses](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses)
 for more information on adding and managing licenses.

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/get-started-with-verkada-security-cameras#connect-your-camera)

Connect your camera


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

While Verkada cameras are considered low-voltage devices that do not require a certified electrician to install, we strongly recommend you work with a system integrator or other professional for installation.

Refer to the camera’s [setup guide](https://www.verkada.com/docs/?product=videoSecurity&contentType=setupGuide)
 for mounting instructions.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/get-started-with-verkada-security-cameras#power-and-network)

Power and network

Verkada cameras use Power over Ethernet (PoE) for power and communication over the LAN. In most cases, cameras will need to connect directly to a standard switch. PoE injectors can be used when a PoE switch is not available. See [Camera Power Requirements](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/camera-specifications/camera-power-requirements)
 for the power requirements of your specific camera model.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/get-started-with-verkada-security-cameras#firmware-updates)

Firmware updates

Your camera will run an automatic firmware update once connected to the internet indicated by a flashing orange LED on the front of the camera. This typically takes about 3–5 minutes; see [Camera LED Status Indicators](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/camera-specifications/camera-led-status-indicators)
 for troubleshooting steps if the LED does not turn solid blue within this time.

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/get-started-with-verkada-security-cameras#check-network-settings)

Check network settings


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada cameras are designed to be plug-and-play. However, if your environment includes a firewall with custom rules and policies, you may need to make some configuration changes to get your cameras connected to the cloud. See [Camera Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/camera-specifications/camera-network-settings)
 for more information.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/get-started-with-verkada-security-cameras#review-your-available-bandwidth)

Review your available bandwidth

Your internet speed requirements will depend on the number of cameras at your location. While Verkada cameras store video data locally in on-camera storage, they require an internet connection to send metadata to the cloud. Viewing video through the cloud, archiving video, or using other advanced features will increase bandwidth usage.

See [Bandwidth Consumption & Uplink Requirements](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/camera-specifications/bandwidth-consumption-uplink-requirements-for-video)
 for the bandwidth requirements of your specific camera model.

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/get-started-with-verkada-security-cameras#configure-alerts)

Configure alerts


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada Command allows you to receive push, email, and SMS alerts for events generated in your organization. The ![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1795869993-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FylYKicREo6JpuOJH4teK%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-91bd70c6d63692bdc09cfe2b790499421775da49%252F05283db7c21547b9b9a924fe0723bd14f6720315.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8793c1e0&sv=2) in the bottom left of Command takes you to the **Alerts** page where you can set up and manage alerts. Camera events include motion detection, loitering detection, online status, and more. See [Events and Alerts](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/events-and-alerts)
 and [Configure Camera Event Alerts](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/events-and-alerts/create-camera-event-alerts)
 for more information on camera events and creating alerts.

Last updated 1 day ago

# Roles and Permissions for Access Control | Access Control | Verkada Help

As of November 14, 2024, access control permissions have changed. Users with legacy access control roles will maintain their permissions until they are updated to the current roles detailed in this article. See [Legacy Access Control Roles](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/configuration-and-setup/legacy-access-control-roles)
 for more information.

This article describes the set of roles and associated permissions for [Verkada Access Control](https://www.verkada.com/access-control/)
. For more information on roles and permissions for other Verkada product lines, see [Roles and Permissions for Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
.

* * *

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control#permissions-considerations)

Permissions considerations

*   Subsites inherit permissions from all parent sites, including the ultimate parent.
    
*   Users can belong to multiple groups. When roles conflict, the user receives the **highest role** granted directly or through any group.
    
*   Group-assigned roles can be manually upgraded but not downgraded. Remove the user from the group with the higher role to downgrade their access.
    

Permissions for access control are set at both the organizational level and the site level. There are two org-level roles and one site-level role that define a user’s permissions to view and manage access control permissions and devices:

Access control roles are granted to users independently of one another.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control#org-level-roles)

Org-level roles


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Access System[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control#access-system)

The Access System role grants permissions to manage org-wide access control settings for all sites.

At a high level, these are the permissions granted to each level of Access System roles:

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F134288481-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaaHs5RfKqv9Z49mi02cC%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-026c6834aecc908f93e2907aee7e53e3f68659b3%252F56ea0081a973d9d23dcb78d339155c52a617757e.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=20f7bd0c&sv=2)

None

Does **not** have permission to manage org-wide access control settings for an organization.

Access System Manager

A user or group with Access System Manager can:

*   View, add, delete, and edit door schedules and door exceptions.
    
*   View, add, delete, and edit access exceptions.
    

Access System Admin

A user or group with Access User Admin can:

*   Do everything that an Access System Manager can do.
    
*   Inherits [Access Site Admin](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control)
     permissions for **all sites**.
    
*   Grant [Access System Role](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control)
     and [Access Site Role](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control)
     permissions for any site.
    
*   Configure org-wide access settings, such as Bluetooth unlock.
    
*   Add, edit, and delete badge templates.
    
*   Edit and delete buildings, floors, and add floorplans to floors.
    
*   View the descriptions of and delete saved event reports created by other users.
    
*   [Enable support access](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/enable-support-access)
     to Command for Organization.
    

Access User Management[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control#access-user-management)

The Access User Management role grants permissions to manage access users, credentials, and access groups.

At a high level, these are the permissions granted to each level of Access User Management roles:

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F134288481-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaaHs5RfKqv9Z49mi02cC%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-74df2d3ae83b53f3ac26d4ae01e4a6f1198977b0%252Ff727908be1d9ea009b2f181222054529b96e723a.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=20180c31&sv=2)

None

Does **not** have permission to manage an organization’s access users or groups.

Access Credential Manager

A user or group with Access Credential Manager can:

*   View all access users.
    
*   Add, edit, and delete credentials for access users.
    
*   Add and delete profile pictures for access users.
    
*   Print user badges.
    
*   Configure Pass app settings for access users.
    
*   Grant and suspend access for access users, including editing a user’s start and end date for temporary access.
    

Access User Manager

A user or group with Access User Manager can:

*   Do everything that an Access Credential Manager can do.
    
*   Add and edit access users (not synced via SCIM), including updating all user profile information.
    
*   Add and remove users from existing access groups (not synced via SCIM).
    

Access User Admin

A user or group with Access User Admin can:

*   Do everything an Access User Manager can do.
    
*   Grant [Access User Management Role](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control)
     permissions for the organization.
    
*   Delete access users (not synced via SCIM).
    
*   Add, edit, and delete access groups (not synced via SCIM).
    
*   [Enable support access](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/enable-support-access)
     to Command for Organization.
    

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control#site-level-role)

Site-level role


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Access Site[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control#access-site)

The Access Site role grants permissions to manage access control settings, devices, and door access.

At a high level, these are the permissions granted to each level of Access Site roles:

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F134288481-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaaHs5RfKqv9Z49mi02cC%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-e0599d6030595af7ba548a13720d2efe19b87faf%252F2752516270ba07c3cb2bb4d617bebf13ff731520.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5b56c9dc&sv=2)

None

Does **not** have permission to manage a site’s access control settings or devices.

Access Site Viewer

A user or group with Access Site Viewer permissions for a site can:

*   View any door in the site.
    
*   Unlock doors from Command for doors the user has access to.
    
*   View a floorplan that has doors from the site added.
    
*   View live and historical access events for the site.
    
*   Run, save, export, and distribute reports of historical access events.
    
*   Add and edit alerts based on access events.
    
*   Run and end roll call reports from existing roll call templates and mark people as safe or missing on an active roll call report.
    

Access Site Manager

A user or group with Access Site Manager permissions for a site can:

*   Do everything an Access Site Viewer can do.
    
*   Unlock any door in the site from Command.
    
*   Override the schedule for any door in the site from Command.
    
*   Change a door’s schedule to another preexisting schedule.
    
*   Apply or remove preexisting door exceptions.
    
*   Add, configure, and delete access levels.
    
*   View live and historical access events.
    
*   Run, save, export, and distribute reports of historical access events.
    
*   Create, configure, and delete roll call templates.
    
*   View areas and clear anti-passback violations.
    

Access Site Admin

A user or group with Access Site Admin permissions for a site can:

*   Do everything an Access Site Manager can do.
    
*   Grant [Access Site Role](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control)
     permissions for the site.
    
*   Add, configure, and delete access control devices.
    
*   Add, configure, and delete doors, AUX inputs, and AUX outputs.
    
*   Add, configure, and delete lockdowns.
    
*   Configure areas and anti-passback (APB) settings.
    
*   Manage site-level access settings for the site, such as Bluetooth unlock and scheduled firmware updates.
    
*   [Enable support access](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/enable-support-access)
     to Command for Organization.
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control#set-permissions)

Set permissions


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Users[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control#users)

**Org-level**

In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .Under Org Settings, select Users.Select your user.On the left side panel, next to Access Control Roles, click Edit.a. Grant the necessary org-level access control roles. b. Click Apply Changes.

**Site-level**

In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .Under Org Settings, select Users.Select your user.At the top right, click Manage Roles.a. From the Access Site Role dropdown, select the permission level for the needed sites. b. Click Save.

Groups[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control#groups)

**Org-level**

In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .Under Org Settings, select Groups.Select your group.On the left side panel, next to Access Control Roles, click Edit.a. Grant the necessary org-level access control roles. b. Click Apply Changes.

**Site-level**

In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .Under Org Settings, select Groups.Select your group.At the top, click Site Roles.a. At the top right, click Manage Roles. b. From the Access Site Role dropdown, select the permission level for the needed sites c. Click Save.

* * *

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control#common-access-control-permission-configurations)

Common access control permission configurations

**Scenario**

**Role Configuration**

User needs total control over all access control system settings, devices, and users. ​ For example, a Security Director.

Access System Admin

Access User Admin

User needs to be able to create and edit door schedules or exceptions applied to doors in one or more sites.

For example, a security team member.

Access System Manager

User is responsible for onboarding new users by printing badges and adding them to access groups. ​ For example, an HR staff member.

Access User Manager

User is only responsible for adding credential info and printing badges for new users, such as SCIM-synced users. ​ For example, an HR staff member.

[Access Credential Manager](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control)

User needs to manage all site-specific access control settings but should **not** be able to edit user or access group settings (granted by User Management Roles). ​ For example, an office General Manager.

Access Site Admin

User needs to manage which access groups have access to doors for a particular site but should **not** be able to edit other access control settings for the site. ​ For example, an office facilities staff member.

[Access Site Manager](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control)

User only needs to view and unlock certain doors for a particular site. ​ For example, a front desk receptionist.

[Access Site Viewer](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/roles-and-permissions-for-access-control)

* * *

**Revisions**

11/14/2024:

*   Added the new Access System, Access User Management, and Access Site roles.
    
*   Removed the legacy Access Control Admin, Access Control Manager, and Access Site Admin roles. See [Legacy Access Control Roles](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/configuration-and-setup/legacy-access-control-roles)
     for more information.
    

**Prefer to see it in action?** Check out the [video tutorial](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=akeui7lbme0)
.

# Alarms Network Settings | New Alarms | Verkada Help

This article is a guide for new Alarms. Refer to this [article](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/classic-alarms-network-settings)
 if you have classic Alarms. See [New Alarms vs Classic Alarms](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/new-alarms-vs-classic-alarms)
 if you are unsure which version of Alarms you have.

* * *

This article outlines the required network settings that your Verkada Alarms devices need to communicate with [Verkada Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
. For more information on the required network settings for other Verkada product lines see [Required Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings)
.

Verkada devices are incompatible with LANs that require proxy servers or Secure Socket Layer (SSL)/Transport Layer Security (TLS) inspection. If either is in use, a bypass for all Verkada devices must be implemented for Verkada devices to communicate with Verkada Command.

[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/alarms-specifications/alarms-network-settings#ip-address)

IP address


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Alarms devices must be assigned an IPv4 address to communicate on the LAN and to Verkada Command. Alarms devices use Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP) and User Datagram Protocol (UDP) to obtain their IP addresses and network configurations.

If you require your Alarm device to have a specific IP address, create a DHCP reservation using the device’s Media Access Control (MAC) address (found on the device’s label).

[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/alarms-specifications/alarms-network-settings#domain-name-system)

Domain Name System


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Alarms devices use the DNS server to resolve Verkada’s fully qualified domain names (FQDN) to IP addresses to communicate with them. Your DHCP server tells the Alarms device where the DNS server is on the network and the Alarms device communicates using UDP port 53.

DNS over HTTPS (DoH) is currently not supported.

[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/alarms-specifications/alarms-network-settings#firewall-settings)

Firewall settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Alarms devices require access to many endpoints to ensure they can communicate with Command and all features will be accessible. Many customers may want to allow the devices to communicate with the general required endpoints.

These are the general domains to allow, **applicable for all organization-regions**:

Copy

    34.216.15.26 - UDP/123
    *.verkada.com - UDP/123 + TCP+UDP/443
    *.appcenter.ms - TCP/443
    global.turn.twilio.com - TCP/443
    time.cloudflare.com - TCP/4460
    time.cloudflare.com - UDP/123

If your firewall does not allow wildcard masking, or you prefer to have the entire FQDN of the endpoint in your firewall rules, you can add the domains to your allowlist based on the region your devices are in.

**Region: United States**

Copy

    34.216.15.26 - UDP/123
    api.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    firmware.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    index.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    time.control.verkada.com - UDP/123
    update.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.global-prod.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vprotect.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    *.appcenter.ms - TCP/443
    global.turn.twilio.com - TCP/443

BZ11s in **all regions** require these endpoints:

Copy

    global.stun.twilio.com - UDP/3478
    global.turn.twilio.com - UDP/3478

**WH52 / BK22**

Copy

    224.0.0.251 UDP/5353
    BP52_IP     TCP/UDP 5607
    BP52_IP     TCP/UDP 5606

Use the [Verkada Network Tester](https://network-tester.support.verkada.com/)
 to verify your devices can connect to Verkada Command. Select your region and the **Alarms** product type to run the check.

The following endpoints must be allowed on your network for the test to work:

*   speed.cloudflare.com
    
*   network-tester.support.verkada.com

# New Alarms vs. Classic Alarms | New Alarms | Verkada Help

Verkada Alarms was redesigned in 2024 for greater ease of install, reliability, and user experience. The new Verkada Alarms consists of new hardware and software, which operate independently from the classic version of Alarms.

The key difference between new and classic Alarms is the system architecture. Classic Alarms uses a multi-hub design where each device independently communicates with the cloud. New Alarms employs a single-brain architecture, centralizing cloud communication through the alarm panel and connecting all devices locally via low-voltage wiring.

This setup minimizes device offline risks, improves system uptime, supports offline arm/disarm, and simplifies the **reuse of existing sensors and wiring**, avoiding a full system overhaul.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/new-alarms-vs-classic-alarms#hardware-compatibility-list)

Hardware compatibility list


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Because of the different architectures, new Alarms hardware is **not compatible** with classic Alarms hardware. Only some intrusion sensors and the BZ11 horn are compatible with both new and classic Alarms. See the full hardware compatibility list below:

**Description**

# Camera Network Settings | Verkada Cameras | Verkada Help

This article outlines the required network settings that your Verkada camera needs to communicate with [Verkada Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
. For more information on the required network settings for other Verkada product lines see [Required Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings)
.

Verkada devices are incompatible with LANs that require proxy servers or Secure Socket Layer (SSL)/Transport Layer Security (TLS) inspection. If either is in use, a bypass for all Verkada devices must be implemented for Verkada devices to communicate with Verkada Command.

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/camera-specifications/camera-network-settings#status-led)

Status LED


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A blinking blue status LED or an alternating blue and amber status LED on the front of the physical camera indicates that the camera is not communicating with Command. See [Camera LED Status Indicators](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/camera-specifications/camera-led-status-indicators)
 for more information. If you see this behavior, verify that the network is configured according to the camera’s requirements. If the issue persists, contact [Verkada Support](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support)
.

If the camera is offline and still has power, it will continue to record. Once the camera is reconnected to Command, the video will be available. Once a camera comes online, it can take a few hours for the video footage to sync, and the duration depends largely on how long the camera has been offline.

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/camera-specifications/camera-network-settings#ip-address)

IP address


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Cameras must be assigned an IPv4 address to communicate on the LAN and to Verkada Command. Cameras use Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP) and User Datagram Protocol (UDP) to obtain their IP addresses and network configurations.

If you require your camera to have a specific IP address, create a DHCP reservation using the device’s Media Access Control (MAC) address (found on the device’s label).

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/camera-specifications/camera-network-settings#domain-name-system)

Domain Name System


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Cameras use the DNS server to resolve Verkada’s fully qualified domain names (FQDN) to IP addresses to communicate with them. Your DHCP server tells the camera where the DNS server is on the network and the camera communicates using UDP port 53.

DNS over HTTPS (DoH) is currently not supported.

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/camera-specifications/camera-network-settings#power)

Power


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Cameras are powered through Power over Ethernet (PoE). This means the network switch needs to provide power to the camera, or a PoE injector needs to be utilized. For specifics on power requirements, see the [camera’s datasheet](https://www.verkada.com/docs/?product=videoSecurity&contentType=datasheet)
.

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/camera-specifications/camera-network-settings#firewall-settings)

Firewall settings


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada cameras require access to many endpoints to ensure they can communicate with Command and all features will be accessible. Many customers may want to allow the cameras to communicate with the general required endpoints.

These are the general domains to allow, **applicable for all organization-regions**:

Copy

    *:4100 - TCP/UDP on local network
    *.verkada.com - UDP/123 + TCP+UDP/443
    time.cloudflare.com - TCP/4460 + UDP/123
    *.amazonaws.com - TCP+UDP/443

If you prefer a more granular allowlist, you can add both full FQDNs and wildcard domains to your firewall rules based on the region where your devices are located.

Your region is selected when you [create an organization](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
 in Command.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/camera-specifications/camera-network-settings#region-united-states)

Region: United States

Copy

    *:4100 - TCP/UDP on local network (for local streaming)
    api.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api-ga.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    firmware.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    index.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    time.control.verkada.com - UDP/123
    update.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.global-prod.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    *.vnetcap.control.verkada.com - TCP/443
    *.vstream.vnetcap.control.verkada.com - TCP/443
    *.vsubmit.vnetcap.control.verkada.com - TCP/443
    *.vprovision.vnetcap.control.verkada.com - TCP/443
    *.vproxy.vnetcap.control.verkada.com - TCP/443
    *.kinesisvideo.us-west-2.amazonaws.com - TCP+UDP/443
    s3.ap-southeast-2.amazonaws.com - TCP/443†*
    s3.ca-central-1.amazonaws.com - TCP/443†*
    s3.eu-west-1.amazonaws.com - TCP/443†*
    s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com - TCP/443†
    time.cloudflare.com - TCP/4460 + UDP/123

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/camera-specifications/camera-network-settings#region-europe)

Region: Europe

Copy

    *:4100 - TCP/UDP on local network (for local streaming)
    api-ga.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.prod2.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    index.prod2.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.prod2.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    time.cloudflare.com - TCP/4460 + UDP/123
    time.control.verkada.com - UDP/123
    update.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.global-prod.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.prod2.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    *.kinesisvideo.eu-west-1.amazonaws.com - TCP+UDP/443
    s3.eu-west-1.amazonaws.com - TCP/443†

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/camera-specifications/camera-network-settings#region-australia)

Region: Australia

Copy

    *:4100 - TCP/UDP on LAN (for local streaming)
    api-ga.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.prod-ap-syd.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    index.prod.ap.syd.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    relay.prod-ap-syd.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    time.cloudflare.com - TCP/4460 + UDP/123
    time.control.verkada.com - UDP/123
    update.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.global-prod.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.prod.ap.syd.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    *.kinesisvideo.ap-southeast-2.amazonaws.com - TCP+UDP/443
    s3.ap-southeast-2.amazonaws.com - TCP/443†

* * *

**Footnotes:**

*   †Required for cloud backup.
    
*   \*Only required if your [data storage location](https://help.verkada.com/command/data-protection-and-security/set-a-default-or-camera-specific-location-for-image-and-video-data-storage-and-processing)
     is set outside the United States.
    

Use the [Verkada Network Tester](https://network-tester.support.verkada.com/)
 to verify your devices can connect to Verkada Command. Select your region and the **Cameras** product type to run the check.

The following endpoints must be allowed on your network for the test to work:

*   speed.cloudflare.com
    
*   network-tester.support.verkada.com
    

**Prefer to see it in action?** Check out the [video tutorial](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=5pRUeH_bhw0)
.

# Contact Verkada Support | Command | Verkada Help

Your Verkada license includes enterprise support. Verkada Support is available 24/7 via phone or [live chat](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support#h_926781db34)
.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support#contact-verkada-support)

Contact Verkada Support


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before you contact Verkada Support, it is best to have a support token ready. See [Enable Support Access](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/enable-support-access)
 for more information on creating a support token.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support#command-navigation)

Command navigation

1

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support#log-in-to-verkada-command)

Log in to Verkada [Command](http://command.verkada.com/login)
.

2

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support#at-the-bottom-left-click-greater-than-contact-us)

At the bottom left, click **\>** **Contact Us**.

3

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support#connect-with)

Connect with:

*   Verkada Support via live chat or phone (available 24/7).
    
*   Verkada Sales Representative via email or phone listed for your organization.
    

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support#admin-page)

Admin page

1

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support#in-verkada-command-go-to-all-products-greater-than-admin)

In Verkada Command, go to **All Products** > **Admin** .

2

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support#in-the-left-navigation-click-support)

In the left navigation, click **Support** .

3

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support#connect-with-1)

Connect with:

*   Verkada Support via live chat or phone (available 24/7).
    
*   Verkada Sales Representative via email or phone listed for your organization.
    
    ![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F705858581-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FNRq5qDDjsYNxwNzF1bcB%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-f9813c257091ab5a81e3000fc80ac60c98362ada%252F8de2072e96d98dae68554fe0e3544939fc254b7e.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=14843f59&sv=2)

# Enable Support Access | Command | Verkada Help

[Verkada Support](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support)
 may request access to your Verkada Command account to assist with troubleshooting.

Any action taken by Verkada Support in your account is included in your [organization audit log](https://help.verkada.com/command/organization-wide-settings/manage-and-view-audit-logs)
.

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/enable-support-access#enable-support-access)

Enable support access


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Org Admins, Site Admins, and Access Site Admins can generate and share a support access token to allow Verkada Support to access their accounts.

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .**

2

**In the left navigation, click Support .**

3

**Select Enable Support Access.**

4

**Toggle on Enable Support Access and configure these additional settings as needed:**

a. [Access Duration](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/enable-support-access#h_317ed2f7e3)
 b. [Access Token](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/enable-support-access#h_31ecb633d6)
 c. [Enable Video and Image Access](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/enable-support-access#h_f0a68673bc)
 d. [Limit Access to Sites](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/enable-support-access#h_cdd8b3a3a9)

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F705858581-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FNRq5qDDjsYNxwNzF1bcB%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-7753a0d4f739c706e9db9dee94f38fa476caee9c%252Fed162a783425f6aa084010d700e99871eb006bdb.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ac79573e&sv=2)

**Note:** Verkada Support **does not** automatically gain access to your account when you enable an access token. You will need to open a support case and share this token with them before they can access your account.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/enable-support-access#access-duration)

Access duration

The support access duration is set to auto-expire after 24 hours by default. Admins have the option to extend access for up to 90 days.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/enable-support-access#access-token)

Access token

Access tokens are unique to each admin user account and must be provided to Verkada Support before they can access your account.

**Note**: The access token grants the same permissions as the account that generated it. Verkada Support will have access to the same devices and settings that the active user has. If **Enable Video and Image Access** is toggled on, Verkada Support is able to see video and image data.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/enable-support-access#video-and-image-access)

Video and image access

Verkada Support does not have access to footage, thumbnails, archives, or audio by default. This means that Verkada Support can’t view images, video, or audio, unless you explicitly grant permission.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/enable-support-access#limit-access-to-sites)

Limit access to sites

Org Admins can select the sites they want to grant Verkada Support access to for enhanced privacy.

1

**From the Enable Support Access page, toggle on Limit Access to Sites.**

2

**Select the site(s) you want Verkada Support to be able to access.**

3

**Click Done when finished.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F705858581-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FNRq5qDDjsYNxwNzF1bcB%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-a02947fccf56fe433cc81d337c07965b2df348d6%252Ff005a5a41448f84af5a4b60016f5cdc1b50508e6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7b3102c7&sv=2)

**Note:** Verkada Support will not be able to access any sites within the organization if this setting is toggled on and no sites are selected.

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/enable-support-access#revoke-support-access)

Revoke support access


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada Support will immediately lose access to your account when the access token duration expires. You can end access at any time by revoking the access token.

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .**

2

**In the left navigation, click Support .**

3

**Select Enable Support Access.**

4

**Toggle off Enable Support Access.**

5

**Click Revoke to confirm.**

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/enable-support-access#enable-support-access-from-the-command-app)

Enable support access from the Command app


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

**Open the Verkada Command app.**

2

**In the top left, click .**

3

**In the bottom left, click Help > Support Token.**

4

**On Support Access click Enable.**

5

**Configure these settings as needed:**

a. [Access Duration](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/enable-support-access#h_317ed2f7e3)
 b. [Access Token](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/enable-support-access#h_31ecb633d6)
 c. [Enable Video and Image Access](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/enable-support-access#h_f0a68673bc)
 d. [Limit Access to Sites](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/enable-support-access#h_cdd8b3a3a9)

* * *

**Prefer to see it in action?** Check out the [video tutorial](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=TbR7z6Ub-fI)
.

Last updated 22 hours ago

Was this helpful?

# Add Cellular Gateway to Command - Government Solutions | Government Solutions | Verkada Help

You need to add your gateway to a standard (non-Government Solutions) Command organization to update before you can commission it in a Government Solutions organization.

You must create a [Verkada Command account](https://command.verkada.com/register)
 and log in with [Org Admin](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
 permissions to activate and configure a gateway.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/configuration-and-setup/add-cellular-gateway-to-command-government-solutions#claim-your-gateway)

Claim your gateway


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

**Follow the steps in** [**Add Cellular Gateway to Command**](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/configuration-and-setup/add-cellular-gateway-to-command)
 **to add your gateway to a standard (non-Government Solutions) Command organization.**

2

**Allow the gateway to update to the latest firmware version.**

3

**Decommission the gateway from the standard Command organization.**

4

**Follow the steps in** [**Add Cellular Gateway to Command**](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/configuration-and-setup/add-cellular-gateway-to-command)
 **to add your gateway to a Government Solutions Command organization.**

Last updated 1 day ago

# CJIS Support Status | Government Solutions | Verkada Help

Verkada works with law enforcement and criminal justice agencies in certain states that require access to Criminal Justice Information Services (CJIS) via the National Crime Information Center (NCIC) database. To enable this access, Verkada follows FBI and state requirements that protect the security and integrity of criminal justice information (CJI).

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/cjis-support-status#cjis-compliance-process)

CJIS compliance process


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The CJIS Security Policy is a detailed framework of requirements that agencies and vendors must follow to protect criminal justice information. It addresses areas such as personnel security, data encryption, and physical safeguards. To access CJI or NCIC in a given state, Verkada must comply with both FBI and state-specific CJIS requirements, including:

Background checks[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/cjis-support-status#background-checks)

All employees with unescorted access to CJI must complete state and federal fingerprint-based background checks in each state where Verkada seeks CJI/NCIC access. Access is granted only after these checks are successfully completed and clearance is confirmed.

Signed security addendum[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/cjis-support-status#signed-security-addendum)

Verkada signs a CJIS Security Addendum with each agency customer before enabling access to CJI/NCIC in Verkada Command. This agreement commits Verkada to maintaining a security program that meets federal requirements.

State-specific requirements[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/cjis-support-status#state-specific-requirements)

Many states have additional requirements for customer access to CJI/NCIC. Verkada works with the CJIS Systems Officer (CSO), Terminal Agency Coordinator (TAC), and Local Agency Security Officer (LASO) in each state to meet these requirements.

* * *

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/cjis-support-status#supported-states)

Supported states

Verkada can support customer access to CJI/NCIC in the following states:

*   Arkansas\*
    
*   Arizona
    
*   California\*
    
*   Illinois\*
    
*   Kentucky\*
    
*   Maryland
    
*   Missouri
    
*   Nebraska
    
*   North Carolina\*
    
*   Pennsylvania
    

\*Have a live NCIC integration

This list will be updated as Verkada’s offering expands to more states. If you are a law enforcement agency in a state where Verkada does not currently have NCIC access, please contact [\[email protected\]](https://help.verkada.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#ee8981988b9c80838b809aae988b9c858f8a8fc08d8183)
.

Last updated 20 hours ago

Was this helpful?

# Enable NCIC Alerts | Government Solutions | Verkada Help

Data from the National Crime Information Center (NCIC) is sensitive criminal justice information and must be handled securely. For this reason, NCIC alerts are only available in Verkada’s [Government Solutions Command organizations.](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/get-started-with-government-solutions)

* * *

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/events-and-alerts/enable-ncic-alerts#id-1.-request-ncic-in-your-government-solutions-organization)

1\. Request NCIC in your Government Solutions organization

This feature is not enabled by default and requires Verkada to support [Criminal Justice Information Services (CJIS)](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/cjis-support-status)
 compliance in the state where the data is accessed. Contact your Sales Representative or [\[email protected\]](https://help.verkada.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#94f3fbe2f1e6faf9f1fae0d4e2f1e6fff5f0f5baf7fbf9)
 to get started.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/events-and-alerts/enable-ncic-alerts#id-2.-enable-ncic-in-feature-manager)

2\. Enable NCIC in Feature Manager

You need Org Admin permissions to access Feature Manager.

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin.**

2

**Select Feature Manager.**

3

**To the right of NCIC LPR Data Integration, click the dropdown and select Enable.**

This feature is only available on cameras with vehicle analytics enabled.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/events-and-alerts/enable-ncic-alerts#id-3.-grant-cjis-viewer-permissions)

3\. Grant CJIS viewer permissions

After the feature is enabled, Org Admins must assign CJIS Viewer permissions to the appropriate personnel who are CJIS-approved. This action can only be granted on a per-user basis.

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin.**

2

**Select Users & Permissions > Users.**

3

**Select the user you want to edit.**

4

**At the top, click > Grant CJIS Viewer.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1400995684-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F79mFgTcvQ8N4ByjEDZUn%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-feb7ca527dd2cd772e6274af59fb88d75d32fda2%252Fb85fb32a890657a4e1a0dd87d0d18f798cf173a5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6309951d&sv=2)

After the feature is enabled and users have the required permissions, you can create a new NCIC alert.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/events-and-alerts/enable-ncic-alerts#configure-ncic-alerts)

Configure NCIC alerts


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/events-and-alerts/enable-ncic-alerts#create-alert-greater-than-cameras)

Create Alert > Cameras

1

**On the Command homepage, left navigation, click Alerts.**

2

**At the top left, click New Alert.**

3

**On Select Event, choose Camera > License Plate Hotlist.**

4

**On Cameras:**

a. Choose to receive alerts from **Sites** or **Individual Cameras**. b. Click **Done** to continue.

5

**On Select License Plate Hotlist:**

a. Select **NCIC.** b. Select **Offense Reasons** to be included within the alert.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1400995684-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F79mFgTcvQ8N4ByjEDZUn%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-eb56981af7743065ed2edec0bbf02142c3832513%252Ff4cb7c02df0cfee81aa2cfbc7e216bfb6bb28a6a.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bd14188d&sv=2)

c. Click **Done** and continue with the alert [recipients](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/events-and-alerts/enable-ncic-alerts#h_b2f69ecae8)
.

Only License Plate Recognition (LPR) enabled cameras can be selected.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/events-and-alerts/enable-ncic-alerts#create-alert-greater-than-recipients)

Create Alert > Recipients

1

**On Recipients, add users individually or assign the alert to a group.**

2

**Select the dropdown menu next to a user or group to choose their notification method(s). Recipients can be notified via push, SMS, or email notifications.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1400995684-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F79mFgTcvQ8N4ByjEDZUn%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-a30e5c666efe865b169b36f277c2ab798ad76c5d%252F3a9609d9912905edd0f35abfff403a95e0b820c8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fcdbb065&sv=2)

3

**(Optional) By default, you will be an alert recipient. Select the dropdown menu and click Delete to remove yourself.**

4

**Click Done and continue with the alert** [**notification schedule**](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/events-and-alerts/enable-ncic-alerts#h_7549527028)
**.**

Any recipient added to this alert will see it appear under the **Shared Alerts** section of their **Alerts** page.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/events-and-alerts/enable-ncic-alerts#create-alert-greater-than-notification-schedule)

Create Alert > Notification Schedule

1

**On Notification Schedule, specify the days and times for the alerts to send notifications. Alerts generate 24/7 by default.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1400995684-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F79mFgTcvQ8N4ByjEDZUn%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-b9042c786a9dd12580abefdd20f412fe59cbac5e%252F7b61969c185d482c85ec3b7f15a687d75aee8d13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f0c3481&sv=2)

2

**Click Done and continue to** [**finish the alert**](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/events-and-alerts/enable-ncic-alerts#h_0f4aeaa90c)
**.**

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/events-and-alerts/enable-ncic-alerts#finish-the-alert)

1

**In the bottom right of the configuration window, click Next.**

2

# Required Access Control Network Settings - Government Solutions | Government Solutions | Verkada Help

This article outlines the required network settings that your Verkada [access controllers](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/access-controllers-series-overview.pdf)
 need to communicate with [Verkada Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
. For more information on the required network settings for other Verkada product lines see [Required Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings)
.

Verkada devices are incompatible with LANs that require proxy servers or Secure Socket Layer (SSL)/Transport Layer Security (TLS) inspection. If either is in use, a bypass for all Verkada devices must be implemented for Verkada devices to communicate with Verkada Command.

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-access-control-network-settings-government-solutions#status-led)

Status LED


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

At the top left of the physical access controller, if you see a flashing blue [status LED](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/troubleshooting/verkada-ac41-status-led)
 this indicates that the access controller is not communicating with Command.

If you see this behavior:

*   Check that the network is set up correctly for the access controller.
    
*   See [Verkada Access Offline Operation](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/troubleshooting/verkada-access-offline-operation)
     to understand what the access system does when it cannot communicate with Command.
    

If the problem persists, contact [Verkada Support](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support)
.

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-access-control-network-settings-government-solutions#ip-address)

IP address


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Access controllers need an IPv4 address to communicate on the local area network (LAN) and to Command through the internet. Access controllers use Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP), UDP ports 67 and 68, to obtain their IP addresses and network configurations.

If you want to have a specific IP address on your access controller, set a DHCP reservation using the access controller’s [Media Access Control (MAC) address](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/hardware-installation/find-a-serial-number-and-mac-address)
 (found on the device’s label).

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-access-control-network-settings-government-solutions#domain-name-system)

Domain Name System


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Access Controllers use the DNS server to resolve Verkada’s fully qualified domain names (FQDN) to IP addresses to communicate with them. Your DHCP server tells the access controller where the DNS server is on the network and the access controller communicates using UDP port 53.

DNS over HTTPS (DoH) is currently not supported.

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-access-control-network-settings-government-solutions#power)

Power


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For specifics on power requirements, see the [access controller’s datasheet](https://www.verkada.com/docs/?product=accessControl&contentType=datasheet)
.

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-access-control-network-settings-government-solutions#firewall-settings)

Firewall settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada access controllers require access to many endpoints to ensure they can communicate with Command and all features will be accessible. Many customers may want to allow the access controllers to communicate with the general required endpoints.

These are the general domains to allow, **applicable for all organization-regions**:

Copy

    34.216.15.26 - UDP/123
    35.166.49.153 - UDP/123 + TCP+UDP/443
    *.verkada.com - UDP/123 + TCP+UDP/443

If you prefer a more granular allowlist, you can add both IP addresses and full FQDNs to your firewall rules based on the region where your devices are located.

Your region is selected when you [create an organization](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
 in Command.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-access-control-network-settings-government-solutions#region-united-states-gov)

Region: United States Gov

**Standard Verkada Endpoints**

Copy

    api.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.global-prod.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api-ga.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP 443
    firmware.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    update.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vconductor.global-prod.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    api.global-prod.control.verkada.com (HTTPS/443)
    update.control.verkada.com (HTTPS/443)
    NTP: returned by DHCP client option 42, if not provided, falls back to time.nist.gov (UDP/123)
    Local streaming: *:4100 on LAN (HTTPS/443)
    RTSP: *:8554 on LAN
    *.kinesisvideo.us-gov-west-1.amazonaws.com (HTTPS/443)
    s3.us-gov-west-1.amazonaws.com (HTTPS/443)
    verkada-firmware.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com (HTTPS/443)
    *.prod-govus-pine.control.verkadagov.com (HTTPS/443)
    api.control.verkada.com (HTTPS/443)

**NTP Endpoints**

Copy

    34.216.15.26 - UDP/123
    35.166.49.153 - UDP/123 + TCP+UDP/443
    time.control.verkada.com - UDP/123
    time.cloudflare.com - TCP/4460
    time.cloudflare.com - UDP/123

**Access Control Endpoints**

Copy

    access.control.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vcerberus.command.verkada.com - TCP+UDP/443
    *.prod-govus-pine.control.verkadagov.com - TCP+UDP/443
    vinnout.prod-govus-pine.command.verkadagov.com 

Use the [Verkada Network Tester](https://network-tester.support.verkada.com/)
 to verify your devices can connect to Verkada Command. Select your region and the **Access** product type to run the check.

The following endpoints must be allowed on your network for the test to work:

*   speed.cloudflare.com
    
*   network-tester.support.verkada.com

# Government Solutions Licensing | Government Solutions | Verkada Help

To access a Government Solutions Command organization, you must have valid Government Solutions licenses for every device in your organization.

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/government-solutions-licensing#how-verkada-licensing-is-applied)

How Verkada licensing is applied


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada licensing is applied for each Command organization, and the licenses co-term to a single expiration date. This means that all of the licenses in an organization are combined, and the expiration date for the organization is the weighted average of all the individual licenses. Learn more about how to [calculate a license expiration date](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/calculate-license-expiration-date)
.

See [Manage Your Licenses](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses)
 for information on licencing for other Verkada product lines.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/government-solutions-licensing#license-requirements-by-product-family)

License requirements by product family


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Refer to this table for an overview of the license requirements of each product family:

**Product Family**

**License requirement**

Air Quality Sensors

One Government Solutions license per sensor

Cameras

One Government Solutions license per camera

Optional: One Cloud Backup License per 30-day increments on a single device’s cloud retention. Learn more about [Extended Cloud Backup Licensing](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/historical-playback/extended-cloud-backup-licensing)
.

Multisensor cameras

One Government Solutions MLT4 camera license per CH52-E Four-Camera Multisensor

Gateway

One Government Solutions cellular gateway license per cellular gateway.

Optional: One Government Solutions data plan license per connected camera or intercom. A four-head multisensor camera needs four data licenses.

Guest

One Workplace license grants you access to use one Guest iPad

Viewing Station

One viewing station license per viewing station

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/government-solutions-licensing#purchase-government-solutions-licenses)

Purchase Government Solutions licenses


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Government Solutions licenses are available in 1, 3, 5, and 10-year terms.

There are two types of licenses: capacity increase (CAP) and renewal (RNW).

*   **Capacity Increase (CAP) licenses**: Verkada CAP licenses are automatically activated when the associated Verkada hardware order is shipped. New device licenses include a 30-day extension beyond the purchased term to accommodate shipping and installation. The extension period is fixed and does not depend on when the device is installed or activated.
    
*   **Renewal (RNW) licenses:** Verkada RNW licenses extend an organization’s existing term but remain inactive until the earlier of:
    
    *   The date they are claimed within a Command organization or
        
    *   One year after the purchase date. If unclaimed after one year, the license automatically activates, and its term begins to run. Any license claimed beyond this one-year period results in a shortened remaining term. This policy ensures compliance with the intended service period.
        
    

Licenses are usually sold with your Verkada devices, but you can also purchase them separately from your Verkada reseller or sales representative. See the latest [licensing prices](https://www.verkada.com/pricing/)
.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/government-solutions-licensing#renew-your-licenses)

Renew your licenses


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When your licenses are soon to expire, you need to renew your license to avoid losing access to Verkada Command. You can renew your license by contacting your Verkada Sales Representative or your Verkada Reseller.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/government-solutions-licensing#renewal-notifications-and-license-expiration)

Renewal notifications and license expiration

30 days before expiry, you will expect to:

*   Receive an email notifying you that your licenses are about to expire.
    
*   See a banner in Command.
    

You will lose access to Command if you haven’t renewed your license within 30 days after your expiration date.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/government-solutions-licensing#licensing-overcap-policy)

Licensing overcap policy


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

An organization is considered to be in overcap when it has more devices commissioned than the number of licenses claimed.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/government-solutions-licensing#overcap-policy)

Overcap policy

Verkada enforces software compliance by requiring each hardware product to have a valid, claimed software license(see requirements above). The Overcap policy introduces an **Invalid** status for organizations that exceed their claimed licenses, ensuring compliance across all Verkada products. After a 90-day grace period, organizations without proper licensing lose access to critical functions, including device management and notifications.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/government-solutions-licensing#how-it-works)

How it works

Verkada will notify all Command users 90 days **before** an organization loses access, prompting them to claim additional licenses. Organization Admins will receive in-product banners and emails over 90 days to ensure they restore compliance.

All devices will remain functional when access to Command is restricted. However, users will still have access to the **License Manager**, **Devices**, and **Technical Support** pages when an organization is no longer compliant.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/government-solutions-licensing#restore-compliance)

Restore compliance

Organization Admins can perform **one** of the following actions to restore compliance:

*   Claim any unused licensing keys.
    
*   Remove any unused devices from the organization.
    
*   Contact your Sales Representative or email [\[email protected\]](https://help.verkada.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#f09c9993959e83999e97b08695829b919491de939f9d)
     if you believe there has been an error with the licensing implementation on your account.
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/government-solutions-licensing#faq)

FAQ


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

What happens if I have insufficient or expired licenses?[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/government-solutions-licensing#what-happens-if-i-have-insufficient-or-expired-licenses)

Verkada will send you an email notification and add a banner notification to your Command Organization.

You need valid licenses to use Command. If you don’t [claim your licenses](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/find-and-add-license-keys-to-command)
 when adding new devices or products or renew them when they expire, you will lose access to most of your Command functionality after a 30-day grace period.

*   For expired organizations, you have a 30-day grace period before you lose access.
    
*   For organizations with insufficient licenses, you have a 90-day grace period before you lose access.
    
*   Contact your Verkada Partner or Sales Representative to purchase additional licenses.
    

At the end of this grace period, you will no longer have access to any of your devices or configure any settings. Alarms and Event notifications will also be disabled. You will, however, be able to delete devices and products so you get back into compliance in case you have insufficient licenses.

How will I know if my licenses are soon to expire?[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/government-solutions-licensing#how-will-i-know-if-my-licenses-are-soon-to-expire)

30 days before your license is set to expire, Verkada will send you an email notification and add a banner notification to your Command Organization.

How do I regain full access to Command?[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/government-solutions-licensing#how-do-i-regain-full-access-to-command)

If your access to Command was limited due to insufficient licenses, you can:

*   Delete the products that are above your license cap to get back into compliance
    
*   Contact your Verkada Partner or Sales Representative to purchase additional licenses.
    

If your access to Command was limited due to expired licenses, you can contact your Verkada Partner or Sales Representative to renew your licenses.

Will my devices still record data?[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/government-solutions-licensing#will-my-devices-still-record-data)

As long as your Verkada devices are still connected, they will continue to record data. This data will be available when you regain access to Command (as long as you’re still within the retention period for the given device). Badges and Verkada Pass will still work as before, but you’ll be unable to change your settings via Command.

What happens if I don’t return my expired trial devices?[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/compliance/government-solutions-licensing#what-happens-if-i-dont-return-my-expired-trial-devices)

Trialing a Verkada device is the best way to experience how our products and platform works. You can initiate a free trial for most of our devices through your Verkada Sales Rep, or your Verkada Partner.

The free trial lasts for 30 days. After the 30 days are up, you’ll see a banner in Command reminding you to return or purchase your trial devices. If you don’t return the devices within 30 days of the expiry date they will stop working as expected.

If you need additional time to test our trial devices and platform, you can ask your Verkada Sales Rep for an extension.

Last updated 1 day ago

Was this helpful?
