# Required Air Quality Sensor Network Settings - Government Solutions | Government Solutions | Verkada Help

Verkada devices need to communicate with a [Government Solution Command organization](https://www.verkada.com/solutions/government-grade)
 via their local network. In most cases, minimal updates to your network settings are needed. Additional configuration may be required for complex or highly secure networks.

See [Required Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings)
 for more information on the required network settings for other Verkada product lines.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-air-quality-sensor-network-settings-government-solutions#compatibility)

Compatibility


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada devices are incompatible with local area networks (LANs) that require proxy servers or Secure Socket Layer (SSL)/Transport Layer Security (TLS) inspection. If either is in use, a bypass for all Verkada devices must be implemented for your Verkada devices to communicate with Verkada Command.

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-air-quality-sensor-network-settings-government-solutions#ip-address)

IP address


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada devices must be assigned an IPv4 address to communicate on the LAN and to Verkada Command through the internet. By default, all Verkada devices use Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP) and User Datagram Protocol (UDP) to obtain their IP addresses and network configurations.

If you require your device to have a specific IP address, create a DHCP reservation using the device’s Media Access Control (MAC) address (found on the device’s label). ​

Verkada devices may utilize path MTU discovery to determine the maximum transmission unit of the network path. Therefore, it is necessary to permit ICMP Fragmentation Needed (Type 3, Code 4) and ICMPv6 Packet Too Big (Type 2) packets. Ensure your firewall(s) are configured to permit this in the return path to your Verkada devices.

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-air-quality-sensor-network-settings-government-solutions#domain-name-system)

Domain Name System


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada devices use the Domain Name System (DNS) server to resolve Verkada’s fully qualified domain names (FQDN) to IP addresses to communicate with them. Your DHCP server tells the Verkada device where the DNS server is on the network, and the device communicates using UDP port 53.

DNS over HTTPS (DoH) is not currently supported.

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-air-quality-sensor-network-settings-government-solutions#power)

Power


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Most Verkada devices are powered through Power over Ethernet (PoE). You can use the product [datasheets](https://www.verkada.com/docs/?contentType=datasheet)
 to figure out the power requirements for your Verkada devices.

These are the most common power requirements:

*   IEE 802.3af, Type 1 PoE
    
*   IEEE 802.3at, Type 2 PoE+
    
*   IEEE 802.3bt, Type 3 PoE++
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-air-quality-sensor-network-settings-government-solutions#air-quality-sensors-firewall-settings)

Air Quality Sensors firewall settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada Air Quality Sensors require access to many endpoints to ensure they can communicate with Command and that all features are accessible.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-air-quality-sensor-network-settings-government-solutions#region-united-states-gov)

Region: United States Gov

*   api.prod-govus-pine.control.verkadagov.com (TCP+UDP/443)
    
    *   3.32.137.127/32
        
    *   3.31.127.57/32
        
    *   3.30.93.146/32
        
    
*   api.control.verkada.com (TCP+UDP/443)
    
    *   35.155.73.204/32
        
    *   54.186.237.126/32
        
    *   35.166.49.153/32
        
    *   35.84.130.83/32
        
    
*   vsensor.prod-govus-pine.verkadagov.com (TCP+UDP/443)

# Required Command Connector Network Settings - Government Solutions | Government Solutions | Verkada Help

Verkada devices need to communicate with a [Government Solution Command organization](https://www.verkada.com/solutions/government-grade)
 via their local network. In most cases, minimal updates to your network settings are needed. Additional configuration may be required for complex or highly secure networks.

See [Required Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings)
 for more information on the required network settings for other Verkada product lines.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-command-connector-network-settings-government-solutions#compatibility)

Compatibility


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada devices are incompatible with local area networks (LANs) that require proxy servers or Secure Socket Layer (SSL)/Transport Layer Security (TLS) inspection. If either is in use, a bypass for all Verkada devices must be implemented for your Verkada devices to communicate with Verkada Command.

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-command-connector-network-settings-government-solutions#ip-address)

IP address


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada devices must be assigned an IPv4 address to communicate on the LAN and to Verkada Command through the internet. By default, all Verkada devices use Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP) and User Datagram Protocol (UDP) to obtain their IP addresses and network configurations.

If you require your device to have a specific IP address, create a DHCP reservation using the device’s Media Access Control (MAC) address (found on the device’s label). You can also set up [static IP addresses](https://help.verkada.com/command-connector/configuration-and-setup/configure-static-ip-addresses-for-command-connector)
 in Command for Command Connector.

Verkada devices may utilize path MTU discovery to determine the maximum transmission unit of the network path. Therefore, it is necessary to permit ICMP Fragmentation Needed (Type 3, Code 4) and ICMPv6 Packet Too Big (Type 2) packets. Ensure your firewall(s) are configured to permit this in the return path to your Verkada devices.

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-command-connector-network-settings-government-solutions#domain-name-system)

Domain Name System


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada devices use the Domain Name System (DNS) server to resolve Verkada’s fully qualified domain names (FQDN) to IP addresses to communicate with them. Your DHCP server tells the Verkada device where the DNS server is on the network, and the device communicates using UDP port 53.

DNS over HTTPS (DoH) is not currently supported.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-command-connector-network-settings-government-solutions#command-connector-firewall-settings)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Required Cellular Gateway Network Settings - Government Solutions | Government Solutions | Verkada Help

Verkada devices need to communicate with a [Government Solution Command organization](https://www.verkada.com/solutions/government-grade)
 via their local network. In most cases, minimal updates to your network settings are needed. Additional configuration may be required for complex or highly secure networks.

See [Required Network Settings](https://help.verkada.com/command/required-network-settings)
 for more information on the required network settings for other Verkada product lines.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-cellular-gateway-network-settings-government-solutions#compatibility)

Compatibility


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada devices are incompatible with local area networks (LANs) that require proxy servers or Secure Socket Layer (SSL)/Transport Layer Security (TLS) inspection. If either is in use, a bypass for all Verkada devices must be implemented for your Verkada devices to communicate with Verkada Command.

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-cellular-gateway-network-settings-government-solutions#ip-address)

IP address


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada devices must be assigned an IPv4 address to communicate on the LAN and to Verkada Command through the internet. By default, all Verkada devices use Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol (DHCP) and User Datagram Protocol (UDP) to obtain their IP addresses and network configurations.

If you require your device to have a specific IP address, create a DHCP reservation using the device’s Media Access Control (MAC) address (found on the device’s label). ​

Verkada devices may utilize path MTU discovery to determine the maximum transmission unit of the network path. Therefore, it is necessary to permit ICMP Fragmentation Needed (Type 3, Code 4) and ICMPv6 Packet Too Big (Type 2) packets. Ensure your firewall(s) are configured to permit this in the return path to your Verkada devices.

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-cellular-gateway-network-settings-government-solutions#domain-name-system)

Domain Name System


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada devices use the Domain Name System (DNS) server to resolve Verkada’s fully qualified domain names (FQDN) to IP addresses to communicate with them. Your DHCP server tells the Verkada device where the DNS server is on the network, and the device communicates using UDP port 53.

DNS over HTTPS (DoH) is not currently supported.

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-cellular-gateway-network-settings-government-solutions#power)

Power


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Most Verkada devices are powered through Power over Ethernet (PoE). You can use the product [datasheets](https://www.verkada.com/docs/?contentType=datasheet)
 to figure out the power requirements for your Verkada devices.

These are the most common power requirements:

*   IEE 802.3af, Type 1 PoE
    
*   IEEE 802.3at, Type 2 PoE+
    
*   IEEE 802.3bt, Type 3 PoE++
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-cellular-gateway-network-settings-government-solutions#cellular-gateway-firewall-settings)

Cellular Gateway firewall settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada Cellular Gateways require access to many endpoints to ensure they can communicate with Command and that all features are accessible.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/required-network-settings/required-cellular-gateway-network-settings-government-solutions#region-united-states-gov)

Region: United States Gov

*   api.prod-govus-pine.control.verkadagov.com (TCP+UDP/443)
    
    *   3.32.137.127/32
        
    *   3.31.127.57/32
        
    *   3.30.93.146/32
        
    
*   api.control.verkada.com (TCP+UDP/443)
    
    *   35.155.73.204/32
        
    *   54.186.237.126/32
        
    *   35.166.49.153/32

# Air Quality Sensor Status LED | Air Quality | Verkada Help

Each Verkada [Air Quality Sensor](https://www.verkada.com/air-quality/sensors#overview)
 is equipped with an outside LED light. This light indicates its operating status. Verkada offers the [SV11](https://www.verkada.com/sensors/sv11/)
 series and SV20 series (including [SV21](http://sv21/)
, [SV23](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
, [SV25](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
).

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-status-led#sv11-series)

SV11 series


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The [SV11](https://www.verkada.com/sensors/sv11/)
 series follows the same LED convention as all Verkada cameras.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-f40ec6af76669b489ca83b0c4cceab8e74b284e3%252F39d533797af0dee409035ed6d8d0e6f232f303d0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c7ae8471&sv=2)

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-status-led#sv20-series)

SV20 series


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The newer SV20 series ([SV21](http://sv21/)
, [SV23](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
, [SV25](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
) uses a white LED indicator; however, its status is analogous to that of the blue LED on the SV11.

# Installation Guidelines for Sensors | Air Quality | Verkada Help

For best performance, use this article to learn about the standard and recommended guidelines for installing Verkada [Air Quality Sensors](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
. ​

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/hardware-installation/installation-guidelines-for-sensors#standard-guidelines-by-sensor)

Standard guidelines by sensor


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/hardware-installation/installation-guidelines-for-sensors#sv20-series)

SV20 series

Here are some standard guidelines for the [SV20 Series](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
 installation:

*   **CO₂ monitoring**
    
    *   Wall mounting, between 3-6 ft (0.9–1.8m) from floor
        
    *   Keep sensor at least 5 ft (1.5m) away from any doors or operable windows
        
    
*   **Vape detection**
    
    *   Ceiling mounting, no more than 8-9 ft (2.4–2.7m) from the ground. If the height is increased, detection decreases.
        
    *   If placed in a bathroom, 1 sensor per 2 stalls is recommended. At least 3 ft (0.9m) from vents or walls.
        
    *   Wall mounting may lead to inaccurate vape detection.
        
    
*   At least 3 ft (0.9m) away from areas that are exposed to airflow and circulation (e.g. HVAC vents, windows, refrigerator blowers, and so on).
    
*   Away from direct sunlight exposure.
    

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/hardware-installation/installation-guidelines-for-sensors#sv11)

SV11

Here are some standard guidelines for the [SV11](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/sensors-quick-start-guide.pdf)
 installation:

*   Mount indoors on a ceiling. We recommend to installed 8 ft (2.4m) above the floor.
    
*   On a solid, nonmetallic surface (e.g. drywall, drop ceiling, wood, concrete, and so on).
    
*   At least 3 ft (0.9m) away from areas that are exposed to airflow and circulation (e.g. HVAC vents, windows, refrigerator blowers, and so on).
    
*   Away from direct sunlight exposure.
    
*   Wall mounting is possible, however, leads to inaccurate temperatures and air quality detection and should be avoided, if possible.
    

The SV11 is designed to be installed on the ceiling; the range and accuracy values listed in the [data sheet](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/sensors-quick-start-guide.pdf)
 are based on the device mounted in this position. If the SV11 is mounted on a wall (vertically), it will still function, but the range and accuracy values may not be within the range specified in the [data sheet](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/sensors-quick-start-guide.pdf)
.

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/hardware-installation/installation-guidelines-for-sensors#recommendations-for-best-performance)

Recommendations for best performance


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/hardware-installation/installation-guidelines-for-sensors#installation-location)

Installation location

To achieve the best accuracy for all the sensors on the device, we recommend to mount the sensor on an 8 ft (2.4m) ceiling. This provides up to 250 sq ft (23 sqm) of total coverage per sensor.

**Note**: For vape detection, put 1 sensor for every 2 stalls in a bathroom.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-0dbc18c61a99b0bb14323991586b7dce02c55c2f%252Fcabff804080f73edfbcdac9d3b3ebaa70c540310.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f02af8f0&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/hardware-installation/installation-guidelines-for-sensors#installation-surface)

Installation surface

The sensors are designed to be installed on a solid nonmetallic surface such as drywall, a drop ceiling, concrete, or wood. Metallic or surfaces that adjust the predictable heat generated by the device may lead to temperature inaccuracies.

If the SV11 is mounted on a metal surface in a cold \[-5º to 5º C (23° to 41° F)\] or hot \[27º to 50º C (80° F to 122° F)\] environment, we recommend to place a piece of rubber material between the surface and the SV11 mounting plate. This recommendation ensures that the temperature of the mounting surface has less of an impact on the accuracy of the SV11 sensor readings.

The SV20 series devices utilize a hardened plastic mount plate that significantly reduces this effect, but we still recommend that they be installed on a solid, nonmetallic surface. ​

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/hardware-installation/installation-guidelines-for-sensors#power-consumption)

Power consumption

Verkada environmental sensors use industry-standard 802.3af \[Power over Ethernet (PoE)\]. During normal operation, the SV11 consumes 4W of power and the SV20 series devices typically consume 3W of power (max of 4W of power). For more information, see [Environmental Sensor Power Requirements](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-power-requirements)
.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/hardware-installation/installation-guidelines-for-sensors#calibration-time)

Calibration time

When the device is first plugged-in, temperature, TVOC, and CO₂ (only on the SV20 series) readings may be higher or lower than anticipated. These readings self-correct over an automated calibration period and do not represent a significant amount of variability.

All air quality sensors have an initial calibration period of 4 hours, but can take up to 3 days to complete full calibration of the TVOC. For optimal accuracy, we recommend to mount the sensors in a stable environment without intermittent events such as sporadic HVAC events.

**Note**: There’s a possibility that there will be variability in the sensor readings if 2 or more air quality sensors are placed next to one another. Each sensor has its own inherit characteristics and calibration can result in different readings.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/hardware-installation/installation-guidelines-for-sensors#temperature-humidity-range-and-accuracy)

Temperature, humidity range, and accuracy

Below are the ranges and accuracy measurements for each of the air quality sensor series temperature and humidity sensors. These values represent the typical and recommended installation location. If the sensor is installed outside of the recommendations, the range and accuracy may fall out of the accuracy range stated in the [data sheet](https://help.verkada.com/en/articles/6732870-what-s-new-in-the-sv20-series)
.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/hardware-installation/installation-guidelines-for-sensors#sv20-series-1)

SV20 series

**Temperature Range**

**Temperature Accuracy**

**Humidity Accuracy**

**Comments**

< -5º C (23° F)

N/A

N/A

Not within operating range of the device

\-5º to 45º C (23° to 113° F)

Typical ± 0.3º C (± 0.54º F)

Max ± 1º C (± 1.8º F)

Operating Range: 0–95% non-condensing

Accuracy: ± 3% @ 25º C

Accuracy measurements based on the sensor being installed

\> 45º C (113° F)

N/A

N/A

Not within operating range of the device

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/hardware-installation/installation-guidelines-for-sensors#sv11-1)

SV11

**Temperature Range**

**Temperature Accuracy**

**Humidity Accuracy**

**Comments**

< -5º C (23° F)

N/A

N/A

Not within operating range of the device

\-5º to 50º C (23° to 123° F)

Typical ± 2.5º C (± 4.5º F)

Max ± 3.5º C (± 6.5º F)

± 5% to ± 10%

Accuracy measurements based on the sensor being installed

\> 50º C (122° F)

N/A

N/A

Not within operating range of the device

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/hardware-installation/installation-guidelines-for-sensors#wall-mounting)

Wall mounting

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/hardware-installation/installation-guidelines-for-sensors#sv20-series-2)

SV20 series

The **SV20 series** devices can be mounted on a wall without issue; however, we don’t recommended for use with vape detection.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/hardware-installation/installation-guidelines-for-sensors#sv11-2)

SV11

The **SV11** can be mounted on a wall, however, we don’t recommended it. The ranges and accuracy of the sensors are specified for the device being installed on a solid ceiling surface. If installed on a wall, the accuracy and ranges of the SV11 sensors may be outside of what is specified in the [data sheet](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/sensors-quick-start-guide.pdf)
.

**Mount on a non-solid surface (example: hanging in the air)**

SV11 sensors are designed to be installed on a solid ceiling surface facing the ground. If the SV11 sensor is installed in "free air", where the front and back of the device are exposed, the accuracy of the temperature and vape detection on the sensor may not fall within the stated range.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/hardware-installation/installation-guidelines-for-sensors#exposure-to-direct-sunlight)

Exposure to direct sunlight

For the highest accuracy, do not place the sensor where it is exposed to direct sunlight. If the sensor is exposed to direct sunlight, the temperature and humidity readings may fall out of the accuracy range stated in the [data sheet](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/sensors-quick-start-guide.pdf)
.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/hardware-installation/installation-guidelines-for-sensors#exposure-to-air-circulation)

Exposure to air circulation

If the sensor is exposed to consistent airflow or sporadic airflow (for example, an HVAC vent, a refrigerator blower, a window, and so on), the accuracy of the temperature sensor and the other onboard sensors may fall out of the accuracy range stated in the data sheet. Exposure to airflow changes the thermodynamics of the device which leads to varying inaccuracies in the temperature, humidity, and other sensor readings.

Airflow as present in areas, such as HVAC ducts, can generate pressure drops, back pressure, and dynamic fluctuations leading to increased sensor noise and reduced accuracy.

For the highest accuracy, mount the sensor away from HVAC vents or areas where the device could be exposed to varying levels of airflow or circulation.

# Security Screening Settings | Guest | Verkada Help

Verkada Guest Security Screening allows organizations across all industries to instantly vet visitors. Per Guest Type, organizations can configure a security screening step that require visitors to present an ID, which is used for searches across external databases. Guest offers a set of controls for the results returned by the feature as well as tools for responding to confirmed offenders.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/configuration-and-setup/security-screening-settings#control-security-screening-content)

Control Security Screening Content


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/configuration-and-setup/security-screening-settings#hide-incomplete-records)

Hide Incomplete Records

Incomplete records are records that are missing a photo of the offender and a complete date of birth for the offender. By default, incomplete records are displayed after all high quality records have been dismissed.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1436127735-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FZyuELZr7uIcXX3WnjX0N%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-edd8f0a9689b875ea83ac4de0a835f7fdd500ac0%252F68a10f80b4ab83f2ec8d77df7ae7cf80a850eb6f.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=756ef3b7&sv=2)

The Hide Incomplete Records toggle allows organizations to focus only on high quality records when reviewing security screening results. With the toggle on, incomplete records do not need to be reviewed. Guest users will still have the option to review incomplete records once high quality records have been dismissed:

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1436127735-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FZyuELZr7uIcXX3WnjX0N%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-1675b2a0aa7ad9728b3b93471e8c23e020075832%252F1b8264f68cb3024cdd269d2cf1d25a8af4f85688.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=be96745&sv=2)

To turn on the **Hide Incomplete Records** toggle:

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Workplace >** **Guest.**

2

**On the left navigation, click Guest Settings.**

3

**Under Sites > Security Screening.**

4

**Toggle on Hide Incomplete Records.**

A user must be a **Workplace Site Admin** to toggle **Hide Complete Records**\*.\*

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/configuration-and-setup/security-screening-settings#record-age-filter)

Record Age Filter

The Record Age Filter allows organizations to display only records created within a specified number of years, counting back from the current date, as defined by the administrator.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1436127735-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FZyuELZr7uIcXX3WnjX0N%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-7a1b1af2d0abf2cdaeaf6789a83dbfacaefee688%252Fc0521be27de7de35696e65e3149efb386fb3917c.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4423fc26&sv=2)

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Workplace >** **Guest.**

2

**On the left navigation, click Guest Settings.**

3

**Under Organization > Security & Data.**

4

**Toggle Ignore records older than… and set the desired number of years.**

A user must be an **Org Admin** to toggle the Record Age Filter.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/configuration-and-setup/security-screening-settings#configuring-security-screening-outcomes)

Configuring Security Screening Outcomes


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/configuration-and-setup/security-screening-settings#retention-of-saved-identification-info)

Retention of Saved Identification Info

If a Guest user confirms a match between a visitor and a record from the security screening, the record as well as the visitor’s identification information will be available on Command for an admin-defined period of time. This time is determined by the **Retention of Saved Identification Info** setting. In the event of a confirmed match, the retained visitor information can include:

*   visitor’s name
    
*   visitor’s date of birth
    
*   image of the visitor’s ID
    
*   visitor’s address
    
*   visitor’s badge photo
    

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1436127735-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FZyuELZr7uIcXX3WnjX0N%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-3280dbea98a220f00ba16b4ff537f22141dc3857%252F595be1488cb82dd1ac3265bee473db3991b75bdc.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=115d683e&sv=2)

When Guest Types are configured to save an image of visitor’s IDs, these images will be saved for the period of time set in Retention of Saved Identification Info setting.

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Workplace >** **Guest.**

2

**On the left navigation, click Guest Settings.**

3

**Under Organization > Security & Data.**

4

**Under Retention of Saved Identification Info, input a number between 1 and 90.**

A user must be an **Org Admin** to configure the Retention of Saved Identification Info setting.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/guest/configuration-and-setup/security-screening-settings#staff-notifications)

Staff Notifications

Staff notifications are sent to relevant contacts for important security screening events, which include:

1

**A match is confirmed between a visitor and a security screening record. The confirmed record is included in these notifications as a PDF and also contain the visitor’s identification information.**

2

**A visitor is added to the Previously Dismissed Matches list. The records that were dismissed for the visitor are included in the notification as a PDF.**

Command users can be selected for staff notifications. External phone numbers and emails may also be enrolled to receive staff notifications.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1436127735-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FZyuELZr7uIcXX3WnjX0N%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-5fcef4a587b7986bf423d464839fe1cf9f021968%252F9c1fe7a91c2c4227a39e8fbda100790289efa5ea.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=feb25962&sv=2)

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Workplace >** **Guest.**

2

**On the left navigation, click Guest Settings.**

3

**Under Sites > Staff Notifications.**

4

**Add relevant contacts.**

A user must be a **Workplace Site Admin** to configure the staff notifications.

* * *

**Prefer to see it in action?** Check out the [video tutorial](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Y9SH2w1glvY)
.

# Microsoft Entra ID SAML Integration - Government Solutions | Government Solutions | Verkada Help

Verkada Command can integrate with Microsoft Entra ID using Security Assertion Markup Language (SAML).

SAML handles the authentication side of things allowing Microsoft Entra ID to be used to manage access to Command, the same as any other Software as a Service (SaaS) application already integrates into your Microsoft Entra ID tenant. This means that you can incorporate Command into your existing identity framework and authorize users based on your current policies.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/single-sign-on-sso/microsoft-entra-id-saml-integration-government-solutions#set-up-saml-in-microsoft-entra-id)

Set up SAML in Microsoft Entra ID


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada Command is registered as a gallery application and can be found within the Microsoft Entra ID marketplace; in other words, you can leverage it with Microsoft Entra ID Free, Microsoft Entra ID P1, and Microsoft Entra ID P2 licenses.

To get started, you need your `client-ID`. Learn how to [generate it and configure your email domains](https://help.verkada.com/command/single-sign-on-sso/saml/enable-saml-for-your-command-account)
, then return to this article to complete the remainder of this process.

1

**Add Verkada Command as an enterprise application in your Microsoft Entra ID directory: Go to your Microsoft Entra ID overview page and select Enterprise applications.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1400995684-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F79mFgTcvQ8N4ByjEDZUn%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-a79722a44181b1fdc58b4a446717b725395bf3f0%252Fea7d4d52ebddb8b4b886e1e9eb2febc75e0d86b3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=97057553&sv=2)

2

**At the top of the page, select New Application and search for Verkada Command.**

3

**Select Verkada Command and click Create.** _**Be patient as it can take a few minutes to add the application to your**_ **Microsoft Entra ID** _**tenant**_**.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1400995684-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F79mFgTcvQ8N4ByjEDZUn%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-31d38b1f41a163cd63acdd388f7841043225dcba%252Fa059e22dc1d67995f891ded49cfd7d882ce4e00a.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f68fc42a&sv=2)

Once the page refreshes, you should see a similar menu (as shown below). ​

4

**On Set up single sign-on, click Get started.**

​

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1400995684-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F79mFgTcvQ8N4ByjEDZUn%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-6a28059d10b2ee41a6e442c29b98e00025eff15a%252F7cf12443f73d5124fb52129d4b2835c317bf1d57.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=73d5a593&sv=2)

5

**Choose SAML as the single sign-on method.**

​

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1400995684-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F79mFgTcvQ8N4ByjEDZUn%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-d6d6ca8dd62db59b642475c10341b7b46962fb2c%252F0e6513aae4262222ba5c16809425c6c77d2b8333.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5857b2d2&sv=2)

6

**If necessary, click Edit to further configure your SAML connection.**

7

**Configure the following fields. You need to add your client ID to the end of each URL before adding them to Microsoft Entra ID. See example below the note.**

a. For **Identifier**: [https://saml.prod-govus-pine.verkadagov.com/saml/sso](https://saml.prod-govus-pine.verkadagov.com/saml/sso/)
 b. For **Reply URL**: [https://saml.prod-govus-pine.verkadagov.com/saml/sso](https://saml.prod-govus-pine.verkadagov.com/saml/sso)
 c. For **Sign on URL**: [https://saml.prod-govus-pine.verkadagov.com/saml/login](https://saml.prod-govus-pine.verkadagov.com/saml/login)
 ​[​](https://saml.prod-ap-syd.verkada.com/saml/sso)
**Note**: To confirm which region you’re located, please refer to where [your organization was created for Verkada](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
. ​

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1400995684-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F79mFgTcvQ8N4ByjEDZUn%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-e84505986b291d1cf02b8ac24fe7db4af6b4733e%252Ff62fd260c99f8d34d4950ec1001629614d31095d.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ba8e6286&sv=2)

**Click Save.**

9

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1400995684-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F79mFgTcvQ8N4ByjEDZUn%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-8cdb4bb7a93e576e03f624af4351e402854ae662%252F8a7793cc70060ce40c5de3ee9b01b011005ee621.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e5768dcd&sv=2)

If you use a different source attributes for email, configure the attributes according to the source attribute you want to use.s

The next dialogs that appear contain tools that you can use after the integration has been finalized.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/single-sign-on-sso/microsoft-entra-id-saml-integration-government-solutions#upload-your-federation-metadata-xml-in-command)

 in Command.

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/single-sign-on-sso/microsoft-entra-id-saml-integration-government-solutions#test-the-saml-connection-in-microsoft-entra-id)

1

​

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1400995684-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F79mFgTcvQ8N4ByjEDZUn%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-67a512262a5b97e88b3dc244907bae7a5fd6e955%252Ff3f197e1c60a2b69aaa4e5ac9d7dadce9ac29dde.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a9826f25&sv=2)

2

**Log in with Sign in as current user. If everything is set up correctly, you should be redirected to the Command platform.**

​

3

**Log in with single-sign on to verify access to Command.**

Microsoft Entra ID does not support nested groups for app access at this time. All users must be direct members of groups for assignment.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/single-sign-on-sso/microsoft-entra-id-saml-integration-government-solutions#log-in-via-the-mobile-application)

Android and iOS on Command supports login through SAML.

In the **email address** field, enter your email and click **Next**. You should be redirected to your IdP (Microsoft Entra ID) to complete the login process.

# Okta SAML Integration - Government Solutions | Government Solutions | Verkada Help

Verkada Command can integrate with Okta using Security Assertion Markup Language (SAML).

SAML handles the authentication process, allowing Okta to be used to manage access to Command, the same as any other Software as a Service (SaaS) application already integrated into your Okta tenant. This means Command can be incorporated into your existing identity framework and be access-controlled based on your current policies in place.

* * *

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/single-sign-on-sso/okta-saml-integration-government-solutions#before-you-begin)

Before you begin

For a successful integration, choose the best path for your region:

*   [Enable SAML for Your Command Account](https://help.verkada.com/command/single-sign-on-sso/saml/enable-saml-for-your-command-account)
    
*   **For US orgs**, you will use an existing Verkada application following steps directly below.
    

Create a Verkada Okta app[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/single-sign-on-sso/okta-saml-integration-government-solutions#create-a-verkada-okta-app)

Log in to Okta.Go to the Applications page and click Browse App Catalog.In the search bar, type Verkada.Click Add.​Click Done.

Attribute mappings[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/single-sign-on-sso/okta-saml-integration-government-solutions#attribute-mappings)

Navigate to Directory > Profile Editor > choose the Verkada app > verify the attributesClick on Mappings and Verify App to Okta user mappings​User to App mappings:​

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/single-sign-on-sso/okta-saml-integration-government-solutions#configuration)

Configuration


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

**In Okta, select the Sign On tab for the Verkada app, and click Edit.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1400995684-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F79mFgTcvQ8N4ByjEDZUn%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-1b411990400f985bbbea74e4ca4d9632f5cd6ff1%252F528acaaf4123dd8ead3b738eecea6a5192c1896f.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e0b70f59&sv=2)

2

**Scroll down to Advanced Sign-On Settings and enter the** [**Client ID**](https://help.verkada.com/command/single-sign-on-sso/saml/enable-saml-for-your-command-account)
 **from your Command account.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1400995684-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F79mFgTcvQ8N4ByjEDZUn%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-74f4293484a71d32b2185c7265e38f1c37e45203%252Fcab4869bcc9e4ccb6bd7cc20ad48af0774f66282.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dd464d44&sv=2)

3

**Select Save.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1400995684-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F79mFgTcvQ8N4ByjEDZUn%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-8b8db3a71413a7f7aeeb7bd67c65c36b8ceb0d76%252F4d52b88b0aaa325eecb346c77acd160de3718e8b.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=446969dd&sv=2)

4

**Scroll further down to SAML Signing Certificates and click Generate new certificate, if a new certificate does not exist.**

5

**To the right of the certificate, select the Actions dropdown and click View IdP metadata**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1400995684-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F79mFgTcvQ8N4ByjEDZUn%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-2420a903551b15e34d1569644982e44f240e4fd2%252F59ebff57b10aaee9573e7c81c7655a6715b7aab4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=28a2261c&sv=2)

6

**Right click on the metadata and select save as and download as XML file type.**

7

**After downloading the XML file, you need to** [**upload it to Command**](https://help.verkada.com/command/single-sign-on-sso/saml/enable-saml-for-your-command-account)
**.**

8

**In the Verify Metadata section, click Run Login Test.**

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/government-solutions/single-sign-on-sso/okta-saml-integration-government-solutions#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Updating usernames (emails) does not automatically take effect in Command**. If you need to change a username, un-assign the user from the SAML app, then re-add the user to the app for the change to take effect.
    
*   **If a new user cannot log in via SSO**, it could be because the email domain is not being added to the SSO configuration in the Verkada backend. If the user’s email is outside of the email domains provided when SSO was set up, this causes the user to be unable to use SSO. If this is the cause of the problem, you need to edit the SSO configuration and add this domain to remedy the issue.
    
*   **If you experience any other problems with setting up SSO**, contact [Verkada Support](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support)
    .
    

Last updated 1 day ago

Was this helpful?

# Loss of Network Connection for Air Quality Sensors | Air Quality | Verkada Help

Each Verkada [Air Quality Sensor](https://www.verkada.com/air-quality/sensors#overview)
 is equipped with an outside LED light. This light indicates its operating status. Verkada offers the [SV11](https://www.verkada.com/sensors/sv11/)
 series and SV20 series (including [SV21](http://sv21/)
, [SV23](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
, [SV25](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
).

A flashing white (SV20 series) or flashing blue (SV11) [status LED](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-status-led)
 on the front of the sensor indicates the sensor is not communicating with Verkada Command. If you see this behavior:

*   Check that the network is set up correctly for the sensor’s requirements.
    
*   If the problem persists, contact [Verkada Support](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support)
    .
    

When sensors are offline, alerts/events do not trigger. They continue to record measurements and sync with Command once they reconnect.

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/troubleshooting/loss-of-network-connection-for-air-quality-sensors#sv20-series)

SV20 series


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The SV20 series may reboot where the device recovers with an internet connection or without one. A reboot technically still results in some data loss (no more than 5 minutes of the latest data).

If the SV20 series sensors lose an internet connection, these scenarios can occur:

Scenario Status

Sensor Result

Sensor still has power and has not rebooted after internet loss.

Sensor should record data as usual, as long as the sensor gets uninterrupted power.

Sensor power cycles after loss of internet within 24 hours.

Command still records data as usual.

Sensor powers off for more than 24 hours.

Command does not record data, because the RTC on the device is no longer reliable.

If an SV20 series sensors have a static IP configured, sensor devices have a [recovery mechanism](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/configure-static-ip-addresses-for-air-quality-sensors-sv20-series-only)
 to account for configuration mistakes or network changes. The device performs a series of checks at regular intervals to ensure connectivity. In case any of these tests fail or the sensor is unable to establish a TLS connection with the **api.control.verkada.com** endpoint, the device falls back to the DHCP operation and begins a [troubleshooting workflow](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/configure-static-ip-addresses-for-air-quality-sensors-sv20-series-only)
.

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/troubleshooting/loss-of-network-connection-for-air-quality-sensors#sv11)

SV11


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

As of December 13, 2021, the SV11 supports offline storage.

If the SV11 sensor loses an internet connection, these scenarios can occur:

Scenario Status

Sensor Result

Device loses internet connectivity.

Device continues recording data indefinitely

Device reboots at any point while offline.

Device does not record data when rebooted. An internet connection must be resumed for data recording to resume, because of the lack of an RTC. When the device reboots, the timestamp is unknown until an internet connection resumes.

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/troubleshooting/loss-of-network-connection-for-air-quality-sensors#for-all-sensors)

For all sensors


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If any Verkada sensor loses an internet connection, these scenarios can occur:

Scenario Status

Sensor Result

Device goes from online to offline.

Device records data.

Device is offline (not connected to internet, but still powered on, then reboots with no internet.

Device does not record data from that point.

Device reboots with no internet, then internet resumes.

Device recording resumes.

The device must be online for (Command) to retrieve data from it. If the device is offline, you cannot view sensor data. You should receive an alert (if you previously set up [sensor events and alerts](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/events-and-alerts/configure-air-quality-event-alerts)
) when their device goes offline.

Last updated 23 hours ago

Was this helpful?

# Bulk Edit Air Quality Sensor Settings | Air Quality | Verkada Help

Using the Verkada Command platform, you can edit a group of Verkada [Air Quality Sensors](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-settings)
 and their respective settings, all at once.

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/bulk-edit-air-quality-sensor-settings#bulk-select-sensors)

Bulk select sensors


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Devices.**

2

**Select the air quality sensors you want to modify.**

3

**In the search bar, enter device type: Air Quality to filter only for sensors.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-8b016475de7f2bbfb7165fe59f401dc59c47a86e%252F8446ea2a6c032cbcc513ffd9c4bab19666f008b1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=459d6f1a&sv=2)

​**Note**: You can only edit in bulk when **Air Quality** is the only device type selected.

4

**Check the box next to each sensor you want to update.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-d4402c1d6a0ea8fe80c2457416fb5e01a92f2c94%252F1ab4c9e3ac5e795e2c28d434e777f630ca9becf4.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3d894867&sv=2)

Alternatively, at the top, click the black box (with a white vertical line) to select **all** devices within the **site** or **org**.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-c76c357f25ae5bde1708e1697bc04405f3984b33%252Ff163a626b5e30d09c9108f848111cc62618e9599.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f7054ce8&sv=2)

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/bulk-edit-air-quality-sensor-settings#bulk-edit-sensor-settings)

Bulk edit sensor settings


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

**Once you have selected your devices, at the top right, click Edit Settings.**

​**Note**: This may appear as just a gear icon if you’re viewing from a mobile browser or a low-resolution monitor.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-7e31c41391eb36bbf00be14e6d4c67082fb1ca22%252Fe368d4e884eef048c7c5fa1d66a2d0ccc1f37f5d.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=18b3da62&sv=2)

2

**On Edit Settings, you can modify Site, Location, Sensors and Triggers (Alert Thresholds), Notification Settings, and Offline Notifications. See** [**Air Quality Sensor Settings**](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-settings)
 **for details on how to configure those settings.**

*   If a given parameter is identical across all selected devices, it appears as the set value.
    
*   If there is a different value set across any of the devices, it appears as **Mixed**.
    
    ![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-af156dcb4e86ddc55dc39e4567bc9915b2558e15%252Ffcc75c891c6a727feada1a9db318a608e91e66cd.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=50d2b705&sv=2)
    

3

**Some model devices contain more or less sensor capabilities than others. You can edit all available sensor reader settings. If you select a mix of sensor devices with different capabilities:**

*   Changes are still applied to all sensors.
    
*   Devices with additional capabilities are also modified.
    
    For example, you can modify **Temperature** and **Carbon Monoxide** sensors for an [SV23](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
     and [SV25](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
    . However, because this reading only exists on the SV25, the **Temperature** sensor reading is applied to all devices, and the **Carbon Monoxide** sensor reading is only applied to the SV25s.
    
    ![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-4864348df2fe23fd6638973066d8859c4ff18cb4%252F4a3e8589c50f5e7678680fb69f3acf8e11b61a3b.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ae157157&sv=2)
    

4

**You can set up triggers for the selected device(s) that will generate alerts:**

a. Click **Set Trigger** or **Edit Trigger** for a sensor reading. b. Set your **Thresholds** and **Event Trigger**. c. (Optional) Click [**Create Alert**](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/events-and-alerts/configure-air-quality-event-alerts)
 to set up and receive notifications via Email, SMS, or Push Notifications (to the [Command app](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
). d. Once you create your alert, click **Save**. **Note**: When editing devices in bulk, you should see a list of alerts that you are listed as an Editor. [Org Admins](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
 will see all alerts.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-845b4a5f3c5c68a9999de9179d667c1f0f5b0526%252F291a74b1bc202e4a992df7c15567156a9b5768bc.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5bea267&sv=2)

​

5

**Once your changes are finalized, click Next.**

6

**When prompted, confirm the changes that you are about to make, and click Apply.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-43a8fe269e0e03c5a6b8d562b16faf947420c6a9%252F8a6cdd277f006f9ab4d9c1467cfa0c5ebc48d92c.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f85b5db6&sv=2)

​**Important**: After a bulk change is applied, it cannot be reverted. Any single device configurations are overwritten with the new values and must be set again from their device settings page.

7

**After the change is confirmed, Command applies the modifications to your devices.**

​ ​**Recommendation**: If you modify multiple devices at once, this step can take some time. Do not exit or leave this page while changes are being applied. Leaving or exiting the page during this step can lead to the change only being partially applied. ​

8

**Once the changes are completed, and you are prompted with a confirmation or error summary, click Done. If you run into any unexpected errors, contact** [**Verkada Support**](https://www.verkada.com/contact/)
**.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-0710472b3dd6b6bb574dc11045a8af64700984da%252F39f1a4f39baa9182f169d364af4b9e5ec3ac36a7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=442171c0&sv=2)

Last updated 22 hours ago

Was this helpful?

# Create a Person of Interest for Air Quality sensors | Air Quality | Verkada Help

Verkada cameras allow you to create a Person of Interest (POI) using one or more photos of a person’s face. When paired with an Air Quality sensor, cameras can help identify and track nearby individuals during specific air quality alerts.

*   The camera paired to the sensor must have People Analytics enabled to support POI creation and people tracking from Air Quality sensors.
    
*   Sensor readings must be configured with triggers to generate events. See [Air Quality Sensor Settings](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-settings)
     for more information.
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/create-a-person-of-interest-for-air-quality-sensors#enable-air-quality-people-insights)

Enable Air Quality People Insights


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To activate People Insights on your Air Quality sensors, you first need to activate the feature for your organization.

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin.**

2

**In the left navigation, select Feature Manager.**

3

**Under Air Quality > Sensor People Insights, select Enabled from the dropdown menu.**

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/create-a-person-of-interest-for-air-quality-sensors#create-a-person-of-interest-profile)

Create a Person of Interest profile


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/create-a-person-of-interest-for-air-quality-sensors#people-analytics-page)

People analytics page

You can create a Person of Interest profile from the People page. Organizations with POI profiles already created will automatically start tracking Air Quality POI. See [Create a Person of Interest](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/create-a-person-of-interest)
 for more information.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/create-a-person-of-interest-for-air-quality-sensors#air-quality-events-page)

Air Quality events page

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Air Quality.**

2

**Select your sensor, then choose an event on the right to view the individuals detected during that event.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-aa8c67da27e6134cf2485d86bc3f40dc0d72d14d%252Fc12559124407f8fe7477603e39fd2738787b1a40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=17a617e7&sv=2)

3

**Thumbnails will populate on the right. Click** **in the top right of the image you want to make a POI.**

a. Select **Add Person of Interest**. b. Name the POI. c. Click **Create.**

4

**You can now view profiles and their associated air quality events from the People Insights tab in the left navigation.**

POI event footage follows the camera’s retention period. For example, if a camera has 30-day retention, POI event clips will no longer be available after that period.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/create-a-person-of-interest-for-air-quality-sensors#remove-a-poi-profile)

Remove a POI profile


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Cameras.**

2

**On the left navigation, click People.**

3

**On the left, under People Lists, select the list the POI profile is in.**

4

**Click the photo of the POI you want to manage.**

5

**Click next to their name and select Remove this person.**

Last updated 1 day ago
