# Manage Your Licenses | Command | Verkada Help

To have access to [Verkada Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
, you must have valid Verkada licenses for all your Verkada products.

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses#how-verkada-licensing-is-applied)

How Verkada licensing is applied


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Verkada licensing is applied for each Command organization, and the licenses co-term to a single expiration date. This means that all of the licenses in an organization are combined, and the expiration date for the organization is the weighted average of all the individual licenses. Learn more about how to [calculate a license expiration date](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/calculate-license-expiration-date)
.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses#view-licenses-and-active-products)

View licenses and active products


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Licenses and active products are available on the Command [License Manager page](https://command.verkada.com/admin/org-settings/license-manager)
.

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin .**

2

**In the left navigation, select Licenses & Renewals.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F705858581-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FNRq5qDDjsYNxwNzF1bcB%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-9c51fdf140fbaab6d9001f86a6d78064ddbe54e6%252Ff8f4fb05373787f14c0406248009cf0d8ce7657a.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=83e4ff21&sv=2)

For each product type that requires a license, you see a count of the active products and claimed licenses. If you have _less_ claimed licenses than active products _for any of your product types_, your license state is **Invalid**, which means you’ll need to [claim your license key](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/find-and-add-license-keys-to-command)
 to continue using Command. Learn more about how to [manage your licenses](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses)
.

If you uninstall or replace a product, for example due to a warranty replacement, you must remember to delete the product from Command. If you do not delete the product, it will continue to count against your active products. Please note that deleting a product also removes all data associated with the product (e.g., footage, camera settings), so do not delete the product before you’re absolutely certain that you will not re-add that specific device to Command.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses#view-the-license-state-and-expiration-date)

View the license state and expiration date

At the top left of the **Manage Licenses** page, you can see the expiration date for your licenses and the current License state of your organization. All Verkada licenses [co-term to a single expiration date](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses)
, so you will only see a single expiration date even if you have bought and claimed multiple license keys.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses#view-transaction-log-of-all-license-actions)

View transaction log of all license actions

The transaction shows a log of all license actions taken in your organization, such as [claiming a new license key](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/find-and-add-license-keys-to-command)
, or unclaiming a key if it was claimed by mistake. If you have any questions regarding the transactions in your log, contact [Verkada Support](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support)
.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F705858581-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FNRq5qDDjsYNxwNzF1bcB%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-871b39a82960ede722626bb37c2ab5c59027528c%252Fc6322db8e18428880621d4b9c72baa09f4ee8126.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dcc418c9&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses#move-devices-between-command-organizations)

Move devices between Command organizations


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Licenses do not automatically move with the device. If you need to move devices from one Command organization to another, you need to move the license keys separately. Contact [\[email protected\]](https://help.verkada.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#abc7c2c8cec5d8c2c5ccebddced9c0cacfca85c8c4c6)
 for support in moving device licenses between Command organizations.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses#license-requirements-by-product-family)

License requirements by product family


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Refer to this table for an overview of the license requirements of each product family:

**Product Family**

**License requirement**

Access Control

One door license per door on:

AC62

AC42

AC41

AC12

AX11 IO Controller: One access IO controller license per controller

Mobile NFC: One mobile NFC credentials license per 20 users

Alarms

One alarm license per location (physical address). Alarm licensing covers a limited number of devices and video verification events.

In addition, **one license per device** for the following:

BZ11 Horn speaker

Cellular backup module

Learn more about each [alarm license each tier offered](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/compliance-licensing-trials/classic-alarms-licensing)
.

Cameras

One camera license per Verkada camera

One camera license per non-Verkada camera (channel) connected to a Command Connector

Optional: One Cloud Backup License per 30-day increments on a single device’s cloud retention. Learn more about [Extended Cloud Backup Licensing](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/historical-playback/extended-cloud-backup-licensing)
.

Multisensor cameras

One MLT2 camera license per two-camera multisensor

One MLT4 camera license per four-camera multisensor

Environmental sensors

One sensor license per environmental sensor

Gateway

One cellular gateway license per cellular gateway

One Wi-Fi gateway license per Wi-Fi gateway

Optional: One data plan license per connected camera or intercom. A multisensor camera needs four data licenses.

Intercom

One Intercom license per intercom device

One Desk Station license per iPad running the Verkada Desk Station app

Viewing station

One viewing station license per viewing station

Workplace

One Workplace license grants you access to use one Guest iPad and one Mailroom site.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses#purchase-command-licenses)

Purchase Command licenses


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Command licenses are available in 1, 3, 5, and 10-year terms.

There are two types of licenses: capacity increase (CAP) and renewal (RNW).

*   **Capacity Increase (CAP) licenses**: Verkada CAP licenses are automatically activated when the associated Verkada hardware order is shipped. New device licenses include a 30-day extension beyond the purchased term to accommodate shipping and installation. The extension period is fixed and does not depend on when the device is installed or activated.
    
*   **Renewal (RNW) licenses:** Verkada RNW licenses extend an organization’s existing term but remain inactive until the earlier of:
    
    *   The date they are claimed within a Command organization or
        
    *   One year after the purchase date. If unclaimed after one year, the license automatically activates, and its term begins to run. Any license claimed beyond this one-year period results in a shortened remaining term. This policy ensures compliance with the intended service period.
        
    

Licenses are usually sold with your Verkada devices, but you can also purchase them separately from your Verkada reseller or sales representative. See the latest [licensing prices](https://www.verkada.com/pricing/)
.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses#renew-your-licenses)

Renew your licenses


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When your licenses are soon to expire, you need to renew your license to avoid losing access to Verkada Command. You can renew your license by contacting your Verkada Sales Representative or your Verkada Reseller.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses#renewal-notifications-and-license-expiration)

Renewal notifications and license expiration

30 days before expiry, you will expect to:

*   Receive an email notifying you that your licenses are about to expire.
    
*   See a banner in Command.
    

You will lose access to Command if you haven’t renewed your license within 30 days after your expiration date.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses#licensing-overcap-policy)

Licensing overcap policy


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

An organization is considered to be in overcap when it has more devices commissioned than the number of licenses claimed.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses#overcap-policy)

Overcap policy

Verkada enforces software compliance by requiring each hardware product to have a valid, claimed software license(see requirements above). The Overcap policy introduces an **Invalid** status for organizations that exceed their claimed licenses, ensuring compliance across all Verkada products. After a 90-day grace period, organizations without proper licensing lose access to critical functions, including device management and notifications.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses#how-it-works)

How it works

Verkada will notify all Command users 90 days **before** an organization loses access, prompting them to claim additional licenses. Organization Admins will receive in-product banners and emails over 90 days to ensure they restore compliance.

All devices will remain functional when access to Command is restricted. However, users will still have access to the **License Manager**, **Devices**, and **Technical Support** pages when an organization is no longer compliant.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses#restore-compliance)

Restore compliance

Organization Admins can perform **one** of the following actions to restore compliance:

*   Claim any unused licensing keys.
    
*   Remove any unused devices from the organization.
    
*   Contact your Sales Representative or email [\[email protected\]](https://help.verkada.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#e08c8983858e93898e87a09685928b818481ce838f8d)
     if you believe there has been an error with the licensing implementation on your account.
    

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses#faq)

FAQ


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

What happens if I have insufficient or expired licenses?[](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses#what-happens-if-i-have-insufficient-or-expired-licenses)

Verkada will send you an email notification and add a banner notification to your Command Organization.

You need valid licenses to use Command. If you don’t [claim your licenses](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/find-and-add-license-keys-to-command)
 when adding new devices or products or renew them when they expire, you will lose access to most of your Command functionality after a 30-day grace period.

*   For expired organizations, you have a 30-day grace period before you lose access.
    
*   For organizations with insufficient licenses, you have a 90-day grace period before you lose access.
    
*   Contact your Verkada Partner or Sales Representative to purchase additional licenses.
    

At the end of this grace period, you will no longer have access to any of your devices or configure any settings. Alarms and Event notifications will also be disabled. You will, however, be able to delete devices and products so you get back into compliance in case you have insufficient licenses.

How will I know if my licenses are soon to expire?[](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses#how-will-i-know-if-my-licenses-are-soon-to-expire)

30 days before your license is set to expire, Verkada will send you an email notification and add a banner notification to your Command Organization.

How do I regain full access to Command?[](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses#how-do-i-regain-full-access-to-command)

If your access to Command was limited due to insufficient licenses, you can:

*   Delete the products that are above your license cap to get back into compliance
    
*   Contact your Verkada Partner or Sales Representative to purchase additional licenses.
    

If your access to Command was limited due to expired licenses, you can contact your Verkada Partner or Sales Representative to renew your licenses.

Will my devices still record data?[](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses#will-my-devices-still-record-data)

As long as your Verkada devices are still connected, they will continue to record data. This data will be available when you regain access to Command (as long as you’re still within the retention period for the given device). Badges and Verkada Pass will still work as before, but you’ll be unable to change your settings via Command.

What happens if I don’t return my expired trial devices?[](https://help.verkada.com/command/licensing-and-warranty/manage-your-licenses#what-happens-if-i-dont-return-my-expired-trial-devices)

Trialing a Verkada device is the best way to experience how our products and platform works. You can initiate a free trial for most of our devices through your Verkada Sales Rep, or your Verkada Partner.

The free trial lasts for 30 days. After the 30 days are up, you’ll see a banner in Command reminding you to return or purchase your trial devices. If you don’t return the devices within 30 days of the expiry date they will stop working as expected.

If you need additional time to test our trial devices and platform, you can ask your Verkada Sales Rep for an extension.

* * *

**Prefer to see it in action?** Check out the [video tutorial](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=uzn7B9k2qpU)
.

# Manage Sites and Subsites | Verkada Cameras | Verkada Help

Verkada sites are a logical way of grouping and managing devices within [Verkada Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/get-started-with-verkada-command)
 and provide several feature options that make managing and viewing the devices in a site easier.

Site permissions are broken down into roles, so you can also specify the type of access each user or group has to devices within the site. To make the viewing experience more secure, users can only see devices in the sites where they have been granted access. This allows you to scope which devices are accessible to each user or group.

See [Roles and Permissions for Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
 for more information.

Subsites are used to grant permissions to specific sections of a site. This eliminates having to create a new site each time you need to scope permissions to one or more devices. You can nest a subsite in other subsites, providing a permissions hierarchy for better access control. An example use case: Only allowing access to outdoor cameras.

* * *

You need at least **Site Admin** permissions to create and manage sites.

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/manage-sites-and-subsites#create-a-site)

Create a site


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Cameras.**

2

**At the top right, click Manage Sites. Alternatively, on the left navigation, click the Sites icon.**

3

**At the top right, click Create Site.**

4

**Name your site and click Add.**

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/manage-sites-and-subsites#rename-a-site)

Rename a site

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin.**

2

**On the left navigation, click the Sites icon.**

3

**Click the ellipses icon and select Rename to change the name of the site. Alternatively, to the right, you can click the site’s name to edit it inline.**

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/manage-sites-and-subsites#delete-a-site)

Delete a site

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin.**

2

**On the left navigation, click the Sitesicon.**

3

**Select the site that you want to delete.**

4

**Confirm that all devices in that site have been deleted or moved to another site.**

5

**At the top right, click the ellipses dropdown and select Delete.**

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/manage-sites-and-subsites#configure-settings-and-permissions)

Configure settings and permissions


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you access and select a site, you have more options to configure for that site.

You need at least **Site Admin** permissions to create and manage sites.

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Cameras.**

2

**In the left panel, select a specific site or click Manage Sites.**

3

**Click the kebab icon and select a specific site.**

4

**For selected site, configure these settings, as needed:**

*   **Reorder Cameras**—Change the order in which you see the cameras. This feature is helpful where you can prioritize the feeds you want to see in a specific order.
    
*   [**View as Grid**](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/live-streaming/cuadriculas)
    —Display all the cameras in the site as a grid.
    
*   **View Site Stats**—View trends of data usage for cameras at the site and individual level.
    
*   **Set Bandwidth Limit**—Restrict the amount of network resources allocated to camera-related activities, such as streaming.
    
*   **Share Site**—[Share camera sites and floor plans](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/sharing-video/share-multiple-cameras)
     (in bulk) to give people temporary access to a site or subsite.
    
*   **Star Site**—[Create a starred view](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/manage-sites-and-subsites#h_2513e8a755)
     to filter your most viewed sites.
    

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/manage-sites-and-subsites#add-cameras-to-an-empty-site)

Add cameras to an empty site

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Cameras.**

2

**Scroll down until you see the empty site.**

3

**Click the camera icon.**

4

**Select Add New Cameras to be taken to the Add Devices page with this site preselected.**

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/manage-sites-and-subsites#move-cameras-to-a-new-site)

Move cameras to a new site

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Cameras.**

2

**At the top left, check the box next to the camera’s feed. You should see a bar at the top of the page.**

3

**Use the Select Site dropdown box to select the destination site to move the cameras to**

4

**Select Move Cameras to this site and add the cameras you want to move.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1795869993-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FylYKicREo6JpuOJH4teK%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-86c4311e345859b1164f8a26a302c013ff62594a%252F7dd67e6c3d22cee28c564eae3c9f9756912b278d.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5284e251&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/configuration-and-setup/manage-sites-and-subsites#manage-your-sites-permissions)

Manage your site’s permissions

The Site Manager page allows admins to view the number of users who have access to the site and their permissions and roles based on the products on the site.

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin.**

2

**On the left navigation, click Sites.**

3

**Select the site where you want to manage permissions.**

4

**On the right pane, select Manage Permissions. You should see a list of all user groups and users in the organization.**

5

**At the top right, use the search field to find a specific group or user and click that group’s or user’s row.**

6

**Edit the various roles that apply to the user.**

You cannot edit roles that have been inherited from a parent site or a group.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1795869993-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FylYKicREo6JpuOJH4teK%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-fc34ec9bea2ce9e6d975044b93da411429ddb76f%252Fb9bc3c18d6e905020015618e9e8374e7eb5c3a78.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=da5170c&sv=2)

Alternatively, you can manage your permissions as follows:

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Cameras.**

2

**In the left panel, select a specific site or click Manage Sites.**

3

**On the Sites page, at the far right, click Manage Permissions.**

4

**Continue with steps above to manage your site’s permissions, as needed.**

# BACnet for Verkada Air Quality Sensors | Air Quality | Verkada Help

Verkada [Air Quality Sensors](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
 offer your organization a way to monitor essential indoor air quality factors, such as [CO2](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
, [CO](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
, [PM 2.5](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
, [PM 4.0](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
, [PM 10.0](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
, [AQI](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
, [TVOC](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
, and [formaldehyde](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
.

The [Building Automation and Control Networks (BACnet)](https://www.ashrae.org/technical-resources/technical-faqs/question-51-what-is-bacnet)
 integration allows Verkada sensors to inform a building’s Heating, Ventilation, and Air Conditioning (HVAC) system about an air quality metric or any sensor reading, allowing the building HVAC to respond to these indoor air quality conditions.

Verkada sensors can integrate with the Building Management System (BMS) protocol, BACnet. By integrating Verkada’s sensors with this protocol, your organization’s HVAC systems can now automatically respond to suboptimal air conditions. Learn how to [configure BACnet for your Verkada Air Quality Sensors](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/configure-bacnet-on-air-quality-sensors)
.

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/bacnet-for-verkada-air-quality-sensors#about-bacnet)

About BACnet


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

BACnet is a communication protocol specifically designed for building automation and control systems. It is an industry-standard protocol used to facilitate the exchange of data between various devices and systems within a building, such as HVAC, lighting, security, and other building automation systems.

BACnet provides a standardized way for different devices and systems from different manufacturers to communicate with each other, regardless of the underlying hardware or software implementation.

The goal of BACnet is to enable efficient and standardized communication between different building automation devices, promoting interoperability, scalability, and flexibility in the design and operation of building control systems.

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/bacnet-for-verkada-air-quality-sensors#benefits-of-bacnet)

Benefits of BACnet


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here are some instances where the intuitiveness of BACnet can be beneficial to your organization:

*   Adjusts the temperature in a room or building to save costs
    
*   Adjusts the output of dampers to increase fresh air circulation in a room
    
*   Turns on supply fans
    
*   Automatically closes windows when poor air quality is detected
    
*   Automatically turns on air filtration systems and increases outdoor airflow when the CO2 levels are high
    
*   Only runs air through filtration systems when pollution thresholds are met, to avoid unnecessary filtration when the air is clean
    
*   Automatically increases the ventilation rate in a lab when there are high levels of VOCs
    
*   Uses the [SV23](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
     and [SV25](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
     as occupancy sensors to save on HVAC energy costs, if programmed to allow the HVAC system to reduce its operation when the room is unoccupied
    
*   Uses the [SV25](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
     light sensor to turn off the lights in a room when it is unoccupied, but light is detected
    
*   Triggers a strobe or alarm if vaping is detected
    

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/bacnet-for-verkada-air-quality-sensors#use-cases-for-bacnet)

Use cases for BACnet


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If your BMS, also sometimes called a Building Automation System (BAS), supports BACnet, you can use Verkada sensors as inputs to control HVAC equipment or any other equipment inside your BMS.

BACnet allows centralized control and monitoring, and by accepting various input readings from Verkada sensors, such as temperature, humidity, [PM 2.5](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
, [TVOC](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
, and [CO2](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
 among others, can be used to control the outputs to remediate the effects. For example, a sensor installed in a meeting room could trigger a high CO2 alert, which would then feed this information in turn to the BAS/BMS, which in turn controls a specific action such as powering on a ventilation fan or damper in the meeting room.

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/bacnet-for-verkada-air-quality-sensors#example-implementation)

Example implementation


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Scenario**: You want your Verkada Air Quality sensor to monitor CO2 in a conference room and increase fresh air flow when CO2 hits 700 ppm.

1

**Install the Verkada Air Quality Sensor and put it on your BACnet network.**

2

**Enable BACnet on the device and give it a unique device ID. See** [**how to enable BACnet on a device**](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/bacnet-for-verkada-air-quality-sensors#h_2d2ca08f93)
**.**

3

**Go to your BACnet over IP compatible BMS, and use the "discover" feature to find your Verkada sensor. In this example, use Vykon WorkPlace N4.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-fd9d50cadad9e68ea06b41585b5bab03824c09b3%252F6b94c8262ff8c822caa8cfef838c007623a67d60.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=27ab36c&sv=2)

This returns the BACnet devices found on the network.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-3813a336bbd7f67860d06d46d6432000bf68203b%252F8301a638e4c71999af53ac0f2f3ec89702570185.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=25408f1b&sv=2)

4

**Rename the device and add it to your BMS.**

5

**Run a BACnet Who-Has discover to find all the available points.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-1c2ea640a84a70088dc5f3b7d534337669157a5e%252Fa9115d3d1199859d819e7d8e4e5fb7d4f4fe39f1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cce6823b&sv=2)

6

**Add the points to your BMS and use them to make HVAC decisions.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-51af7f3175cd3fcd1a81cc3f7159b86fc102015d%252F54011e3800ce03b65114bdaeb9c14883591f96ee.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8b0e31ac&sv=2)

a. In this case, **In2** is linked to the SV25 CO2 reading, which goes to **In A** which is a **GreaterThanEqual** function. b. If the **SV25 CO2** reading is above **700 ppm**, send **True**; otherwise, send **False**. c. Link the **Out** (the output) of that function to the input of a BooleanWritable variable; in this case, **In16**. **In16** determines the **Out** boolean. d. Link the **Out** boolean to your damper control.

*   If **Out** is True, the damper is **open**.
    
*   If **Out** is **False**, the damper is **closed**.
    

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/bacnet-for-verkada-air-quality-sensors#faq)

FAQ


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Do all BMSs/BASs use BACnet?[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/bacnet-for-verkada-air-quality-sensors#do-all-bmss-bass-use-bacnet)

No, not all Building Management Systems (BMSs)/Building Automation Systems (BASs) support BACnet. Most major HVAC providers have products and controllers that support this feature. However, you should talk with your HVAC specialist to understand if your system is supported.

**Required**. Your building must have a BAS that is compatible with BACnet IP to use this integration. We recommend that you contact your HVAC specialist to understand if your system is supported. If you are unsure whether your BAS supports BACnet, contact [Verkada Support](https://www.verkada.com/contact/)
 for additional assistance.

Which sensor readings are supported by BACnet?[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/bacnet-for-verkada-air-quality-sensors#which-sensor-readings-are-supported-by-bacnet)

You can use all Verkada [sensor readings](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
 as inputs for your BMSs, such as [temperature](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
, [humidity](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
, [CO2](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
 values, [Vape Index](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality)
, and so on, to control dampers, ventilation fans, or other HVAC equipment.

Do Verkada sensors control the HVAC directly?[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/bacnet-for-verkada-air-quality-sensors#do-verkada-sensors-control-the-hvac-directly)

No, the Verkada sensors do not control the building’s HVAC system directly. Instead, the sensors relay their readings to your BMS, which in turn uses these as inputs in a function that controls the building’s HVAC, such as adjusting the temperature in a room or increasing the airflow in a closed space.

Do Verkada Air Quality monitors support BACnet MS/TP?[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/bacnet-for-verkada-air-quality-sensors#do-verkada-air-quality-monitors-support-bacnet-ms-tp)

No, BACnet Master Slave (MS)/Token Passing (TP), the hard-wired version of BACnet that requires an [RS-485](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/RS-485)
 connection, similar to our access control readers, is currently not supported by Verkada Air Quality Sensors. Contact your SE should you require additional information or support.

What does BACnet do when enabled?[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/bacnet-for-verkada-air-quality-sensors#what-does-bacnet-do-when-enabled)

Once BACnet is enabled on a device, the BMS controller is now able to "discover" the device on the BACnet network. This is why the BACnet device needs a device ID, which is used to identify the device on the network, as well as a port, also used for communication.The server will initiate a handshake with the device via the "Who-Is/I-Am" flow. It will then figure out what properties the device has with the "Who-Has/I-Have" flow.

The Verkada [SV21](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
, [SV23](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
, and [SV25](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
 all support the BACnet/IP protocol and support IPv4. The UDP port defaults to 47808 (0xBAC0).

Last updated 19 hours ago

Was this helpful?

# Classic Alarms Sites | Classic Alarms | Verkada Help

This article is a guide for classic Alarms. Refer to this [article](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/configuration-and-setup/alarm-sites)
 if you have new Alarms. See [New Alarms vs Classic Alarms](https://help.verkada.com/new-alarms/new-alarms-vs-classic-alarms)
 if you are unsure which version of Alarms you have.

* * *

Alarms sites allow you to manage your Alarms devices. Events from other devices in the organization (cameras, air quality sensors, doors) can become alarm triggers with customizable response actions.

A site automatically becomes an Alarms site when you add an alarm panel or alarm console.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/configuration-and-setup/classic-alarms-sites#create-a-new-site)

Create a new site


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Alarms.**

2

**At the top right, click Add Alarm Site.**

3

**On Location:**

a. Click the **Site** dropdown and select **Add New Site**. b. On **Add New Site**, enter a unique site name, and click **Add**. c. Click the **Location** dropdown and select **Add New Address**, and click **Next**. d. **Confirm** the location.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2326462210-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9tIFgMOGbY4p9wWaKQhl%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-b7dfee18f51f18d96a37a139840217fadf5f4175%252Faaa7d75b0e0e99256d45520052e24b0e611e2828.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f25ba884&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/configuration-and-setup/classic-alarms-sites#designate-an-existing-site-as-an-alarms-site)

Designate an existing site as an Alarms site


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Alarms.**

2

**At the top right, click Add Alarm Site.**

3

**On Location:**

a. Select the desired site. b. Set the location to the address that you would like first responders to be dispatched to the event of an emergency.

4

**Follow the prompts to configure your new alarm site.**

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/configuration-and-setup/classic-alarms-sites#move-devices-between-alarms-sites)

Move devices between Alarms sites


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Alarms.**

2

**Select your alarm site.**

3

**At the top, select Devices.**

4

**Hover over any one of the alarm devices and at the top right of the device, click the ellipsis icon and select Move to move the device to the new alarm site.**

​

**Watch this video to see how this works**

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/configuration-and-setup/classic-alarms-sites#remove-devices-from-your-alarms-site)

Remove devices from your Alarms site


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Alarms.**

2

**Select your alarm site.**

3

**At the top, select Devices.**

4

**Select a device by clicking it and then select the 3 vertical dots in the right-hand corner.**

5

**Hover over any one of the alarm devices and at the top right of the device, click the ellipsis icon and select Delete to remove the devices from the alarm site.**

When you delete an alarm console or alarm panel, the action also removes these devices from your organization.

# How to Arm/Disarm Your Alarm Site | Classic Alarms | Verkada Help

There are multiple methods you can use to arm/disarm your alarm site:

*   Verkada [Command website](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/configuration-and-setup/how-to-armdisarm-your-alarm-site#h_eaec729e84)
    
*   [Alarm console via the keypad](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/configuration-and-setup/how-to-armdisarm-your-alarm-site#h_4e6eb5e049)
    
*   [Alarms app or Command app](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/configuration-and-setup/how-to-armdisarm-your-alarm-site#h_a5a0ab48bc)
    

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/configuration-and-setup/how-to-armdisarm-your-alarm-site#command-website)

Command website

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Alarms. The current state of your alarm site is described by the status under the name of the site.**

2

**Under the name of the alarm site, you have 2 option to disarm:**

*   Toggle on **Disarmed** to disarm your system.
    
*   Clicking the **Armed** slider.
    

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2326462210-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9tIFgMOGbY4p9wWaKQhl%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-02c293ba7459566261c9e7aabc25f16225981d93%252F0e94e59f6894ee7c28f12291d30accafe4911f29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5570a235&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/configuration-and-setup/how-to-armdisarm-your-alarm-site#alarm-console-via-the-keypad)

Alarm console via the keypad

Users without access to Command can arm/disarm the system from [configured keycode(s)](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/configuration-and-setup/configure-classic-alarms-site-settings)
 in your alarm site or the user [keycodes](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/configuration-and-setup/generate-a-user-or-general-keycode-with-classic-alarms)
.

In the alarm console, enter one of your configured site-level or user-generated 6-digit keycode(s) to arm/disarm the system.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2326462210-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9tIFgMOGbY4p9wWaKQhl%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-0372668182addf3419cd52b426b155e3edc10352%252Fc3519f48467a6b01020bf991acb770567750beb8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=babe8378&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/configuration-and-setup/how-to-armdisarm-your-alarm-site#alarms-app-or-command-app)

Alarms app or Command app

Command users of **any** access level who are granted [user permissions](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/roles-and-permissions-for-classic-alarms)
 can also arm/disarm alarm sites from the Verkada **Alarms mobile app** or the **Verkada Command mobile app**.

1

**Log in to the app using your Command credentials.**

2

**Next to the alarm site name, click the Shieldicon to arm/disarm. For the Command app, click the Alarmsicon.**

​**Example**: Alarms App (Disarmed) ​

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2326462210-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9tIFgMOGbY4p9wWaKQhl%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-6fe77af639f63783261be7768822b2d9ec948aba%252Fe7ef68c33a4ca029dc03707c60a01d93d6b6262b.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9048bae9&sv=2)

**Example**: Alarms App (Armed)

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2326462210-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9tIFgMOGbY4p9wWaKQhl%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-730c380f266a83a30bd9cb48ee8067701cc051bf%252Fa9ea9bd487b980abd50b9809487eae0a49982b56.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d73679e9&sv=2)

​**Example**: Command App

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2326462210-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9tIFgMOGbY4p9wWaKQhl%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-ea355ed2fd2e30c47ec51d8e0d6cf861692c8ee0%252F4c4cb96dff117c661309f36a95cfe46592a4d23a.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6503c3c9&sv=2)

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/configuration-and-setup/how-to-armdisarm-your-alarm-site#badge-to-arm-disarm-from-the-access-controller)

Badge to arm/disarm from the access controller


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can configure a reader on a door to arm or disarm an alarm site. The door you choose to select can be in any site.

**Recommendation**. We recommend to use 2 separate doors to arm and disarm the site. If preferred, however, you can use the **Toggle via Doors** option to configure the door to change the state from armed to disarmed, or vice versa when triggered. Once the door is selected, a valid unlock event (for example, a keycard, Bluetooth, and remote unlock) arms/disarms the site.

To select the door to disarm or arm a site, you must go to your alarms site settings:

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Alarms > Select Site > Settings.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2326462210-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9tIFgMOGbY4p9wWaKQhl%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-e6edc2cef2696b174fb30ab31a77df8878f3ac9a%252F7e94c682574a1896a976f7b02f206a03eb27f41a.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3fdbbeef&sv=2)

2

**Once in the alarms site settings, click Arm/Disarm > Select Doors.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2326462210-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9tIFgMOGbY4p9wWaKQhl%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-869ab36b7efe0b3886f25d9963561020557c7021%252F004c6ccb870ce0f708737a9438b13e003ec1f334.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f6918ad0&sv=2)

# Delete Air Quality Sensors from Command | Air Quality | Verkada Help

When you delete an air quality sensor from Verkada Command, you erase all of its data and reset it to factory default settings. This is a good way to reset the sensor and start over, move it to a different organization, or remove it, if no longer needed.

You must be an Org Admin with Site Admin permissions on the site that contains the sensor(s) to delete and remove sensors from your org. Learn more about [Roles and Permissions for Command](https://help.verkada.com/command/users-and-permissions/roles-and-permissions-for-command)
.

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Air Quality.**

2

**Select the sensor you want to delete.**

3

**On the sensor’s page, at the top right, click Settings.**

4

**On Edit Settings, go to Device.**

5

**At the right of Delete Device, click Delete.**

​

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-1afe51ec32183937e628ad4e941229e7c136fff8%252F8daa249b109d41ef7676b0c2c4a9a7ec7c51910e.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f0692644&sv=2)

6

**Complete the validation prompt for the selected device and click Apply.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-bc11ab3d32da7266bbfa3d9b6913e586ead3a2cd%252F20d75e34ed899146654445e5d686934bf0c6c077.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=80b52f3b&sv=2)

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/delete-air-quality-sensors-from-command#delete-a-sensor-from-the-mobile-app)

Delete a sensor from the mobile app


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

**In your Command app, go to Air Quality > Home.**

2

**Select and tap the sensor you want to delete.**

​

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-163526017ac047ecaf5953b26964cca18265330f%252F2f49b00c20e7e3fa8ec67da49efa34da97dcf43d.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4ce6d099&sv=2)

3

**At the top right, tap the option menu > Settings.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-c80732afd056380a39881febd784b0b149963ace%252F14da606c7effbfd137238c2c726e44445aa68b79.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4d46fa67&sv=2)

4

**Tap Delete Sensor.**

5

**Follow the prompts to confirm.**

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/delete-air-quality-sensors-from-command#bulk-delete-sensors-from-command)

Bulk delete sensors from Command

1

**In Command, go to All Products > Devices.**

2

**Filter for device type: Air Quality.**

3

**Check the box next to the sensors you want to delete.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-d4402c1d6a0ea8fe80c2457416fb5e01a92f2c94%252F1ab4c9e3ac5e795e2c28d434e777f630ca9becf4.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3d894867&sv=2)

Alternatively, at the top, click the black box (with white vertical line) to select **all** devices within the **site** or **org**.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-c76c357f25ae5bde1708e1697bc04405f3984b33%252Ff163a626b5e30d09c9108f848111cc62618e9599.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f7054ce8&sv=2)

4

**At the top right, click Delete. Note: This may appear asif you’re viewing from a mobile browser or a low-resolution monitor.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-eadd2cb38f87e9e73d4be8959745d3e908788e97%252Fb4b1f72cb40f3277b3ed0ee27a40e87a2fa22fd1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b0cc5854&sv=2)

# Manage Alerts Across Verkada Products | Verkada Cameras | Verkada Help

Alerts notify you of important events from your organization. This allows you to shift from reactive to proactive monitoring.

The [Alerts](https://command.verkada.com/alerts/device-events)
 page lets users view their subscribed alerts to easily find important events and relevant footage. You can set up alerts for events across the [cameras](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/events-and-alerts/create-camera-event-alerts)
, intercom, [access control](https://help.verkada.com/access-control/alerts-and-events/configure-access-control-event-alerts)
, [alarms](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/events-and-alerts/configure-alarms-event-alerts)
, [gateway](https://help.verkada.com/connectivity/events-and-alerts/configure-gateway-status-alerts)
, and [air quality](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/events-and-alerts/configure-air-quality-event-alerts)
 product lines.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/events-and-alerts/manage-alerts-across-verkada-products#edit-alerts)

Edit alerts


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

**On the Command homepage, left navigation, click Alerts .**

2

**Under My Alerts:**

a. Hover over the alert you want to edit. b. To the right of the alert, click . c. Select **Edit Alert**. d. Select the event setup step you want to edit and make any needed changes. e. Click **Done** and repeat with other event setup steps as needed.

3

**Click Save once all changes have been made.**

Alerts configured with the old alert system containing multiple event times are not supported under the new alert system. If you see the message **Editing this alert is no longer supported,** recreate the alert to update its configuration or contact [Verkada Support.](https://help.verkada.com/command/need-help/contact-verkada-support)

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1795869993-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FylYKicREo6JpuOJH4teK%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-cf69d2c6a7e39ad56a3845573170766833961935%252Ffb132ea804f6784d1499e6554b230f5e2ddf2999.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a38bd934&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/events-and-alerts/manage-alerts-across-verkada-products#mute-alerts)

Mute alerts


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/events-and-alerts/manage-alerts-across-verkada-products#mute-an-alert)

Mute an alert

1

**On the Command homepage, left navigation, click Alerts .**

2

**Under My Alerts:**

a. Hover over the alert you want to mute. b. To the right of the alert, click . c. Select **Mute Alert** and choose the duration. If you choose **Custom**, set the duration and click **Apply**.

#### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/events-and-alerts/manage-alerts-across-verkada-products#mute-all-alerts)

Mute all alerts

1

**In Command, go to All Products > Admin.**

2

**On Org Settings, select Manage Alerts.**

3

**In the top right, click the mute icon to mute all alerts.**

a. Choose the duration for the alert to mute. b. (Optional) If you choose **Custom**, set the duration and click **Apply**. c. Click **Yes** to confirm and mute all alerts.

Muting an alert will only mute it for your account and not other alert recipients.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/events-and-alerts/manage-alerts-across-verkada-products#delete-alerts)

Delete alerts


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

**On the Command homepage, left navigation, Alerts.**

2

**Under My Alerts:**

a. Hover over the alert you want to delete. b. To the right of the alert, click . c. Select **Delete Alert**.

3

**Click Delete when prompted to confirm the deletion.**

You can only delete alerts that you created. Contact the admin who created a shared alert to delete it.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/events-and-alerts/manage-alerts-across-verkada-products#manage-editors)

Manage editors


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can add editors to an alert you create so other admins can also view and manage the alert. Editors can view, modify, or delete the alert from the [**Manage Alerts**](https://command.verkada.com/admin/manage-alerts)
 page.

1

**On the Command homepage, left navigation, Alerts.**

2

**Under My Alerts:**

a. Hover over the alert you want to manage editors. b. To the right of the alert, click . c. Select **Manage Editors**. d. Add or remove users or groups as needed.

3

**Click Save to confirm the changes.**

Editors are **not** added as alert [recipients](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/events-and-alerts/create-alerts-across-verkada-products)
 by default. This means editors can not see the events on their Alerts page and will not receive notifications for alerts unless they are also added as alert recipients.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/verkada-cameras/events-and-alerts/manage-alerts-across-verkada-products#find-events)

Find events


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Alerts page contains more information about notifications, including date and time, notification type, site, and location.

1

**On the Command homepage, left navigation, click Alerts.**

2

**(Optional) Use the filters in the search bar to narrow down the events.**

3

**Select an event to view the associated video clip.**

Historical footage and thumbnails are **only** accessible for the duration of the camera’s retention.

* * *

**Prefer to see it in action?** Check out the [video tutorial](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=b697WsAOqW4)
.

# Alarm Setup and Install Best Practices | Classic Alarms | Verkada Help

Building materials, obstructions, distance, and general radio frequency (RF) interference are highly variable across different environments and from the time of day. As such, we highly recommend that you read and follow guidelines outlined in this article to ensure that your wireless system operates to the best of its ability.

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/hardware-installation/alarm-setup-and-install-best-practices#add-your-wireless-alarm-hub-to-verkada-command)

Add your wireless alarm hub to Verkada Command


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

**Remove the cover from your alarm hub and plug the device into a Power over Ethernet (PoE) switch.**

2

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Add Devices and select a site. This will be your alarms site.**

3

**Find and enter the 12-character serial number, beginning with "DQ6", located at the bottom of the device or on the box that was provided.**

4

**Click Activate.**

5

**Once you activate your hub, follow the setup flow to configure your alarms site. If you added it to an existing alarms site, you can skip this step.**

6

**Navigate to the Alarms > Devices tab and verify that your wireless hub is reporting online and the LED on the hub is solid blue.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2326462210-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9tIFgMOGbY4p9wWaKQhl%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-5ba0bb0ffac4630c86073bf89ef8f9f8400ed828%252F1d4b6ef0d1b70d9b563f4f768ab8a8c44b249060.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=96250579&sv=2)

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/hardware-installation/alarm-setup-and-install-best-practices#add-your-wireless-sensors-to-command)

Add your wireless sensors to Command


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Place your wireless sensors next to the wireless hub.

**Note**: Prior to installing the sensors in their final locations, our team will verify that all of your sensors are properly communicating with your hub and reporting events to Command.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/hardware-installation/alarm-setup-and-install-best-practices#add-your-wireless-sensors-by-sn)

Add your wireless sensors by SN

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Devices.**

2

**At the top right, click Add Devices and select a site. This is the alarms site associated to your wireless sensor.**

3

**Find and enter the 12-character serial number, located at the bottom of the device or on the box that was provided.**

4

**Click Activate to automatically associate the sensor to the alarms site and the hub(s) in your organization.**

**Note**: Wireless sensors and hubs do **not** have to exist in the same Alarms site. Sensors automatically communicate with the closest physical hub that exists in your entire organization.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/hardware-installation/alarm-setup-and-install-best-practices#power-on-your-wireless-sensors)

Power on your wireless sensors

When the sensors are first powered on, they automatically try to join the closest hub to report their status.

1

**Pull the battery tabs from your sensor(s) to power on the device.**

2

**Initiate trigger event(s), as detailed in** [**Set Up Your Wireless Devices**](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/hardware-installation/set-up-your-wireless-alarm-devices)
**, for your specific sensor (door open/close, motion detected, button press, and so on).**

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/hardware-installation/alarm-setup-and-install-best-practices#validate-wireless-sensor-coverage)

Validate wireless sensor coverage

1

**Place the hub as close to the desired location as possible, such as the center of the floor/building for maximum coverage.**

2

**The most recent sensor events are time-stamped in the Alarms site > Devices tab. You can monitor this page to ensure that sensor events and the sensor’s current signal strength are properly reported to Command.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2326462210-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9tIFgMOGbY4p9wWaKQhl%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-f7077f0ae25694ecfbcdb6e5d80f444492079ddb%252Fea9126c36651ab9d0b6a2a31207a4c4be6b64fbb.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3d822de8&sv=2)

3

**Relocate your wireless sensors to their desired install locations and send several trigger events (door open/close, motion detected, panic button press, glass break tester, and shorting the metal contacts on the water sensor). The lowest recommended Received Signal Strength Indicator (RSSI) is -85. We recommend not allowing lower values (for example, 90, -95, and so on); this weak signal strength means that the sensors will likely drop offline and experience difficulties upgrading. The -85 RSSI provides a safer barrier to the variability in environmental changes.**

4

**If the events are reported to Command, install the sensor in its final location and send 1 more event for good measure; otherwise:**

a. If no events are being received, move closer to the hub to determine if the issue is related to signal coverage. b. If you find that events are received when you move closer to the hub, perform a site walk to determine if there are any obstructions that could be dampening the signal. c. Reposition the hub for better coverage and restart the testing. d. If all else fails, you may want to consider purchasing an additional hub and license to fully cover your floor/building.

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/hardware-installation/alarm-setup-and-install-best-practices#configure-command)

Configure Command


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before you begin this configuration, verify your [alarm site settings](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/configuration-and-setup/configure-classic-alarms-site-settings)
 and validate system operations by raising a few test alarms.

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/hardware-installation/alarm-setup-and-install-best-practices#put-your-alarm-site-in-test-mode)

Put your Alarm site in test mode

When the system is put in test mode, the system and monitoring agents still go through the alarms flow, but do **not** dispatch emergency services, unless you explicitly request it.

1

**Toggle on Enable Emergency Dispatch.**

2

**Toggle on Monitoring Test Mode.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2326462210-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9tIFgMOGbY4p9wWaKQhl%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-f0e2abc5c3f79544edaba33cf5ba7be2f5fbd95e%252Ff323e9f7a36c0e81f7b1ceffda1d356b7d62c256.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=82f82a23&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/hardware-installation/alarm-setup-and-install-best-practices#configure-the-user-call-list-and-notifications)

Configure the user call list and notifications

**Required**. At least 1 user with a phone number must be subscribed to receive a call from our monitoring agents.

In the screenshot example, the first person listed receives a call and then the following person would be the second to be called if the first person is unavailable, and so on. Each user will receive SMS and email notifications when an alarm is raised.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2326462210-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9tIFgMOGbY4p9wWaKQhl%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-ab2767aeb2785872c71282f4ea585367e82a23a2%252F0552b338fe236bb79ba4ba5d26831050d2b3501b.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f6687e1d&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/hardware-installation/alarm-setup-and-install-best-practices#add-wireless-or-wired-sensors-as-triggers)

Add wireless or wired sensors as triggers

**Note**: All added sensors are used as triggers.

1

**On the Alarm Triggers page (for Wireless Sensor Events or Wired Sensor Events), click Add Sensor.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2326462210-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9tIFgMOGbY4p9wWaKQhl%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-0ea89a7353b204b03491b1a9768397bf1b68af40%252F8e150637629d38bcad602ece79b2da0c586427ab.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=43e71646&sv=2)

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2326462210-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9tIFgMOGbY4p9wWaKQhl%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-e86b4dced2b2c572cf5f6be7d8342de9a1f00452%252F227689ec4aaa55476f700f403987def4cf85263d.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ba95af69&sv=2)

2

**Click Editto configure additional settings, such as door contact sensors and panic buttons.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2326462210-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9tIFgMOGbY4p9wWaKQhl%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-578fa6da41764afd4c1cae020bd8736bac7a86d4%252Fda63968fdc193c9843a6b5859d98813a02cfb536.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=360dbbd6&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/hardware-installation/alarm-setup-and-install-best-practices#arm-the-site-and-raise-a-test-alarm)

Arm the site and raise a test alarm

1

**Arm the alarms site from Command and monitor the Activity tab.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2326462210-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9tIFgMOGbY4p9wWaKQhl%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-548d11acec120b01eeb6c0164c0a44824ae68504%252Fb1457dd12497f7974671e7c0f645ae9734a15135.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=78f26a29&sv=2)

2

**Trigger your sensors and after the entry delay has elapsed, an alarm should be raised.**

*   Users on the notification list can resolve the alarm by spelling out their last name and phone number associated with their account to the monitoring agent.
    
*   Command users can also manually resolve the alarm banner or by disarming their system.
    
    ![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2326462210-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9tIFgMOGbY4p9wWaKQhl%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-f2edb24285afdf5840bd723ebce2ff4a17cb9862%252F1f1e00588d41095cc16a19e7f6a5fbaf3916e27f.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=afaa5b4e&sv=2)
    

3

**Expand the alarm-raised event to see all of the sensors that were tripped:**

a. Under the alarm period, click **See Details**. In this view, you can see details about the flow of events for the raised alarm event. b. Click **See more** to expand the list of device events and include context camera footage for raise-alarm events, if configured.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2326462210-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9tIFgMOGbY4p9wWaKQhl%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-c1e4f373861c4e01aa4dafaeff5daeac1be12167%252Ffc75fb7c75709499065d83829a9107f68b4f79ae.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ed35de44&sv=2)

### 

[](https://help.verkada.com/classic-alarms/hardware-installation/alarm-setup-and-install-best-practices#ensure-the-event-population)

Ensure the event population

Under the alarm site > **Devices** tab, ensure that all of the wireless sensors have populated at least 1 event.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2326462210-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9tIFgMOGbY4p9wWaKQhl%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-c691ee65609cacbb5c32e476751bbd2bf7035f6f%252Fb7a6c0aef5d71e3f522283469fc4d9f768e2285f.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f4600f36&sv=2)

# Configure BACnet on Air Quality Sensors | Air Quality | Verkada Help

Verkada [Air Quality Sensors](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
 offer your organizations a way to monitor essential indoor air quality factors, such as [CO2](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
, [CO](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
, [PM 2.5](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
, [PM 4.0](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
, [PM 10.0](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
, [AQI](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
, [TVOC](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
, and [formaldehyde](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/sensor-data/air-quality-sensor-readings)
.

The [Building Automation and Control Networks (BACnet)](https://www.ashrae.org/technical-resources/technical-faqs/question-51-what-is-bacnet)
 integration allows Verkada sensors to inform a building’s Heating, Ventilation, and Air Conditioning (HVAC) system about an air quality metric or any sensor reading, allowing the building HVAC to respond to these indoor air quality conditions.

Verkada sensors can integrate with the Building Management System (BMS) protocol, BACnet. By integrating Verkada’s sensors with this protocol, your organization’s HVAC systems can now automatically respond to suboptimal air conditions. Learn more about [BACnet for Verkada Air Quality Sensors](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/bacnet-for-verkada-air-quality-sensors)
.

To use this integration, your building must have a Building Automation System (BAS) that is compatible with BACnet IP. We recommend that you contact your HVAC specialist to understand if your system is supported. If you are unsure or need help, contact [Verkada Support](https://www.verkada.com/contact/)
.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/configure-bacnet-on-air-quality-sensors#enable-bacnet-for-your-org-using-the-feature-manager)

Enable BACnet for your org using the Feature Manager


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To activate the BACnet functionality on your sensors, you first need to enable the BACnet feature for your organization.

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Admin.**

2

**Select the Privacy & Security tab.**

3

**Click Feature Manager.**

4

**Under Air Quality, find Sensor BACnet and change it from Disable to Enable.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-67ab3faa7c56358e462438be17f0b39af2845030%252F772863bf6645683a2d094823cce8a35d86ee0a53.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a157f7bf&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/configure-bacnet-on-air-quality-sensors#enable-bacnet-on-a-verkada-sensor)

Enable BACnet on a Verkada sensor


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once the BACnet feature is enabled for your organization, you’re ready to enable it on your devices. Learn more about [BACnet for Verkada Air Quality Sensors](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/bacnet-for-verkada-air-quality-sensors)
.

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Air Quality.**

2

**Click the sensor you want to enroll for BACnet.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-f4794300d9bd36590320402204d9f69a38aab3d9%252Fd14e46752ee887282eaccfe73c018033a70b69a2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8937e998&sv=2)

3

**At the top right, click the Settings icon (gear).**

4

**On the left, click BACnet. (If you don’t see the BACnet option, ensure the device is an** [**SV21**](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
**,** [**SV23**](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
**, or** [**SV25**](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
**, and** [**ensure BACnet is enabled for your organization**](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/bacnet-for-verkada-air-quality-sensors)
**.)**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-a4b7846285cd5df0beb7381b1e37c14fa464a441%252F235117b107fa4ef83518ad92780fac4f861faf1f.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e66db610&sv=2)

a. Click the dropdown and select **Enable**. b. Assign a unique **BACnet** **Device ID** so you can identify your sensor on your BAS/BMS. The Device ID identifies the device on the BACnet network; therefore, each Verkada sensor should have a unique Device ID in the range of 0–4194302. c. Assign a **BACnet port**. The default BACnet port is **47808**, which is a commonly used UDP port for BACnet/IP, but it can also be any number in the range of 47808–47823. We recommend that the UDP port stay unchanged because the default value is mainly used.

5

**Click Apply to save your changes.**

BACnet should now be enabled on the device. Anything on the BACnet server can now poll the device for properties.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/configure-bacnet-on-air-quality-sensors#disable-bacnet-on-a-verkada-sensor)

Disable BACnet on a Verkada sensor


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

**In Verkada Command, go to All Products > Air Quality.**

2

**Click the sensor you want to disable BACnet for.**

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-f4794300d9bd36590320402204d9f69a38aab3d9%252Fd14e46752ee887282eaccfe73c018033a70b69a2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8937e998&sv=2)

3

**At the top right, click the Settings icon (gear).**

4

**On the left, click BACnet. (If you don’t see the BACnet option, ensure the device is an** [**SV21**](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
**,** [**SV23**](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
**, or** [**SV25**](https://docs.verkada.com/docs/air-quality-sensors-overview.pdf)
**, and** [**ensure BACnet is enabled for your organization**](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/bacnet-for-verkada-air-quality-sensors)
**.)**

a. Click the dropdown and select **Disable**.

![](https://help.verkada.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057705728-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJtgmyWYlTEX9DpjvBwTL%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-f12a87c05414b69aa6cb846ec344dd9014496338%252Fdaa725ff60ce4ccc85fb7b763c9431410ddc281b.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=757ca6a2&sv=2)

b. Click **Apply** to save your changes.

* * *

[](https://help.verkada.com/air-quality/configuration-and-setup/configure-bacnet-on-air-quality-sensors#bacnet-pics)

BACnet [PICS](https://www.bacnetinternational.net/catalog/manu/siemens/CM110665en_06_001.pdf)



------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
